--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\BadgerLib\Settlements.cs ---
public static DataTable GetIncomingSettlementWires(string server, bool processedOnly)
        {
            string sql = @"SELECT * FROM vIncomingSettlementWires WHERE PROCESSED = @Processed";
            
            using (var conn = Database.Connection.GetConnection(server))
            {
                using (var cmd = conn.CreateCommand())
                {
                    cmd.CommandText = sql;
                    cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@Processed", processedOnly);
                    
                    var adapter = new System.Data.SqlClient.SqlDataAdapter((System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand)cmd);
                    var dt = new DataTable();
                    adapter.Fill(dt);
                    return dt;
                }
            }
        }


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\ModernTreasuryLib\Backfill.cs ---
namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class Backfill
    {
        
        public static async Task RunAsync(DataTable assets)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assets == null || assets.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No assets supplied for backfill.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id"))
                    continue;

                string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_pipeline_label_max") ? row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString() : null;

                
                decimal oface = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "oface", "oface_text");
                decimal purchaseProceeds = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "purchase_proceeds", "purchase_proceeds_text");
                decimal gainOnSale = CalculateGainOnSale(purchaseProceeds, oface);

                
                string fileNum = GetString(row, "file_num") ?? GetString(row, "file_number") ?? GetString(row, "FILE NUMBER");
                string effectiveDate = GetString(row, "effective_date") ?? GetString(row, "EFF_DATE");
                string fundingDate = GetString(row, "funding_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE_INPUT");

                
                string tradeId = GetString(row, "trade_id");
                string accountId = GetString(row, "account_id");
                string tradeDate = GetString(row, "trade_date");
                string settleDate = GetString(row, "settle_date");
                decimal price = GetDecimal(row, "price");
                string investorMemoAccountName = GetString(row, "investor_memo_account_name");
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;

                
                string investorMemoCategoryId = null;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_mt_account_id") && row["investor_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    investorMemoCategoryId = row["investor_mt_account_id"].ToString();

                
                string investorIPMemoCategoryId = null;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_IP_mt_account_id") && row["investor_IP_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    investorIPMemoCategoryId = row["investor_IP_mt_account_id"].ToString();

                
                string assetCategoryId = await ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for Asset {assetId}");
                    continue;
                }
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_category", assetCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + assetCategoryId, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);

                
                string subCategoryId_funding = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Funding", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);
                string subCategoryId_trades = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Trades", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_trades_subcategory", subCategoryId_trades, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_trades, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);

                
                var tradesCategoryIds = new List<string> { subCategoryId_trades };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoCategoryId)) tradesCategoryIds.Add(investorMemoCategoryId);

                
                var fundingCategoryIds = new List<string> { subCategoryId_funding };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorIPMemoCategoryId)) fundingCategoryIds.Add(investorIPMemoCategoryId);


                
                var ipAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) ipAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) ipAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) ipAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;             
                ipAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();

                var tradeAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeId)) tradeAccountMetadata["trade_id"] = tradeId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(accountId)) tradeAccountMetadata["account_id"] = accountId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeDate)) tradeAccountMetadata["trade_date"] = tradeDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settleDate)) tradeAccountMetadata["settle_date"] = settleDate;
                if (price > 0m) tradeAccountMetadata["price"] = price.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoAccountName)) tradeAccountMetadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = investorMemoAccountName;
                tradeAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
                tradeAccountMetadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
                tradeAccountMetadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "backfill";

                
                string investmentPaymentId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, fundingCategoryIds, oface, ipAccountMetadata);
                string gainOnSaleId = null;
                string purchaseProceedsId = null;
                if (purchaseProceeds > 0)
                {
                    gainOnSaleId = await CreateGainOnSaleLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_trades }, gainOnSale, tradeAccountMetadata);
                    purchaseProceedsId = await CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, tradesCategoryIds, purchaseProceeds, tradeAccountMetadata);
                }

                
                string ltIPId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, investmentPaymentId, investor_contra_memo_account_id, oface, fileNum, effectiveDate, fundingDate);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltIPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Investment Payment ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");

                if (purchaseProceeds > 0 && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsId) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(gainOnSaleId))
                {
                    string ltPPId = await CreatePurchaseProceedsInverseTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, purchaseProceedsId, investmentPaymentId, gainOnSaleId, purchaseProceeds, oface, gainOnSale, tradeId, accountId, tradeDate, settleDate, price, investorMemoAccountName);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltPPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Purchase Proceeds inverse ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");
                }
            }
        }

        
        public static async Task RunAsyncOriginations(DataTable assets)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assets == null || assets.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No assets supplied for originations backfill.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id"))
                    continue;

                string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_pipeline_label_max") ? row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString() : null;

                decimal oface = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "oface", "oface_text");
                string fileNum = GetString(row, "file_num") ?? GetString(row, "file_number") ?? GetString(row, "FILE NUMBER");
                string effectiveDate = GetString(row, "effective_date") ?? GetString(row, "EFF_DATE");
                string fundingDate = GetString(row, "funding_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE_INPUT");
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;

                string assetCategoryId = await ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for Asset {assetId}");
                    continue;
                }
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_category", assetCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + assetCategoryId, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);

                string subCategoryId_funding = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Funding", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);

                var ipAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) ipAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) ipAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) ipAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;                
                ipAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();

                string investmentPaymentId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_funding }, oface, ipAccountMetadata);

                string ltIPId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, investmentPaymentId, investor_contra_memo_account_id, oface, fileNum, effectiveDate, fundingDate);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltIPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Investment Payment ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");
            }
        }

        
        public static async Task RunAsyncSettlements(DataTable assets)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assets == null || assets.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No assets supplied for settlement backfill.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id"))
                    continue;

                string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_pipeline_label_max") ? row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString() : null;

                decimal netSettlementPayment = GetDecimal(row, "net_settlement_payment");
                string fileNum = GetString(row, "file_num") ?? GetString(row, "file_number") ?? GetString(row, "FILE NUMBER");
                string effectiveDate = GetString(row, "effective_date") ?? GetString(row, "EFF_DATE");
                string fundingDate = GetString(row, "funding_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE_INPUT");
                decimal oface = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "oface", "oface_text");
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;
                string finalDispositionDate = GetString(row, "final_disposition_date") ?? GetString(row, "FINAL_DISPOSITION_DATE");
                string settlementType = GetString(row, "settlement_type") ?? GetString(row, "SETTLEMENT_TYPE");
                string settlementReason = GetString(row, "settlement_reason") ?? GetString(row, "SETTLEMENT_REASON");
                string settlementAccount = GetString(row, "settlement_account") ?? GetString(row, "SETTLEMENT_ACCOUNT");


                string assetCategoryId = await ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for Asset {assetId}");
                    continue;
                }
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_category", assetCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + assetCategoryId, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);

                string subCategoryId_funding = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Funding", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);

                var ipAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) ipAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                ipAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) ipAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) ipAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(finalDispositionDate)) ipAccountMetadata["final_disposition_date"] = finalDispositionDate;
                if (netSettlementPayment > 0m) settlementAccountMetadata["net_settlement_payment"] = netSettlementPayment.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementType)) settlementAccountMetadata["settlement_type"] = settlementType;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementReason)) settlementAccountMetadata["settlement_reason"] = settlementReason;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementAccount)) settlementAccountMetadata["settlement_account"] = settlementAccount;

                string settlementAccountId = await CreateSettlementLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_settlement }, netSettlementPayment, settlementAccountMetadata);

                
                string ltSettleId = await CreateInvestorLedgerAccountSettlementTransactionsAsync(
                    assetId,
                    pipelineLabel,
                    investmentPaymentId,
                    settlementAccountId,
                    investor_contra_memo_account_id,
                    oface,
                    fileNum,
                    effectiveDate,
                    fundingDate,
                    finalDispositionDate,
                    netSettlementPayment,
                    settlementType,
                    settlementReason
                );
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltSettleId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Settlement ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");
            }
        }

        
        private static async Task<string> CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(string server, string assetId, string pipelineLabel, List<string> categoryIds, decimal amountForMap, JObject metadata)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label;
            string ledgerAccountName = assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label;

            var ledgerAccount = new JObject
            {
                ["name"] = ledgerAccountName,
                ["currency"] = "USD",
                ["normal_balance"] = "debit",
                ["ledger_account_category_ids"] = JArray.FromObject(categoryIds),
                ["ledger_id"] = targetLedger,
                ["description"] = accountLabel
            };
            if (metadata != null && metadata.HasValues) ledgerAccount["metadata"] = metadata;
            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccount);
            string id = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, assetId, "backfill_create_ledger_account_investment_payment", id, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label, assetId, amountForMap, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + id, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);
            return id;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(string assetId, string pipelineLabel, string investmentPaymentAccountId, string contraLedgerAccountId, decimal amount, string fileNum, string effectiveDate, string fundingDate)
        {
            if (amount <= 0m) return null;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(contraLedgerAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Missing ledger account id(s) for Asset {assetId} Investment Payment backfill.");
                return null;
            }

            int amountInt = ToInt(amount);
            var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) metadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) metadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) metadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;

            var ltIP = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Backfill Investment Payment for Asset {assetId}",
                ["status"] = "posted",
                ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                {
                    new JObject { ["amount"] = amountInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = investmentPaymentAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata },
                    new JObject { ["amount"] = amountInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = contraLedgerAccountId }
                }
            };

            string ltIPBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ltIP);
            string ltIPId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            string ltIPUrl = "https:

            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_create_investment_payment_ledger_transaction", ltIPId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, "_Backfill_IP", assetId, amount, ltIPUrl, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);
            return ltIPId;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreatePurchaseProceedsInverseTransactionAsync(
            string assetId,
            string pipelineLabel,
            string purchaseProceedsAccountId,
            string investmentPaymentAccountId,
            string gainOnSaleAccountId,
            decimal purchaseProceeds,
            decimal oface,
            decimal gainOnSale,
            string tradeId,
            string accountId,
            string tradeDate,
            string settleDate,
            decimal price,
            string investorMemoAccountName)
        {
            if (purchaseProceeds <= 0m) return null;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(gainOnSaleAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Missing ledger account id(s) for Asset {assetId} Purchase Proceeds inverse transaction.");
                return null;
            }

            int ppInt = ToInt(purchaseProceeds);
            int ipInt = ToInt(oface);
            int gosInt = ToInt(gainOnSale);

            var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeId)) metadata["trade_id"] = tradeId;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(accountId)) metadata["account_id"] = accountId;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeDate)) metadata["trade_date"] = tradeDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settleDate)) metadata["settle_date"] = settleDate;
            if (price > 0m) metadata["price"] = price.ToString();
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoAccountName)) metadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = investorMemoAccountName;
            metadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
            metadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "backfill";

            var entries = new JArray
            {
                new JObject { ["amount"] = ppInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = purchaseProceedsAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() },
                new JObject { ["amount"] = ipInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = investmentPaymentAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() },
                new JObject { ["amount"] = gosInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = gainOnSaleAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() }
            };

            if (purchaseProceeds < oface)
            {
                int diffInt = ToInt(oface - purchaseProceeds);
                string contraId = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = diffInt, ["direction"] = "debit", ["ledger_account_id"] = contraId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() });
            }

            var lt = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Backfill Purchase Proceeds for Asset {assetId}",
                ["status"] = "posted",
                ["ledger_entries"] = entries
            };

            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(lt);
            string ltId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            string url = "https:

            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_create_purchase_proceeds_inverse_ledger_transaction", ltId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, "_Backfill_PP_Inverse", assetId, purchaseProceeds, url, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);
            return ltId;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateInvestorLedgerAccountSettlementTransactionsAsync(
            string assetId,
            string pipelineLabel,
            string investmentPaymentAccountId,
            string settlementAccountId,
            string contraLedgerAccountId,
            decimal oface,
            string fileNum,
            string effectiveDate,
            string fundingDate,
            string finalDispositionDate,
            decimal netSettlementPayment,
            string settlementType,
            string settlementReason)
        {
            if (oface <= 0m && netSettlementPayment <= 0m) return null;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(contraLedgerAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(settlementAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Missing ledger account id(s) for Asset {assetId} Settlement backfill.");
                return null;
            }

            int ofaceInt = ToInt(oface);
            int nspInt = ToInt(netSettlementPayment);

            var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) metadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) metadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) metadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(finalDispositionDate)) metadata["final_disposition_date"] = finalDispositionDate;
            if (netSettlementPayment > 0m) metadata["net_settlement_payment"] = netSettlementPayment.ToString();
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementType)) metadata["settlement_type"] = settlementType;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementReason)) metadata["settlement_reason"] = settlementReason;

            var entries = new JArray();
            if (ofaceInt > 0)
            {
                
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ofaceInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = contraLedgerAccountId });
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ofaceInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = investmentPaymentAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() });
            }
            if (nspInt > 0)
            {
                
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = nspInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = settlementAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() });
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = nspInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = contraLedgerAccountId });
            }

            if (entries.Count == 0) return null;

            var lt = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Backfill Settlement transactions for Asset {assetId}",
                ["status"] = "posted",
                ["ledger_entries"] = entries
            };

            try
            {
                string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(lt);
                string ltId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                string ltUrl = "https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_create_investment_payment_settlement_ledger_transaction", ltId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, "_Backfill_Settlement", assetId, oface + netSettlementPayment, ltUrl, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m);
                return ltId;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Settlement ledger transactions for Asset {assetId}. {ex.Message}");
                return null;
            }
        }

        public static async Task AddInvestmentPaymentToCategoryAsync(DataTable assetCategoryTable)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assetCategoryTable == null || assetCategoryTable.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No rows supplied.");
                return;
            }

            
            string FindColumn(params string[] candidates)
            {
                foreach (var cand in candidates)
                {
                    if (assetCategoryTable.Columns.Contains(cand)) return cand;
                    foreach (DataColumn col in assetCategoryTable.Columns)
                        if (string.Equals(col.ColumnName, cand, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                            return col.ColumnName;
                }
                return null;
            }

            string assetCol = FindColumn("asset_id");
            string categoryCol = FindColumn("ledger_account_category_id", "category_id", "target_category_id");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCol) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(categoryCol))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Required columns not found. Expected 'asset_id' and one of 'ledger_account_category_id', 'category_id', 'target_category_id'.");
                return;
            }

            var seen = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            foreach (DataRow row in assetCategoryTable.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null) continue;
                string assetId = row[assetCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                string targetCategoryId = row[categoryCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetCategoryId))
                    continue;

                string dedupKey = assetId + "|" + targetCategoryId;
                if (!seen.Add(dedupKey))
                    continue;

                try
                {
                    string investmentPaymentLedgerAccountId = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentLedgerAccountId))
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"No Investment Payment ledger account found for asset_id {assetId}.");
                        continue;
                    }

                    
                    string url = $"https:
                    string body = "{}"; 

                    var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();
                    await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(url, body, "Put");

                    Console.WriteLine($"PUT mapped Investment Payment ledger account {investmentPaymentLedgerAccountId} for asset {assetId} to category {targetCategoryId}.");
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to update Investment Payment category for asset {assetId}. {ex.Message}");
                }
            }
        }

        
        private static decimal CalculateGainOnSale(decimal purchaseProceeds, decimal oface)
        {
            decimal diff = Math.Round(purchaseProceeds - oface, 2);
            return diff < 0m ? 0m : diff;
        }

        private static int ToInt(decimal amount) => Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(amount, 2) * 100);

        private static decimal GetDecimal(DataRow row, string col)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(col) || row[col] == DBNull.Value) return 0m;
            try
            {
                return Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row[col]), 2);
            }
            catch
            {
                var s = row[col]?.ToString();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s)) return 0m;
                s = s.Replace("$", string.Empty).Replace(",", string.Empty).Trim();
                if (decimal.TryParse(s, NumberStyles.Number | NumberStyles.AllowCurrencySymbol, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out var m))
                    return Math.Round(m, 2);
                if (decimal.TryParse(s, NumberStyles.Number | NumberStyles.AllowCurrencySymbol, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture, out m))
                    return Math.Round(m, 2);
                return 0m;
            }
        }

        private static bool HasNonEmptyValue(DataRow row, string col)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(col)) return false;
            var v = row[col];
            if (v == null || v == DBNull.Value) return false;
            if (v is string s) return !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s);
            return true;
        }

        private static decimal GetDecimalWithTextFallback(DataRow row, string primaryCol, string textAltCol)
        {
            if (HasNonEmptyValue(row, primaryCol)) return GetDecimal(row, primaryCol);
            if (HasNonEmptyValue(row, textAltCol)) return GetDecimal(row, textAltCol);
            return 0m;
        }

        private static string GetString(DataRow row, string col)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(col) || row[col] == DBNull.Value) return null;
            var s = row[col].ToString();
            return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s) ? null : s;
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\ModernTreasuryLib\FundingFeeDatedLoader.cs ---
public static void LoadDateRangeModernTreasuryFeeProcessingCETAsync(string server, string start_date, string end_date)
        {
            
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(start_date, out var start))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid start_date", nameof(start_date));
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(end_date, out var end))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid end_date", nameof(end_date));
            if (end.Date < start.Date)
                throw new ArgumentException("end_date must be the same or after start_date");

            
            DataTable CETFeeIssueDateList = GetCETWireReportFeeReturnDateList(server, start_date, end_date);

            if (CETFeeIssueDateList == null || CETFeeIssueDateList.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                
                return;
            }

            
            foreach (DataRow row in CETFeeIssueDateList.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null)
                    continue;

                object issuedObj = null;
                if (CETFeeIssueDateList.Columns.Contains("issued"))
                    issuedObj = row["issued"];
                else if (row.ItemArray.Length > 0)
                    issuedObj = row[0];

                if (issuedObj == null || issuedObj == DBNull.Value)
                    continue;

                string issuedStr = issuedObj.ToString().Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(issuedStr))
                    continue;

                
                string target_date = issuedStr;
                if (DateTime.TryParse(issuedStr, out var parsedDate))
                    target_date = parsedDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd");

                try
                {
                    PushDailyCETReceivedFeesToModernTreasury_daterange(server, target_date);
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to process CET fees for date {target_date}: {ex.Message}");
                }
            }
        }

        public static string GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_FromApi(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            return GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_FromApiAsync(server, asset_id).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
        }

        public static async Task<string> GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_FromApiAsync(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(asset_id))
                return string.Empty;

            try
            {
                ServicePointManager.SecurityProtocol = SecurityProtocolType.Tls12;

                var base64Authorization = ModernTreasuryLib.Connectors.GetMTToken();
                using (var client = new HttpClient())
                {
                    client.DefaultRequestHeaders.Authorization = new System.Net.Http.Headers.AuthenticationHeaderValue("Basic", base64Authorization);

                    
                    
                    string categoriesUrl = "https:
                    var matchingCategories = new List<JObject>();

                    for (int page = 1; page <= 5; page++)
                    {
                        var resp = await client.GetAsync(categoriesUrl + "&page=" + page);
                        if (!resp.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                            break;

                        var content = await resp.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(content))
                            break;

                        JToken root = JToken.Parse(content);
                        JArray items = null;
                        if (root.Type == JTokenType.Array)
                        {
                            items = (JArray)root;
                        }
                        else if (root["data"] != null && root["data"].Type == JTokenType.Array)
                        {
                            items = (JArray)root["data"];
                        }
                        else if (root["ledger_account_categories"] != null && root["ledger_account_categories"].Type == JTokenType.Array)
                        {
                            items = (JArray)root["ledger_account_categories"];
                        }

                        if (items == null || items.Count == 0)
                            break;

                        foreach (var it in items)
                        {
                            try
                            {
                                var obj = (JObject)it;
                                var name = (string)obj["name"];
                                if (string.Equals(name?.Trim(), asset_id.Trim(), StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                                {
                                    matchingCategories.Add(obj);
                                }
                            }
                            catch {  }
                        }

                        
                        
                    }

                    if (matchingCategories.Count == 0)
                        return string.Empty;

                    
                    JObject latestCategory = matchingCategories
                        .OrderByDescending(c => (DateTime?) (c["created_at"] != null ? (DateTime?) DateTime.Parse(c["created_at"].ToString()) : null) ?? DateTime.MinValue)
                        .FirstOrDefault();

                    if (latestCategory == null)
                        latestCategory = matchingCategories.First();

                    string categoryId = latestCategory["id"]?.ToString();
                    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(categoryId))
                        return string.Empty;

                    
                    string accountsUrl = $"https:
                    var foundAccounts = new List<JObject>();

                    for (int page = 1; page <= 5; page++)
                    {
                        var resp2 = await client.GetAsync(accountsUrl + "&page=" + page);
                        if (!resp2.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                            break;

                        var content2 = await resp2.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(content2))
                            break;

                        JToken root2 = JToken.Parse(content2);
                        JArray accounts = null;
                        if (root2.Type == JTokenType.Array)
                            accounts = (JArray)root2;
                        else if (root2["data"] != null && root2["data"].Type == JTokenType.Array)
                            accounts = (JArray)root2["data"];
                        else if (root2["ledger_accounts"] != null && root2["ledger_accounts"].Type == JTokenType.Array)
                            accounts = (JArray)root2["ledger_accounts"];

                        if (accounts == null || accounts.Count == 0)
                            break;

                        foreach (var acc in accounts)
                        {
                            try
                            {
                                var aobj = (JObject)acc;

                                
                                var name = (string)aobj["name"];
                                var id = (string)aobj["id"];

                                bool isMatch = false;

                                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(name) && name.IndexOf(asset_id, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0 && name.IndexOf("investment", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0)
                                    isMatch = true;

                                
                                if (!isMatch && aobj["metadata"] != null && aobj["metadata"]["asset_id"] != null)
                                {
                                    var metaAsset = aobj["metadata"]["asset_id"].ToString();
                                    if (string.Equals(metaAsset?.Trim(), asset_id.Trim(), StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                                        isMatch = true;
                                }

                                if (isMatch)
                                    foundAccounts.Add(aobj);
                            }
                            catch { }
                        }

                        
                    }

                    if (foundAccounts.Count == 0)
                        return string.Empty;

                    
                    JObject latestAccount = foundAccounts
                        .OrderByDescending(a => (DateTime?) (a["created_at"] != null ? (DateTime?) DateTime.Parse(a["created_at"].ToString()) : null) ?? DateTime.MinValue)
                        .FirstOrDefault();

                    return latestAccount?["id"]?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"ModernTreasury API lookup failed: {ex.Message}");
                return string.Empty;
            }
        }

        public static async Task AddLedgerAccountsToCategoryAsync(string server, DataTable assetCategoryTable, string ledgerAccountType)
        {
            if (assetCategoryTable == null || assetCategoryTable.Rows.Count == 0)
                return;

            string typeKey = (ledgerAccountType ?? string.Empty).Trim().ToLowerInvariant();
            if (typeKey != "investmentpayment" && typeKey != "purchaseproceeds")
                throw new ArgumentException("ledgerAccountType must be 'InvestmentPayment' or 'PurchaseProceeds'", nameof(ledgerAccountType));

            string FindColumn(params string[] candidates)
            {
                foreach (var cand in candidates)
                {
                    if (assetCategoryTable.Columns.Contains(cand)) return cand;
                    foreach (DataColumn col in assetCategoryTable.Columns)
                        if (string.Equals(col.ColumnName, cand, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                            return col.ColumnName;
                }
                return null;
            }

            string assetCol = FindColumn("asset_id");
            string categoryCol = FindColumn("ledger_account_category_id", "category_id", "target_category_id");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCol) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(categoryCol))
                return;

            var seen = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            foreach (DataRow row in assetCategoryTable.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null) continue;
                string assetId = row[assetCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                string targetCategoryId = row[categoryCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetCategoryId))
                    continue;

                string dedupKey = assetId + "|" + targetCategoryId + "|" + typeKey;
                if (!seen.Add(dedupKey))
                    continue;

                try
                {
                    string ledgerAccountId = ResolveLedgerAccountIdByType(server, assetId, typeKey);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ledgerAccountId))
                        continue;

                    string url = $"https:
                    string body = "{}";

                    var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();
                    await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(url, body, "Put");
                }
                catch
                {
                    
                }
            }
        }

        
        
        public static async Task RemoveLedgerAccountsFromCategoryAsync(string server, DataTable assetCategoryTable, string ledgerAccountType)
        {
            if (assetCategoryTable == null || assetCategoryTable.Rows.Count == 0)
                return;

            string typeKey = (ledgerAccountType ?? string.Empty).Trim().ToLowerInvariant();
            if (typeKey != "investmentpayment" && typeKey != "purchaseproceeds")
                throw new ArgumentException("ledgerAccountType must be 'InvestmentPayment' or 'PurchaseProceeds'", nameof(ledgerAccountType));

            string FindColumn(params string[] candidates)
            {
                foreach (var cand in candidates)
                {
                    if (assetCategoryTable.Columns.Contains(cand)) return cand;
                    foreach (DataColumn col in assetCategoryTable.Columns)
                        if (string.Equals(col.ColumnName, cand, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                            return col.ColumnName;
                }
                return null;
            }

            string assetCol = FindColumn("asset_id");
            string categoryCol = FindColumn("ledger_account_category_id", "category_id", "target_category_id");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCol) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(categoryCol))
                return;

            var seen = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            foreach (DataRow row in assetCategoryTable.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null) continue;
                string assetId = row[assetCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                string targetCategoryId = row[categoryCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetCategoryId))
                    continue;

                string dedupKey = assetId + "|" + targetCategoryId + "|" + typeKey;
                if (!seen.Add(dedupKey))
                    continue;

                try
                {
                    string ledgerAccountId = ResolveLedgerAccountIdByType(server, assetId, typeKey);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ledgerAccountId))
                        continue;

                    string url = $"https:

                    var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();
                    await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(url, null, "Delete");
                }
                catch
                {
                    
                }
            }
        }

        }

        public static bool InsertModernTreasuryMap(string server, string asset_id, string transaction_label, string mt_id, string map_call_type, string pipeline_label, string mt_label_suffix, string asset_lookup, decimal total_amount, string mt_object_url, string calling_class, string title_escrow_company, decimal amount, string funding_date)
        {
            string categoryLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.category_label + asset_id;
            string subcategoryLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.subcategory_label + asset_id;
            string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + asset_id + mt_label_suffix;
            string expected_payment_label = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_label + total_amount;
            string initial_expected_payment_label = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.initial_expected_payment_label + total_amount;
            string payment_order_label = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.payment_order_label + total_amount;
            string archive_expected_payment_label = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.archive_expected_payment_label + total_amount;
            string ledger_transaction_label = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_transaction_label + total_amount;

            DataTable dt = new DataTable();
            dt.Columns.Add("asset_id", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("MODERN_TREASURY_ID", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID", typeof(int));
            dt.Columns.Add("MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID", typeof(int));
            dt.Columns.Add("update_time", typeof(DateTime));
            dt.Columns.Add("CREATED_AT", typeof(DateTime));
            dt.Columns.Add("updated_by", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("pipeline_label", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("asset_lookup", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("transaction_label", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("mt_object_url", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("title_escrow_company", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("amount", typeof(decimal));
            dt.Columns.Add("funding_date", typeof(string));

            DataRow newRow = dt.NewRow();
            newRow["asset_id"] = asset_id;
            newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID"] = mt_id;
            newRow["update_time"] = DateTime.UtcNow;
            newRow["CREATED_AT"] = DateTime.UtcNow;
            newRow["pipeline_label"] = pipeline_label;
            newRow["transaction_label"] = transaction_label;
            newRow["mt_object_url"] = mt_object_url;
            newRow["asset_lookup"] = asset_lookup;
            newRow["updated_by"] = calling_class;
            newRow["title_escrow_company"] = title_escrow_company;
            newRow["amount"] = amount;
            newRow["funding_date"] = funding_date;

            switch (map_call_type)
            {
                case "category":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 1;
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = categoryLabel;
                    newRow["asset_lookup"] = asset_id;
                    break;
                case "ledger_account":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 2;
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = accountLabel;
                    newRow["asset_lookup"] = asset_id;
                    switch (mt_label_suffix)
                    {
                        case " Investment Payment":
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = 1;
                            break;
                        case " Origination Fees":
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = 2;
                            break;
                        case " Appraisal Fees":
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = 3;
                            break;
                        case " Gain on Sale":
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = 4;
                            break;
                        case " Purchase Proceeds":
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = 5;
                            break;
                        case " MSR Asset":
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = 6;
                            break;
                        case " Settlement":
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = 7;
                            break;
                        default:
                            newRow["MT_LEDGER_ACCOUNT_TYPE_ID"] = DBNull.Value;
                            break;
                    }
                    break;
                case "payment_order":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 3;
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = payment_order_label;
                    break;
                case "expected_payment":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 4;
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = expected_payment_label;
                    break;
                case "initial_expected_payment":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 4;
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = initial_expected_payment_label;
                    break;
                case "archive_expected_payment":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 4;
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = archive_expected_payment_label;
                    break;
                case "subcategory":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 5;
                    {
                        
                        string parsedWord = GetCapitalizedWordBeforeSubcategory(transaction_label);
                        string finalSubcategoryLabel = string.IsNullOrEmpty(parsedWord)
                            ? subcategoryLabel
                            : parsedWord + subcategoryLabel;

                        newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = finalSubcategoryLabel;
                    }
                    newRow["asset_lookup"] = asset_id;
                    break;
                case "ledger_transaction":
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 6;
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_LABEL"] = ledger_transaction_label;
                    break;
                default:
                    newRow["MODERN_TREASURY_ID_TYPE_ID"] = 0;
                    break;
            }

            dt.Rows.Add(newRow);

            List<string> insert_statements = Database.DBUtils.GenerateInsertStatements("ModernTreasuryMapping", dt, true, true).inserts_raw_dog;

            foreach (string insert in insert_statements)
            {
                Query q = new Query(insert, server);
                q.Execute();
            }

            return true;
        }

        public static async Task<string> CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync(string subcategoryName, string parentCategoryId, string assetId)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(subcategoryName))
                throw new ArgumentException("subcategoryName is required", nameof(subcategoryName));
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(parentCategoryId))
                throw new ArgumentException("parentCategoryId is required", nameof(parentCategoryId));

            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;

            var ledgerAccountCategory = new MTApiObjects.LedgerAccountCategory
            {
                name = subcategoryName,
                currency = "USD",
                normal_balance = "debit",
                ledger_account_category_ids = new List<string> { parentCategoryId },
                ledger_id = targetLedger,
                description = $"{Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.subcategory_label}{assetId} {subcategoryName}"
            };

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccountCategory);
            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }

        private static string GetCapitalizedWordBeforeSubcategory(string transactionLabel)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(transactionLabel))
                return string.Empty;

            var match = Regex.Match(transactionLabel, @"([A-Za-z0-9]+)_subcategory", RegexOptions.IgnoreCase);
            if (!match.Success || match.Groups.Count < 2)
                return string.Empty;

            string word = match.Groups[1].Value;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(word))
                return string.Empty;

            string lower = word.ToLowerInvariant();
            return char.ToUpperInvariant(lower[0]) + (lower.Length > 1 ? lower.Substring(1) : string.Empty);
        }

        
        private static string ResolveLedgerAccountIdByType(string server, string assetId, string typeKey)
        {
            switch (typeKey)
            {
                case "investmentpayment":
                    return GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment(server, assetId);
                case "purchaseproceeds":
                    return GetMTIDbyAssetId_PurchaseProceeds(server, assetId);
                default:
                    return null;
            }
        }
    }
}
