using static ModernTreasuryLib.Constants;
using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;

namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class MTMSRSaleGlobals
    {
        public static string server = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL;
        public static string msr_trade_id = "";
        public static string asset_id_string = "";
        public static decimal total_msr_sale_amount = 0;
        public static string msr_revenue_account_id = "";
        public static string uti_account_id = "";
        public static string asset_category_id = "";
        public static string msr_asset_ledger_account_id = ""; 
        public static string account_id = ""; 
        public static string investor_memo_category_id = ""; 
    }

    public class MSRSaleFlow
    {
        public static async Task CreateMSRSaleFlowAsync(DataTable assetSaleData, decimal totalSaleAmount)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            if (assetSaleData.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No asset sale data provided.");
                return;
            }

            List<string> assetIds = new List<string>();
            foreach (DataRow row in assetSaleData.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.total_msr_sale_amount = totalSaleAmount;
                assetIds.Add(asset_id);
            }
            MTMSRSaleGlobals.asset_id_string = string.Join(",", assetIds);

            DataRow firstRow = assetSaleData.Rows[0];
            MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_trade_id = firstRow["trade_id"].ToString();
            if (assetSaleData.Columns.Contains("account_id"))
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.account_id = firstRow["account_id"].ToString(); 
            MTMSRSaleGlobals.asset_category_id = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AssetCategory(MTMSRSaleGlobals.server, firstRow["asset_id"].ToString());
            MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_asset_ledger_account_id = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_MSRAsset(MTMSRSaleGlobals.server, firstRow["asset_id"].ToString());

            
            if (assetSaleData.Columns.Contains("investor_mt_account_id") && firstRow["investor_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.investor_memo_category_id = firstRow["investor_mt_account_id"].ToString();

            MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_revenue_account_id = await CreateMSRSaleLedgerAccountAsync(
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.server,
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_trade_id,
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.asset_category_id,
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.investor_memo_category_id
            );

            await CreateMSRSaleExpectedPaymentAsync(
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.server,
                assetSaleData,
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_revenue_account_id,
                ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id, 
                MTMSRSaleGlobals.total_msr_sale_amount
            );
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateMSRSaleLedgerAccountAsync(string server, string MSRTradeID, string assetCategoryId, string investorMemoCategoryId)
        {
            string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + MSRTradeID + "_MSR_Sale";
            string ledgerAccountName = MSRTradeID + "_MSR_Sale";
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;

            
            string tradesSubCategoryId = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Trades", assetCategoryId, MSRTradeID);
            List<string> categoryIds = new List<string> { tradesSubCategoryId };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoCategoryId)) categoryIds.Add(investorMemoCategoryId);

            LedgerAccount ledgerAccount = new LedgerAccount
            {
                name = ledgerAccountName,
                currency = "USD",
                normal_balance = "credit",
                ledger_account_category_ids = categoryIds,
                ledger_id = targetLedger,
                description = accountLabel
            };

            JObject ledgerAccountJo = JObject.FromObject(ledgerAccount);
            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccountJo);

            string result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, MSRTradeID, "create_ledger_account_msr_sale", result, "ledger_account", null, "_MSR_Sale", MSRTradeID, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + result, "MSRSaleFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            return result;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateMSRSaleExpectedPaymentAsync(
            string server,
            DataTable assetSaleData,
            string msrRevenueAccountId,
            string utiAccountId,
            decimal totalSaleAmount)
        {
            int totalSaleIntAmount = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(totalSaleAmount, 2) * 100);

            ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = $"MSR Sale Expected Payment for Sale",
                    ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryEP>()
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = utiAccountId,
                        direction = "debit",
                        amount_lower_bound = totalSaleIntAmount,
                        amount_upper_bound = totalSaleIntAmount,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "msr_trade_id", MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_trade_id },
                            { "asset_ids", MTMSRSaleGlobals.asset_id_string },
                            { "total_msr_sale_amount", totalSaleAmount.ToString() }
                        }
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "msr_sale" },
                    { "initiated_by", "MSRSaleFlow.cs" },
                    { "msr_trade_id", MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_trade_id },
                    { "asset_ids", MTMSRSaleGlobals.asset_id_string },
                    { "total_msr_sale_amount", totalSaleAmount.ToString() }
                }
            };

            
            string investor_contra_memo_account_id = null;
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(MTMSRSaleGlobals.account_id))
            {
                DataTable memo = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(server, MTMSRSaleGlobals.account_id);
                if (memo != null && memo.Rows.Count > 0 && memo.Columns.Contains("investor_contra_memo_account_id"))
                    investor_contra_memo_account_id = memo.Rows[0]["investor_contra_memo_account_id"].ToString();
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assetSaleData.Rows)
            {
                decimal msr_sale_amount = Convert.ToDecimal(row["msr_sale_amount"]);
                int msr_sale_int_amount = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(msr_sale_amount, 2) * 100);

                
                expectedPayment.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(new LedgerEntryEP
                {
                    amount = msr_sale_int_amount,
                    direction = "credit",
                    ledger_account_id = msrRevenueAccountId
                });

                
                expectedPayment.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(new LedgerEntryEP
                {
                    amount = msr_sale_int_amount,
                    direction = "debit",
                    ledger_account_id = utiAccountId
                });

                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_asset_ledger_account_id) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(investor_contra_memo_account_id))
                {
                    expectedPayment.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(new LedgerEntryEP
                    {
                        amount = msr_sale_int_amount,
                        direction = "credit",
                        ledger_account_id = MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_asset_ledger_account_id
                    });
                    expectedPayment.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(new LedgerEntryEP
                    {
                        amount = msr_sale_int_amount,
                        direction = "debit",
                        ledger_account_id = investor_contra_memo_account_id
                    });
                }
            }

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPayment);
            string result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_trade_id, "create_expected_payment_msr_sale", result, "expected_payment", null, "_MSR_Sale", MTMSRSaleGlobals.msr_trade_id, totalSaleAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + result, "MSRSaleFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            return result;
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\ModernTreasuryLib\RemittanceFeesFlow.cs ---
using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;

namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public static class MTRemittanceFeeGlobals
    {
        public static string server = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL;
        public static string remittance_period = "";
    }

    
    public class RemittanceFeesFlow
    {
        
        
        
        
        
        public static async Task CreateRemittanceFeesFlowAsync(
            DataTable data,
            decimal total_am_fee_retained_summary,
            decimal total_am_fee_sold_summary,
            decimal total_incentive_fee_retained_summary,
            decimal total_incentive_fee_sold_summary,
            decimal total_disposition_fee_retained_summary,
            decimal total_disposition_fee_sold_summary,
            decimal total_settlement_fee_summary,
            decimal total_purchase_premium_recovery_summary)
        {
            if (data == null || data.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No remittance fee data supplied.");
                return;
            }

            if (data.Columns.Contains("remittance_period"))
                MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.remittance_period = data.Rows[0]["remittance_period"].ToString();

            
            var activeRows = data.AsEnumerable().Where(r => !IsTerminated(r));
            var terminatedRows = data.AsEnumerable().Where(r => IsTerminated(r));

            await ProcessActiveAsync(activeRows.CopyToDataTableSafe(), total_am_fee_retained_summary, total_am_fee_sold_summary);
            await ProcessTerminatedAsync(terminatedRows.CopyToDataTableSafe(),
                total_incentive_fee_retained_summary,
                total_incentive_fee_sold_summary,
                total_disposition_fee_retained_summary,
                total_disposition_fee_sold_summary,
                total_settlement_fee_summary,
                total_purchase_premium_recovery_summary);
        }

        private static bool IsTerminated(DataRow r)
        {
            if (!r.Table.Columns.Contains("terminated")) return false; 
            var v = r["terminated"];
            if (v == DBNull.Value) return false;
            string s = v.ToString().Trim().ToLowerInvariant();
            return s == "1" || s == "true" || s == "yes" || s == "y";
        }

        #region Active (Asset Management Fee) Processing
        private static async Task ProcessActiveAsync(DataTable active, decimal retainedSummary, decimal soldSummary)
        {
            if (active == null || active.Rows.Count == 0) return;

            bool hasRetained = active.Columns.Contains("am_fee_retained");
            bool hasSold = active.Columns.Contains("am_fee_sold");

            decimal totalRetained = 0m;
            decimal totalSold = 0m;

            
            var sendingGroups = active.AsEnumerable().GroupBy(r => r.Table.Columns.Contains("sending_account_name") ? r["sending_account_name"].ToString() : "(none)");
            string firstLedgerAccountId = null;

            foreach (var group in sendingGroups)
            {
                var aggregateEP = BuildEmptyExpectedPayment($"Asset Management Fees Aggregate EP ({group.Key})", "asset_management_fee_group", group.Key);
                int aggregateRetainedInt = 0; 
                int aggregateSoldInt = 0;

                foreach (DataRow row in group)
                {
                    string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                    decimal retained = hasRetained && row["am_fee_retained"] != DBNull.Value ? Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["am_fee_retained"]),2) : 0m;
                    decimal sold = hasSold && row["am_fee_sold"] != DBNull.Value ? Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["am_fee_sold"]),2) : 0m;
                    totalRetained += retained; totalSold += sold;

                    string categoryId = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AssetCategory(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, assetId);
                    string ledgerAccountId = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync(assetId, categoryId, "AM_Fee");
                    if (firstLedgerAccountId == null) firstLedgerAccountId = ledgerAccountId;

                    if (retained > 0)
                        AddDebitCredit(aggregateEP, retained, Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account, ledgerAccountId, assetId, "asset_management_fee_retained", group.Key);
                    if (sold > 0)
                        AddDebitCredit(aggregateEP, sold, Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account, ledgerAccountId, assetId, "asset_management_fee_sold", group.Key);

                    aggregateRetainedInt += ToInt(retained);
                    aggregateSoldInt += ToInt(sold);
                }

                
                int totalInt = aggregateRetainedInt + aggregateSoldInt;
                aggregateEP.reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account,
                        direction = "debit",
                        amount_lower_bound = totalInt,
                        amount_upper_bound = totalInt,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string,string>
                        {
                            { "sending_account_name", group.Key },
                            { "remittance_period", MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.remittance_period ?? string.Empty },
                            { "fee_group", "asset_management" }
                        }
                    }
                };

                string epBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(aggregateEP);
                string epId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, null, "create_group_expected_payment_asset_management", epId, "expected_payment", null, "_AM_Group", null, (decimal)totalInt/100m, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + epId, "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs", null, 0m);

                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, assetId, $"create_ledger_account_{suffix.ToLower()}", id, "ledger_account", null, "_"+suffix, assetId, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + id, "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs", null, 0m);

                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, null, $"create_{feeGroup}_{disposition.ToLower()}_remittance_fee_purchase_order", id, "payment_order", null, "_RemittanceFeeAgg", null, aggregateAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.payment_order_url_prefix + id, "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            }

            if (totalRetained != retainedSummary)
                throw new InvalidOperationException($"AM Fee Retained aggregate ({totalRetained}) mismatch summary ({retainedSummary}).");
            if (totalSold != soldSummary)
                throw new InvalidOperationException($"AM Fee Sold aggregate ({totalSold}) mismatch summary ({soldSummary}).");

            
            if (firstLedgerAccountId != null)
            {
                if (totalRetained > 0)
                    await CreateAggregatePurchaseOrderAsync(firstLedgerAccountId, totalRetained, "Retained", "asset_management");
                if (totalSold > 0)
                    await CreateAggregatePurchaseOrderAsync(firstLedgerAccountId, totalSold, "Sold", "asset_management");
            }
        }
        #endregion

        #region Terminated (Settlement Fee) Processing
        private static async Task ProcessTerminatedAsync(DataTable term, decimal incentiveRetainedSummary, decimal incentiveSoldSummary, decimal dispositionRetainedSummary, decimal dispositionSoldSummary, decimal settlementFeeSummary, decimal purchasePremiumRecoverySummary)
        {
            if (term == null || term.Rows.Count == 0) return;

            bool hasIncentiveRetained = term.Columns.Contains("incentive_fee_retained");
            bool hasIncentiveSold = term.Columns.Contains("incentive_fee_sold");
            bool hasDispositionRetained = term.Columns.Contains("disposition_fee_retained");
            bool hasDispositionSold = term.Columns.Contains("disposition_fee_sold");
            bool hasSettlementFee = term.Columns.Contains("settlement_fee");
            bool hasPPR = term.Columns.Contains("purchase_premium_recovery");

            decimal totIncentiveRetained = 0m, totIncentiveSold = 0m, totDispositionRetained = 0m, totDispositionSold = 0m, totSettlementFee = 0m, totPPR = 0m;
            string firstLedgerAccountId = null; 

            var sendingGroups = term.AsEnumerable().GroupBy(r => r.Table.Columns.Contains("sending_account_name") ? r["sending_account_name"].ToString() : "(none)");
            foreach (var group in sendingGroups)
            {
                var aggregateEP = BuildEmptyExpectedPayment($"Terminated Settlement Fees Aggregate EP ({group.Key})", "settlement_fee_group", group.Key);
                decimal netDebit = 0m; 

                foreach (DataRow row in group)
                {
                    string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                    string categoryId = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AssetCategory(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, assetId);

                    
                    string incentiveLA = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync(assetId, categoryId, "Incentive_Fee");
                    string dispositionLA = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync(assetId, categoryId, "Disposition_Fee");
                    string settlementLA = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync(assetId, categoryId, "Settlement_Fee");
                    string pprLA = hasPPR ? await CreateLedgerAccountAsync(assetId, categoryId, "Purchase_Premium_Recovery") : null;
                    if (firstLedgerAccountId == null) firstLedgerAccountId = incentiveLA ?? dispositionLA ?? settlementLA ?? pprLA;

                    decimal incRet = hasIncentiveRetained ? GetDecimal(row, "incentive_fee_retained") : 0m; totIncentiveRetained += incRet;
                    decimal incSold = hasIncentiveSold ? GetDecimal(row, "incentive_fee_sold") : 0m; totIncentiveSold += incSold;
                    decimal dispRet = hasDispositionRetained ? GetDecimal(row, "disposition_fee_retained") : 0m; totDispositionRetained += dispRet;
                    decimal dispSold = hasDispositionSold ? GetDecimal(row, "disposition_fee_sold") : 0m; totDispositionSold += dispSold;
                    decimal sett = hasSettlementFee ? GetDecimal(row, "settlement_fee") : 0m; totSettlementFee += sett;
                    decimal ppr = hasPPR ? GetDecimal(row, "purchase_premium_recovery") : 0m; totPPR += ppr;

                    if (incRet > 0) { AddDebitCredit(aggregateEP, incRet, Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account, incentiveLA, assetId, "incentive_fee_retained", group.Key); netDebit += incRet; }
                    if (incSold > 0) { AddDebitCredit(aggregateEP, incSold, Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account, incentiveLA, assetId, "incentive_fee_sold", group.Key); netDebit += incSold; }
                    if (dispRet > 0) { AddDebitCredit(aggregateEP, dispRet, Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account, dispositionLA, assetId, "disposition_fee_retained", group.Key); netDebit += dispRet; }
                    if (dispSold > 0) { AddDebitCredit(aggregateEP, dispSold, Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account, dispositionLA, assetId, "disposition_fee_sold", group.Key); netDebit += dispSold; }
                    if (sett > 0) { AddDebitCredit(aggregateEP, sett, Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account, settlementLA, assetId, "settlement_fee", group.Key); netDebit += sett; }

                    
                    if (ppr > 0 && pprLA != null)
                    {
                        
                        
                        var debitPpr = new LedgerEntryEP { amount = ToInt(ppr), direction = "debit", ledger_account_id = pprLA };
                        var creditClearing = new LedgerEntryEP { amount = ToInt(ppr), direction = "credit", ledger_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account };
                        aggregateEP.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(debitPpr);
                        aggregateEP.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(creditClearing);
                        
                    }
                }

                int netInt = ToInt(netDebit);
                aggregateEP.reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account,
                        direction = "debit",
                        amount_lower_bound = netInt,
                        amount_upper_bound = netInt,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string,string>
                        {
                            { "sending_account_name", group.Key },
                            { "remittance_period", MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.remittance_period ?? string.Empty },
                            { "fee_group", "terminated_settlement" }
                        }
                    }
                };

                string epBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(aggregateEP);
                string epId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, null, "create_group_expected_payment_settlement", epId, "expected_payment", null, "_Settlement_Group", null, (decimal)netInt/100m, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + epId, "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            }

            
            Validate(totIncentiveRetained, incentiveRetainedSummary, "Incentive Fee Retained");
            Validate(totIncentiveSold, incentiveSoldSummary, "Incentive Fee Sold");
            Validate(totDispositionRetained, dispositionRetainedSummary, "Disposition Fee Retained");
            Validate(totDispositionSold, dispositionSoldSummary, "Disposition Fee Sold");
            Validate(totSettlementFee, settlementFeeSummary, "Settlement Fee");
            Validate(totPPR, purchasePremiumRecoverySummary, "Purchase Premium Recovery");
        }
        #endregion

        #region Shared helpers
        private static int ToInt(decimal amt) => Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(amt,2)*100);

        private static ExpectedPayment BuildEmptyExpectedPayment(string description, string txnType, string sendingAccountName)
        {
            return new ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = description,
                    ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryEP>()
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string,string>
                {
                    { "transaction_type", txnType },
                    { "initiated_by", "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs" },
                    { "sending_account_name", sendingAccountName },
                    { "remittance_period", MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.remittance_period ?? string.Empty }
                }
            };
        }

        private static void AddDebitCredit(ExpectedPayment ep, decimal amount, string debitLedgerId, string creditLedgerId, string assetId, string feeType, string sendingAccountName)
        {
            int intAmount = ToInt(amount);
            ep.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(new LedgerEntryEP
            {
                amount = intAmount,
                direction = "debit",
                ledger_account_id = debitLedgerId
            });
            ep.ledger_transaction.ledger_entries.Add(new LedgerEntryEP
            {
                amount = intAmount,
                direction = "credit",
                ledger_account_id = creditLedgerId
            });

            
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateLedgerAccountAsync(string assetId, string categoryId, string suffix)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(categoryId)) return null;
            string label = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + assetId + "_" + suffix;
            LedgerAccount la = new LedgerAccount
            {
                name = assetId + "_" + suffix,
                currency = "USD",
                normal_balance = suffix.Contains("Recovery") ? "debit" : "credit", 
                ledger_account_category_ids = new List<string> { categoryId },
                ledger_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id,
                description = label
            };
            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(la);
            string id = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, assetId, $"create_ledger_account_{suffix.ToLower()}", id, "ledger_account", null, "_"+suffix, assetId, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + id, "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            return id;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateAggregatePurchaseOrderAsync(string ledgerAccountId, decimal aggregateAmount, string disposition, string feeGroup)
        {
            int amtInt = ToInt(aggregateAmount);
            bool isRetained = disposition.Equals("Retained", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            string clearing = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account;
            string debitAccount = isRetained ? ledgerAccountId : Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;

            PaymentOrder po = new PaymentOrder
            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionPO
                {
                    ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryPO>
                    {
                        new LedgerEntryPO { amount = amtInt, direction = "debit", ledger_account_id = debitAccount },
                        new LedgerEntryPO { amount = amtInt, direction = "credit", ledger_account_id = clearing }
                    }
                },
                nsfs_protected = false,
                type = "wire",
                amount = amtInt,
                direction = "debit",
                originating_account_id = debitAccount,
                receiving_account_id = clearing,
                receiving_account_type = "internal_account",
                metadata = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(new Dictionary<string,string>
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "remittance_fee_aggregate" },
                    { "fee_group", feeGroup },
                    { "fee_disposition", disposition.ToLower() },
                    { "remittance_period", MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.remittance_period ?? string.Empty },
                    { "initiated_by", "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs" }
                })
            };

            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(po);
            string id = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTRemittanceFeeGlobals.server, null, $"create_{feeGroup}_{disposition.ToLower()}_remittance_fee_purchase_order", id, "payment_order", null, "_RemittanceFeeAgg", null, aggregateAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.payment_order_url_prefix + id, "RemittanceFeesFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            return id;
        }

        private static decimal GetDecimal(DataRow row, string column)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(column) || row[column] == DBNull.Value) return 0m;
            return Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row[column]), 2);
        }

        private static void Validate(decimal actual, decimal summary, string label)
        {
            if (actual != summary)
                throw new InvalidOperationException($"{label} aggregate ({actual}) does not match summary ({summary}).");
        }
        #endregion
    }

    internal static class DataTableExtensions
    {
        public static DataTable CopyToDataTableSafe(this IEnumerable<DataRow> rows)
        {
            var list = rows.ToList();
            if (!list.Any()) return null;
            return list.CopyToDataTable();
        }
    }
}

using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;

namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public static class MTSettlementGlobals
    {

        public static async Task<string> CreateExpectedPaymentFromSettlementRequest(DataTable assetData)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            if (assetData == null || assetData.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No settlement asset data provided.");
                return null;
            }
            if (assetData.Rows.Count > 1)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("More than one row provided. Only a single asset row expected for settlement expected payment.");
            }

            DataRow row = assetData.Rows[0];
            string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
            decimal projected_net_settlement_payment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["projected_net_settlement_payment"]);
            string statement_date = row["statement_date"].ToString();
            string projected_close_date = row["projected_close_date"].ToString();
            string settlement_type = row["settlement_type"].ToString();
            string settlement_reason = row["settlement_reason"].ToString();
            string settlement_fee = row.Table.Columns.Contains("settlement_fee") && row["settlement_fee"] != DBNull.Value ? row["settlement_fee"].ToString() : "0";
            string unpaid_owner_obligations = row.Table.Columns.Contains("unpaid_owner_obligations") && row["unpaid_owner_obligations"] != DBNull.Value ? row["unpaid_owner_obligations"].ToString() : "0";
            string credits = row.Table.Columns.Contains("credits") && row["credits"] != DBNull.Value ? row["credits"].ToString() : "0";

            decimal roundedAmount = Math.Round(projected_net_settlement_payment, 2);
            int amountInt = Convert.ToInt32(roundedAmount * 100);

            
            string uamCollectionsInternalAccount = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_collections_account;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(uamCollectionsInternalAccount))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("TCB_recon_uam_collections key is not set. Aborting settlement expected payment creation.");
                return null;
            }

            ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = $"Settlement Expected Payment for Asset {asset_id} ({settlement_type})",
                    ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryEP>() 
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = uamCollectionsInternalAccount,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = amountInt,
                        amount_upper_bound = amountInt,
                        date_lower_bound = statement_date,
                        date_upper_bound = projected_close_date,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string,string>
                        {
                            { "asset_id", asset_id },
                            { "projected_net_settlement_payment", roundedAmount.ToString() },
                            { "statement_date", statement_date },
                            { "projected_close_date", projected_close_date },
                            { "credits", credits }
                        }
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string,string>
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "asset_settlement" },
                    { "initiated_by", "SettlementFlow.cs" },
                    { "asset_id", asset_id },
                    { "projected_net_settlement_payment", roundedAmount.ToString() },
                    { "statement_date", statement_date },
                    { "projected_close_date", projected_close_date },
                    { "settlement_type", settlement_type },
                    { "settlement_reason", settlement_reason },
                    { "settlement_fee", settlement_fee },
                    { "unpaid_owner_obligations", unpaid_owner_obligations },
                    { "credits", credits }
                }
            };

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPayment);
            string result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

            bool mapInserted = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTSettlementGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_settlement_expected_payment", result, "expected_payment", null, "_Settlement", asset_id, roundedAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + result, "SettlementFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            if (!mapInserted)
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for settlement expected payment asset_id: {asset_id}");

            return result;
        }

        
        
        public static async Task CreateSettlementDistributionAsync(DataTable settlementData)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (settlementData == null || settlementData.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No settlement distribution data provided.");
                return;
            }
            DataRow row = settlementData.Rows[0];

            
            string asset_id = row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id") ? row["asset_id"].ToString() : null;
            decimal projected_net_settlement_payment = row.Table.Columns.Contains("projected_net_settlement_payment") ? Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["projected_net_settlement_payment"]), 2) : 0m;
            decimal collections_transfer_amount = row.Table.Columns.Contains("collections_transfer_amount") ? Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["collections_transfer_amount"]), 2) : 0m;
            decimal customer_refund_amount = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_refund_amount") ? Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["customer_refund_amount"]), 2) : 0m;
            string account_id = row.Table.Columns.Contains("account_id") ? row["account_id"].ToString() : null;

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(account_id))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("account_id required for settlement distribution (to locate memo accounts).");
                return;
            }

            
            DataTable memoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(MTSettlementGlobals.server, account_id);
            string investor_memo_account_id = null;
            string investor_contra_memo_account_id = null;
            if (memoAccounts != null && memoAccounts.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                DataRow memoRow = memoAccounts.Rows[0];
                investor_memo_account_id = memoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_memo_account_id") ? memoRow["investor_memo_account_id"].ToString() : null;
                investor_contra_memo_account_id = memoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_contra_memo_account_id") ? memoRow["investor_contra_memo_account_id"].ToString() : null;
            }

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investor_memo_account_id) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(investor_contra_memo_account_id))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Missing investor memo or contra memo account id; cannot create distribution ledger transaction.");
                return;
            }

            
            string uam_collections_ledger_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_collections_account; 
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(uam_collections_ledger_account_id))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("UAM collections ledger account id missing.");
                return;
            }

            int netSettleInt = Convert.ToInt32(projected_net_settlement_payment * 100);
            int collectionsTransferInt = Convert.ToInt32(collections_transfer_amount * 100);
            int customerRefundInt = Convert.ToInt32(customer_refund_amount * 100);

            
            var ledgerTransaction = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Settlement Distribution for Asset {asset_id}",
                ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                {
                    new JObject 
                    {
                        ["amount"] = netSettleInt,
                        ["direction"] = "debit",
                        ["ledger_account_id"] = uam_collections_ledger_account_id
                    }
                }
            };

            
            if (collectionsTransferInt > 0)
            {
                ((JArray)ledgerTransaction["ledger_entries"]).Add(new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = collectionsTransferInt,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_memo_account_id
                });
                ((JArray)ledgerTransaction["ledger_entries"]).Add(new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = collectionsTransferInt,
                    ["direction"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id
                });
            }

            
            if (customerRefundInt > 0)
            {
                ((JArray)ledgerTransaction["ledger_entries"]).Add(new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = customerRefundInt,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id
                });
                ((JArray)ledgerTransaction["ledger_entries"]).Add(new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = customerRefundInt,
                    ["direction"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id
                });
            }

            string ltBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerTransaction);
            string ledgerTransactionId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            string ltUrl = "https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTSettlementGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_settlement_distribution_ledger_transaction", ledgerTransactionId, "ledger_transaction", null, "_Settlement", asset_id, projected_net_settlement_payment, ltUrl, "SettlementFlow.cs", null, 0m);

            
            if (collectionsTransferInt > 0)
            {
                var collectionsPO = new PaymentOrder
                {
                    ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionPO
                    {
                        ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryPO>
                        {
                            new LedgerEntryPO { amount = collectionsTransferInt, direction = "debit", ledger_account_id = investor_contra_memo_account_id },
                            new LedgerEntryPO { amount = collectionsTransferInt, direction = "credit", ledger_account_id = investor_memo_account_id }
                        }
                    },
                    nsfs_protected = false,
                    type = "wire",
                    amount = collectionsTransferInt,
                    direction = "credit",
                    originating_account_id = uam_collections_ledger_account_id,
                    receiving_account_id = investor_memo_account_id,
                    receiving_account_type = "internal_account"
                };
                string collPOBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(collectionsPO);
                string collPOId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTSettlementGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_settlement_collections_transfer_payment_order", collPOId, "payment_order", null, "_Settlement", asset_id, collections_transfer_amount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.payment_order_url_prefix + collPOId, "SettlementFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            }

            
            if (customerRefundInt > 0)
            {
                var refundPO = new PaymentOrder
                {
                    ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionPO
                    {
                        ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryPO>
                        {
                            new LedgerEntryPO { amount = customerRefundInt, direction = "debit", ledger_account_id = investor_contra_memo_account_id },
                            new LedgerEntryPO { amount = customerRefundInt, direction = "credit", ledger_account_id = investor_contra_memo_account_id }
                        }
                    },
                    nsfs_protected = false,
                    type = "wire",
                    amount = customerRefundInt,
                    direction = "credit",
                    originating_account_id = uam_collections_ledger_account_id,
                    receiving_account_id = investor_contra_memo_account_id,
                    receiving_account_type = "internal_account"
                };
                string refundPOBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(refundPO);
                string refundPOId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTSettlementGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_settlement_customer_refund_payment_order", refundPOId, "payment_order", null, "_Settlement", asset_id, customer_refund_amount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.payment_order_url_prefix + refundPOId, "SettlementFlow.cs", null, 0m);
            }
        }
    }

using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;

namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class MTTradeGlobals
    {
        public static string server = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL;
        
        public static string trade_id = "";
        public static string account_id = "";
        public static string counterparty_id = "";
        public static string trade_date = "";
        public static string settle_date = "";
        public static decimal price = 0;
        public static string asset_id_string = "";
        public static string investor_memo_account_name = "";

        
        public static decimal total_purchase_proceeds = 0;
        public static decimal total_gain_on_sale = 0;
        public static decimal total_haircut_sweep = 0;
        public static decimal total_oface = 0;
    }

    public class ModernTreasury_Trade
    {
        
        
        public static async Task CreateTradeLedgerAccountsOnlyAsync(DataTable asset_trade_data, string investor_memo_account_id, string investor_contra_memo_account_id)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            if (asset_trade_data == null || asset_trade_data.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No asset trade data provided for backfill ledger account creation.");
                return;
            }

            
            List<string> assetIds = new List<string>();
            foreach (DataRow r in asset_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                if (r.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id") && r["asset_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    assetIds.Add(r["asset_id"].ToString());
            }
            MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string = string.Join(",", assetIds);

            
            await CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
        }

        public static async Task CreateTradeMTAssetsAsync(DataTable asset_trade_data, decimal total_proceeds_summary)
        {
            
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            
            

            
            if (asset_trade_data.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No asset sale data provided.");
                return;
            }
            DataRow row = asset_trade_data.Rows[0];
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_id = row["trade_id"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.account_id = row["account_id"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id = row["counterparty_id"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_date = row["trade_date"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.settle_date = row["settle_date"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.price = Convert.ToDecimal(row["price"].ToString());
            MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds = 0;
            MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale = 0;
            MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep = 0;
            MTTradeGlobals.total_oface = 0;
            List<string> assetIds = new List<string>();

            
            foreach (DataRow assetRow in asset_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = assetRow["asset_id"].ToString();
                assetIds.Add(asset_id);
                MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds = MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["purchase_proceeds"].ToString());
                MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale = MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["gain_on_sale"].ToString());
                MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep = MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["haircut"].ToString());
                MTTradeGlobals.total_oface = MTTradeGlobals.total_oface + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["oface"].ToString());
            }
            MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string = string.Join(",", assetIds);

            
            if (MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds != total_proceeds_summary)
                throw new InvalidOperationException($"Total purchase proceeds ({MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds}) do not match the provided summary ({total_proceeds_summary}).");

            
            await CreateGainOnSaleLedgerAccountAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreatePurchaseProceedsExpectedPaymentsAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateHaircutSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateGainOnSaleSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateWarehouseLineSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateMSRAssetLedgerAccountAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateGainOnSaleLedgerAccountAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string result = null;

            foreach (DataRow row in assets_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.gain_on_sale_label;
                string ledgerAccountName = asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.gain_on_sale_label;
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("pipeline_label") ? row["pipeline_label"].ToString() : null;

                
                string asset_category_id = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AssetCategory(server, asset_id);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(asset_category_id))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Asset Category does not exist for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                }
                else
                {
                    string tradesSubCategoryId = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Trades", asset_category_id, asset_id);

                    
                    List<string> categoryIds = new List<string> { tradesSubCategoryId };
                    if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_mt_account_id") && row["investor_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    {
                        string investorMemoCategoryId = row["investor_mt_account_id"].ToString();
                        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoCategoryId)) categoryIds.Add(investorMemoCategoryId);
                    }

                    
                    LedgerAccount ledgerAccount = new LedgerAccount
                    {
                        name = ledgerAccountName,
                        currency = "USD",
                        normal_balance = "debit",
                        ledger_account_category_ids = categoryIds,
                        ledger_id = targetLedger,
                        description = accountLabel
                    };
                    JObject ledgerAccountJo = JObject.FromObject(ledgerAccount);
                    string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccountJo);
                    result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

                    bool insert_gain_on_sale_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_gain_on_sale", result, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.gain_on_sale_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + result, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m);

                    if (!insert_gain_on_sale_done)
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} Gain On Sale");

                }
            }
            return result;
        }

                    if (!insert_pp_done)
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} Purchase Proceeds");
                }
            }
            return result;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreatePurchaseProceedsExpectedPaymentsAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data)
        {
            string result = null;
            
            
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uf2_collections_account; 
            string receiving_ledger_account_UF2_coll = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UF2_collections_ledger_account_id;
            
            

            
            DataTable memoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(server, MTTradeGlobals.account_id);
            string investor_memo_account_id = null;
            string investor_contra_memo_account_id = null;
            MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name = null;

            if (memoAccounts != null && memoAccounts.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                DataRow memoRow = memoAccounts.Rows[0];
                investor_memo_account_id = memoRow["investor_memo_account_id"]?.ToString();
                investor_contra_memo_account_id = memoRow["investor_contra_memo_account_id"]?.ToString();
                MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name = memoRow["investor_memo_account_name"]?.ToString();
            }

            int total_purchase_proceeds_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds, 2) * 100);

            ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = "Trade # " + MTTradeGlobals.trade_id + " Purchase Proceeds Expected Payment of " + Math.Round(MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds, 2).ToString(),
                    ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryEP>
                    { }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = total_purchase_proceeds_int,
                        amount_upper_bound = total_purchase_proceeds_int,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "asset_ids", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string },
                            
                            { "trade_id", MTTradeGlobals.trade_id },
                            { "total_purchase_proceeds", MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds.ToString() },
                            { "account_name", MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name },
                            { "trade_date", MTTradeGlobals.trade_date },
                            { "settle_date", MTTradeGlobals.settle_date },
                        }
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    
                    { "transaction_type", "purchase_proceeds" },
                    { "initiated_by", "Tradeflow.cs" },
                    { "trade_id", MTTradeGlobals.trade_id },
                    { "account_name", MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name },
                    { "asset_ids", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string },
                    { "total_investment_payment", MTTradeGlobals.total_oface.ToString() },
                    { "total_gain_on_sale", MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale.ToString() },
                    { "total_purchase_proceeds", MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds.ToString() },
                    { "modern_treasury_view", "trade_flow" },
                    { "trade_date", MTTradeGlobals.trade_date },
                    { "settle_date", MTTradeGlobals.settle_date },
                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);

            
            foreach (DataRow row in assets_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                decimal purchase_proceeds = Convert.ToDecimal(row["purchase_proceeds"].ToString());
                int purchase_proceeds_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(purchase_proceeds, 2) * 100);
                decimal oface = Convert.ToDecimal(row["oface"].ToString());
                int oface_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(oface, 2) * 100);
                decimal gain_on_sale = Convert.ToDecimal(row["gain_on_sale"].ToString());
                int gain_on_sale_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(gain_on_sale, 2) * 100);
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("pipeline_label") ? row["pipeline_label"].ToString() : null;
                string investment_payment_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment(CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL, asset_id);
                string gain_on_sale_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_GainOnSale(CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL, asset_id);

                JObject metadata = new JObject
                {
                    ["asset_id"] = asset_id,
                    ["trade_id"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_id,
                    ["oface"] = oface.ToString(),
                    ["gain_on_sale"] = gain_on_sale.ToString(),
                    ["purchase_proceeds"] = purchase_proceeds.ToString(),
                    ["account_name"] = MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name,
                    ["trade_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_date,
                    ["settle_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.settle_date,
                    ["initiated_by"] = "Tradeflow.cs",
                    ["modern_treasury_view"] = "trade_flow"
                };

                JObject ledgerEntryDebit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = purchase_proceeds_int,
                    ["direction"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = receiving_ledger_account_UF2_coll,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };

                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(ledgerEntryDebit);

                JObject ledgerEntryCredit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = oface_int,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investment_payment_mtid,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };

                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(ledgerEntryCredit);

                JObject ledgerEntryCreditGOS = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = gain_on_sale_int,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = gain_on_sale_mtid,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };

                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(ledgerEntryCreditGOS);

                JObject memoLedgerEntryDebit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = purchase_proceeds_int,
                    ["direction"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_memo_account_id,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };

                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(memoLedgerEntryDebit);

                JObject contramemoledgerEntryCredit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = purchase_proceeds_int,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };

                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(contramemoledgerEntryCredit);
            }

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

            bool insert_purchase_proceeds_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, null, "create_purchase_proceeds_expected_payment", result, "expected_payment", null, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_label, null, MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + result, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m);

            if (!insert_purchase_proceeds_done)
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for trade_id: {MTTradeGlobals.trade_id} Expected Payment");

            return result;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateHaircutSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data)
        {
            string result = null;
            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string sourceLedgerAccountUF2Coll = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UF2_collections_ledger_account_id;
            string receivingAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_ups_account;
            int haircutIntAmount = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep, 2) * 100);

            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionEP
                {

                        new LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = haircutIntAmount,
                            direction = "debit",
                            ledger_account_id = receivingLedgerAccountUPS
                        },
                        new LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = haircutIntAmount,
                            direction = "credit",
                            ledger_account_id = sourceLedgerAccountUF2Coll
                        }
                    }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = receivingAccountUPS,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = haircutIntAmount,
                        amount_upper_bound = haircutIntAmount
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>()
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "haircut_sweep" },
                    { "initiated_by", "Tradeflow.cs" },
                    { "trade_id", MTTradeGlobals.trade_id },
                    { "account_name", MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name },
                    { "asset_ids", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string },

                    { "trade_date", MTTradeGlobals.trade_date },
                    { "settle_date", MTTradeGlobals.settle_date },
                }
            };

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPayment);
            result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            bool insert_haircut_sweep_EP_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, null, "create_haircut_sweep_expected_payment", result, "expected_payment", null, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_label, null, MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + result, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m);

            if (!insert_haircut_sweep_EP_done)
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for trade_id: {MTTradeGlobals.trade_id} Haircut Sweep Expected Payment");

        private static async Task CreateMSRAssetLedgerAccountAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;

            foreach (DataRow row in assets_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                
                string asset_category_id = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AssetCategory(server, asset_id);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(asset_category_id))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Skipping MSR Asset creation. Missing category for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                string tradesSubCategoryId = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Trades", asset_category_id, asset_id);

                string msrAccountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + asset_id + "_MSRAsset";
                string msrLedgerAccountName = asset_id + "_MSRAsset";

                
                List<string> categoryIds = new List<string> { tradesSubCategoryId };
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_mt_account_id") && row["investor_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                {
                    string investorMemoCategoryId = row["investor_mt_account_id"].ToString();
                    if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoCategoryId)) categoryIds.Add(investorMemoCategoryId);
                }

                
                LedgerAccount msrLedgerAccount = new LedgerAccount
                {
                    name = msrLedgerAccountName,
                    currency = "USD",
                    normal_balance = "debit",
                    ledger_account_category_ids = categoryIds,
                    ledger_id = targetLedger,
                    description = msrAccountLabel
                };
                JObject msrLedgerAccountJo = JObject.FromObject(msrLedgerAccount);
                string createAccountBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(msrLedgerAccountJo);
                string msrAccountId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

                bool insert_msr_asset_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_msr_asset", msrAccountId, "ledger_account", null, "_MSRAsset", asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + msrAccountId, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m);
                if (!insert_msr_asset_done)
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} MSRAsset ledger account");

                
                DataTable memoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(server, MTTradeGlobals.account_id);
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = null;
                if (memoAccounts != null && memoAccounts.Rows.Count > 0)
                {
                    DataRow memoRow = memoAccounts.Rows[0];
                    investor_contra_memo_account_id = memoRow["investor_contra_memo_account_id"]?.ToString();
                }

                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investor_contra_memo_account_id))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Skipping ledger transaction. Missing investor_contra_memo_account_id for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                
                decimal baseInvestmentPayment = 0m;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investment_payment") && row["investment_payment"] != DBNull.Value)
                {
                    baseInvestmentPayment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["investment_payment"]);
                }
                else if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("oface") && row["oface"] != DBNull.Value)
                {
                    baseInvestmentPayment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["oface"]);
                }
                else
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"No investment payment or oface column value for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                decimal msrAssetAmount = Math.Round(baseInvestmentPayment * 0.0325m, 2); 
                int msrAssetAmountInt = Convert.ToInt32(msrAssetAmount * 100);

                
                var ledgerTransaction = new JObject
                {
                    ["description"] = $"MSR Asset Recognition 3.25% for asset {asset_id}",
                    ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                    {
                        new JObject
                        {
                            ["amount"] = msrAssetAmountInt,
                            ["direction"] = "debit",
                            ["ledger_account_id"] = msrAccountId
                        },
                        new JObject
                        {
                            ["amount"] = msrAssetAmountInt,
                            ["direction"] = "credit",
                            ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id
                        }
                    }
                };

                string ledgerTransactionBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerTransaction);
                string ledgerTransactionId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

                string ltUrl = "https:
                bool insert_msr_asset_lt_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_msr_asset_ledger_transaction", ledgerTransactionId, "ledger_transaction", null, "_MSRAsset", asset_id, msrAssetAmount, ltUrl, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m);
                if (!insert_msr_asset_lt_done)
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} MSRAsset ledger transaction");
            }
        }

        public static async Task CreateSecuritizationTradeMTAssets(DataTable asset_trade_data, decimal transfer_amount)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            if (asset_trade_data == null || asset_trade_data.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No asset trade data provided for securitization trade.");
                return;
            }

            DataRow first = asset_trade_data.Rows[0];
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_id = first.Table.Columns.Contains("trade_id") ? first["trade_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.account_id = first.Table.Columns.Contains("account_id") ? first["account_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id = first.Table.Columns.Contains("counterparty_id") ? first["counterparty_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_date = first.Table.Columns.Contains("trade_date") ? first["trade_date"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.settle_date = first.Table.Columns.Contains("settle_date") ? first["settle_date"].ToString() : null;

            List<string> assetIds = new List<string>();
            foreach (DataRow r in asset_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                if (r.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id") && r["asset_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    assetIds.Add(r["asset_id"].ToString());
            }
            MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string = string.Join(",", assetIds);

            
            DataTable investorMemoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(MTTradeGlobals.server, MTTradeGlobals.account_id);
            if (investorMemoAccounts == null || investorMemoAccounts.Rows.Count == 0)
                throw new InvalidOperationException("No memo accounts found for investor account_id. Securitization trade aborted.");
            DataRow investorMemoRow = investorMemoAccounts.Rows[0];
            string investor_memo_account_id = investorMemoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_memo_account_id") ? investorMemoRow["investor_memo_account_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name = investorMemoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_memo_account_name") ? investorMemoRow["investor_memo_account_name"].ToString() : null;
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(investor_memo_account_id))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("Investor memo account id missing. Securitization trade aborted.");

            
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("counterparty_id is missing in trade data.");
            DataTable counterpartyMemoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(MTTradeGlobals.server, MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id);
            if (counterpartyMemoAccounts == null || counterpartyMemoAccounts.Rows.Count == 0)
                throw new InvalidOperationException("No memo accounts found for counterparty_id. Securitization trade aborted.");
            DataRow counterpartyMemoRow = counterpartyMemoAccounts.Rows[0];
            string counterparty_memo_account_id = counterpartyMemoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_memo_account_id") ? counterpartyMemoRow["investor_memo_account_id"].ToString() : null; 
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(counterparty_memo_account_id))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("Counterparty memo account id missing. Securitization trade aborted.");

            decimal roundedAmount = Math.Round(transfer_amount, 2);
            int amountInt = Convert.ToInt32(roundedAmount * 100);

            
            var ledgerTransaction = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Securitization Trade Transfer {roundedAmount} for Trade {MTTradeGlobals.trade_id}",
                ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                {
                    new JObject 
                    {
                        ["amount"] = amountInt,
                        ["direction"] = "debit",
                        ["ledger_account_id"] = counterparty_memo_account_id
                    },
                    new JObject 
                    {
                        ["amount"] = amountInt,
                        ["direction"] = "credit",
                        ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_memo_account_id
                    }
                }
            };

            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerTransaction);
            string ledgerTransactionId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            string ltUrl = "https:

            bool mapInserted = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTTradeGlobals.server, null, "create_securitization_trade_ledger_transaction", ledgerTransactionId, "ledger_transaction", null, "_SecuritizationTrade", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string, roundedAmount, ltUrl, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m);
            if (!mapInserted)
                Console.WriteLine("Failed to insert MT mapping for securitization trade ledger transaction.");
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\AD.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class AD
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object GetEmails(string group)
        {
            var v = UtilsLib.AD.GetGroupMemberList<string>(group,"cn","mail",true);
            return String.Join("|", v);
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object GetGenericID(string group,string ad_property_to_search, string ad_property_to_return)
        {
            var v = UtilsLib.AD.GetGroupMemberList<string>(group, ad_property_to_search, ad_property_to_return,true);
            return String.Join("|", v);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object InADGroup(string search_string,string ad_property_to_search, string group)
        {
            var groups = UtilsLib.AD.GetGroupMemberList<string>(search_string, ad_property_to_search, "memberOf",true);
            foreach (string s in groups)
            {
                if(s.ContainsIns(group))
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buckets.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public static class Buckets
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string BucketLazy(string asset_id, string field)
        {
            
            string sql = "select b.* from vBuckets b where (b.asset_id = @asset_id or b.max_id = @asset_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("bucket_" + field);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object BucketPicker(object value, string breakout,string display_format, bool return_lowest = false, string delimiter = "-")
        {
            if(null != value && value == ExcelEmpty.Value)
                return null; ;
            string sql = "select dbo.Bucket(@value,@breakout,@display_format,@return_lowest,@delimiter)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.AddParameter("@value",value);
            q.AddParameter("@breakout", breakout);
            q.AddParameter("@display_format", display_format);
            q.AddParameter("@return_lowest", return_lowest);
            q.AddParameter("delimiter",  delimiter);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<object>();
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\BadgerExport.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public class BadgerExport
    {


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GrabBadgerData()
        {
            
            string UseThisView = "vAssetsPositionEx";

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string badger_view_name_override = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "badger_view_name_override");
            if (badger_view_name_override != null)
                if (badger_view_name_override == "vAssetsEx")
                    UseThisView = badger_view_name_override;

            var before = xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
            List<string> only_assets = xlh.GetRangeArray<string>(null, "only_assets", true).ToList();
            DataTable assets = null;
            string view_override = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExist("badger_view_name_override", null);
            if(String.IsNullOrEmpty(view_override))
            {
                assets = BadgerLib.Assets.GetAllAssetInfoWithPosition(UnlockToolkit.DB, only_assets);
            }
            else if(view_override == "vAssetsExCutoff")
            {
                assets = BadgerLib.Assets.GetAllAssetInfoCutoff(UnlockToolkit.DB, only_assets);
            }
            
            
            
            

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "TABLE_ASSETS");
            xlt.DumpData(assets, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(before);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Finito!");
        }

    }
}
