--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\BillOfSale.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public class BillOfSale
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetCounterpartyTradesAsOf(DateTime asOf)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            DateTime start = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "dailyProductionAsOf");
            DataTable results = BadgerLib.Trades.GetCounterpartyTradesAsOf(server, start);

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void ResetTemplate()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.ClearRangeContents(null, new string[] { "trade_date", "settle_date", "trade_num" }, false);
            ClearCollateralFromTicket();

            new XLTable(xlh, "collat_tape").ClearAllButHeader(null);
            new XLTable(xlh, "collat_tape_exceptions").ClearAllButHeader(null);
            new XLTable(xlh, "collat_tape_exceptions").ClearAllButHeader(null);
            xlh.ClearRangeContents(null, "total_urit_portfolio");

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void TradeRecapEmail()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int trade_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "trade_num");
            DateTime trade_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "trade_date");
            DateTime settle_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "settle_date");
            double total_proceeds = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "total_proceeds");
            DataTable summary = BadgerLib.Trades.GetTradeRecapTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, trade_id);
            DataTable detail = BadgerLib.Trades.GetTradeDetail(UnlockToolkit.DB, trade_id);
            var html_summary = UtilsLib.HTMLUtils.QuickToHtml(summary, null, null, "Recap", null);
            var html_detail = UtilsLib.HTMLUtils.QuickToHtml(detail, null, null, "Collateral Detail", null);


            double summary_total = 0;
            if (summary.Rows.Count == 2)
            {
                summary_total = System.Math.Abs(System.Convert.ToDouble(summary.Rows[0][7]));
            }
            double delta = summary_total - total_proceeds;

            DataTable top = new DataTable();
            top.Columns.Add("Source", typeof(string));
            top.Columns.Add("Total_Proceeds_$", typeof(double));

            top.Rows.Add("Spreadsheet", total_proceeds);
            top.Rows.Add("Database", summary_total);
            var delta_html = UtilsLib.HTMLUtils.QuickToHtml(top, null, null, "Spreadsheet vs Database Verification", null);


            string html = delta_html.html + "<br><br>" + html_summary.html + "<br><br>" + html_detail.html;

            string subject = $"[#{trade_id}] **TRADE RECAP** | TD: {trade_date:M/d/yyyy} SD: {settle_date:M/d/yyyy} | Total Proceeds: {total_proceeds:0,000}";

            if (delta != 0)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Something looks jacked - check yo self", "Uh oh...");
            }

            UtilsLib.Mail.CreateOutlookMail(subject, html, null, null, null, null, true);


            

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void InsertNewTrades()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");
            List<string> ranges = new List<string>();
            
            ranges.Add("trades_ups_sells");
            ranges.Add("trades_urit_buys");
            ranges.Add("trades_ups_buys_from_warehouseline");
            ranges.Add("trades_warehouseline_sells_to_ups");

            foreach (string r in ranges)
            {
                xlh.CalcSingleCell(null, r);
                string sql = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, r, false);
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(sql))
                { 
                    Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
                    q.Execute(); 
                }
            }

            double size = BadgerLib.Trades.TotalPositionSize(UnlockToolkit.DB, account_id);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "total_urit_portfolio", size);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Don't forget to check the validation checks!", "DONE!");
            
        }

            xlt.UnhideAllTable();
        }

        public static string GetBaseTradeFilenameInternal(string base_file_name)
        {
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");
            int trade_num = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "trade_num");
            DateTime trade_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "trade_date");
            string account = BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountNames(server, new int[] { account_id });
            string base_file_name_final = $"{account} - {base_file_name} - #{trade_num} - {trade_date:M.dd.yyyy}";
            return base_file_name_final;
        }


        public static string GetTradeBaseFolder()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? trade_num = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("trade_num");
            string base_folder = null;
            if (null == trade_num)
                base_folder = Path.GetTempPath();
            else
                base_folder = BadgerLib.Trades.GetLocalTradeFolder(UnlockToolkit.DB, trade_num.Value);
            return base_folder;

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string GetAccountNames(string account_ids)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(account_ids))
                return "All Origination";
            List<int> accts = account_ids.Split(',').Select(n => System.Convert.ToInt32(n)).ToList();
            return BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountNames(UnlockToolkit.DB, accts);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void ProcessAndSpawnAccountingMail()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "acct_table");
            xlt.TightenUpTable("ASSET ID");
            int trade_num = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "trade_num");
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");

            DateTime settle = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "settle_date");
            
            string trade_folder = BadgerLib.Trades.GetLocalTradeFolder(server, trade_num);
            
            string filename_base = $"Accounting Breakdown - Trade #{trade_num}";
            string subject = $"Accounting Breakdown - Trade #{trade_num} - SETTLE: {settle:M/d/yyyy}";
            string filename_pdf = Path.Combine(trade_folder, filename_base + ".pdf");
            string filename_xlsx = Path.Combine(trade_folder, filename_base + ".xlsx");
            string worksheet_2_export = "Accounting";
            string full_path_pdf = xlh.SaveWorksheetAsPDF(worksheet_2_export, filename_pdf, false);
            string full_path_xls = xlh.ExportSelectedSheetStandard(false, new string[] { worksheet_2_export }, XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX, true, filename_xlsx);

            string body = $"Please find revenue breakdown for trade #{trade_num} and notify us if you have any questions.";
            string to = "billing@unlock.com;unlock@suntera.com";
            string cc = BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountContacts(server, account_id);
            string bcc = "badger@unlock.com;uam@unlock.com";
            UtilsLib.Mail.CreateOutlookMail(subject, body, new string[] { full_path_pdf, full_path_xls }, new string[] { to }, new string[] { cc }, new string[] { bcc }, true, true, null, null);

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void ParseTradePackagePDFs()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            int trade_num = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "trade_num");
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");
            DateTime trade_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "trade_date");
            string account = BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountName(UnlockToolkit.DB, account_id);
            OpenFileDialog d = new OpenFileDialog();
            d.Filter = "PDF|*.pdf";
            d.ShowDialog();
            Dictionary<int, int[]> bill_of_sale_config = new Dictionary<int, int[]>();
            bill_of_sale_config.Add(7, new int[] { 0, 1, 2, 3 });
            bill_of_sale_config.Add(8, new int[] { 0, 1, 2, 3 });
            bill_of_sale_config.Add(9, new int[] { 0, 1, 2, 3 });


            Dictionary<int, int[]> collateral_release_config = new Dictionary<int, int[]>();
            collateral_release_config.Add(7, new int[] { 4 });
            collateral_release_config.Add(8, new int[] { 4 });
            collateral_release_config.Add(9, new int[] { 4 });

            Dictionary<int, int[]> funding_notice_config = new Dictionary<int, int[]>();
            funding_notice_config.Add(7, new int[] { 5, 6 });
            funding_notice_config.Add(8, new int[] { 5, 6 });

            string file = d.FileName;
            
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(file))
                return;
            string directory = BadgerLib.Trades.GetLocalTradeFolder(UnlockToolkit.DB, trade_num);

            if (bill_of_sale_config.ContainsKey(account_id))
            {
                string bill_of_sale = Path.Combine(directory, $"{account} - Bill of Sale & Forward Sale Data Schedule - #{trade_num} - {trade_date:M.d.yyyy} - Fully Executed.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.PDFSplitMerge(file, bill_of_sale_config[account_id], bill_of_sale);
            }
            
            
            if (collateral_release_config.ContainsKey(account_id))
            {
                string collateral_release = Path.Combine(directory, $"{account} - Request for Collateral Release - #{trade_num} - Fully Executed.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.PDFSplitMerge(file, collateral_release_config[account_id], collateral_release);
            }
            if (funding_notice_config.ContainsKey(account_id))
            {
                string funding_notice = Path.Combine(directory, $"{account} - Funding Direction - #{trade_num} - Fully Executed.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.PDFSplitMerge(file, funding_notice_config[account_id], funding_notice);
            }

            FileLib.SpawnProcess(directory, true, false);

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateTradeTapes()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");
            int? trade_num = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "trade_num");
            bool trade_specific_tape = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "trade_specific_tape");
            if (!trade_specific_tape)
                trade_num = null;
            bool include_paid_off_assets = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "include_paid_off_assets");
            List<string> tapes = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<string>(null, "tapegen", true);
            string base_folder = GetTradeBaseFolder();
            string account_name = BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountName(UnlockToolkit.DB, account_id);

            foreach (string tape in tapes)
            {
                xlh.WriteStatusBar("Processing: " + tape);
                DataTable trade = BadgerLib.Trades.GetTradeTape(UnlockToolkit.DB, tape, account_id, null, trade_num, null, include_paid_off_assets);

                string sheet = $"TAPE-{tape}";
                string range = $"{sheet.Replace(" ", "_").Replace("-", "_")}_DETAIL";
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, range);
                xlt.DumpData(trade, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
                string filename_xlsx = $"{account_name} - #{trade_num} - {tape} OLD FORMAT.xlsx";
                string full_path = Path.Combine(base_folder, filename_xlsx);
                xlh.ExportSelectedSheetStandard(false, new string[] { sheet }, XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX, true, full_path);
            }

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateCollateral()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var orig_mode = xlh.GetCurrentCalcMode();
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");
            bool clear_monday_guideline_exceptions = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "clear_monday_guideline_exceptions");
            PopulateCollateralInternal(account_id, clear_monday_guideline_exceptions);

            xlh.ToggleCalcs(orig_mode);
        }

        public static void PopulateCollateralInternal(int account_id, bool clear_monday_guideline_exceptions)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            ResetTemplate();

            List<string> timeout = xlh.GetRangeList<string>(null, "timeout", true);

            

            DataTable results = BadgerLib.Trades.GetEligibleCollateral(server, account_id, null, true, false, false, false, true, false, true, null, clear_monday_guideline_exceptions);

            results.DataSet.RemoveRowsIn<string>("asset_id", timeout);


            ClearCollateralFromTicket();
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "collat_table");

            int data_row = 0;
            


            foreach (DataRow row_tbl in results.Rows)
            {
                
                XLTableRow xltr = xlt.GetXLRow(data_row + 2, true);
                xltr.Update("AGREEMENT #", row_tbl["asset_id"]);
                xltr.Update("CITY-STATE", string.Format("{0}, {1}", row_tbl["city"], row_tbl["state"]));
                xltr.Update("ZIP", row_tbl["zip"]);
                xltr.Update("STARTING HOME VALUE", row_tbl["starting_home_value"]);
                xltr.Update("INVESTMENT PMT", row_tbl["investment_payment"]);
                xltr.Update("EXCHG. RATE", row_tbl["exchange_rate"]);
                xltr.Update("COST LIMIT", row_tbl["cost_limit"]);
                xltr.Update("BASE PRICE", row_tbl["base_price"]);
                
                xltr.Update("DOC STATUS", row_tbl["cert_status"]);
                xltr.Update("CRITICAL NOTE", row_tbl["critical_note"]);
                xltr.Update("FUNDING Source", row_tbl["funding_source"]);
                xltr.Update("JOURNAL", row_tbl["journal_account"]);
                data_row++;
            }

            DateTime trade_date = DateTime.Today.GetNextWeekday(DayOfWeek.Tuesday);
            DateTime settle_date = DateTime.Today.GetNextWeekday(DayOfWeek.Thursday);
            int next_trade_num = NextTradeNum(server);

            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime d = new UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime(DateTime.Today);
            d.AddBusinessDays(2);

            xlh.WriteRange(null, "trade_date", DateTime.Today);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "settle_date", DateTime.Today.AddDays(2));
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "settle_date", d.Date);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "trade_num", next_trade_num);

            xlt.TightenUpTable("AGREEMENT #");

            PopulateTapeAndExceptions();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateTapeAndExceptions()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");

            DataTable eligible_collat = BadgerLib.Trades.GetEligibleCollateral(server, account_id, null, true, false, false, false, true, false, false, null, true);
            DataTable exceptions = BadgerLib.Trades.GetEligibleCollateral(server, account_id, null, true, false, false, false, false, true, false, null, true);
            List<string> timeout = xlh.GetRangeList<string>(null, "timeout", true);
            eligible_collat.DataSet.RemoveRowsIn<string>("asset_id", timeout);
            exceptions.DataSet.RemoveRowsIn<string>("asset_id", timeout);

            

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "collat_tape");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.WriteRange(eligible_collat);

            XLTable xlte = new XLTable(xlh, "collat_tape_exceptions");
            xlte.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlte.WriteRange(exceptions);
        }

        public static int NextTradeNum(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select max(trade_id)+1 from vTrades";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
        }
    }
}

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CashMoneyLoadCostlyTrades()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Loading Problematic Trades");
            XLTable xlt = xlh.XLTable("trades_costly");
            DataTable trades = BadgerLib.Trades.GetCostlyTrades(UnlockToolkit.DB, true, true, true, true);
            xlt.ClearColumnsExcept("MONEY_GIVEN_UP");
            xlt.DumpData(trades, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("ticket_id");
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Costly Trades", false);
            xlh.WriteStatusBar(null);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CashMoney_DoAll()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("[Cash Management] Run all starting...");
            try
            {
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);

                
                CashMoney_LoadBanking();

                
                CashMoney_LoadTrades();
                CashMoney_LoadRepurchases();
                CashMoney_LoadProtectiveAdvances();
                CashMoney_GetMonthlySettlements();

                
                CashMoney_GetBalanceSheetPositions();

                
                CashMoney_LoadClosing();

                
                CashMoney_GetCashManagementSummaryData();

                
                
                
                
                

                xlh.WriteStatusBar("[Cash Management] Run all completed");
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show(n.Message + n.StackTrace, "Oops...");
                xlh.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("[Cash Management] Run All failed - Error: {0}", n.Message));
            }
            finally
            {
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);
            }

        }

        public static void CashMoney_LoadTransactions()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Loading Individual Transactions");
            var accts = new List<long>(new long[] { 80008164388, 80009175797, 80009175847 });
            DataTable trans = BadgerLib.Banking.GetLargeNonClearEdgeTransactions(UnlockToolkit.DB, accts, 5000);
            XLTable tbl_trans = new XLTable(xlh, "bank_trans_all");
            tbl_trans.DumpData(trans.AsEnumerable().Take(tbl_trans.TotalRowsInTable-1).CopyToDataTable(), true, null, null);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CashMoney_LoadClosing()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Loading Customer Pipeline");
            int trade_date = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "pipeline_trade_date");
            int settle_date = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "pipeline_settle_date");
            DataTable pipeline = BadgerLib.Closing.GetClosingPipeline(UnlockToolkit.DB, trade_date,settle_date);
            XLTable xlt = xlh.XLTable("closing_pipeline");
            xlt.DumpData(pipeline, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);


            BadgerLib.Banking.ClearBorrowingBaseQuery(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            
            double? funded_not_originated = BadgerLib.Banking.FundedNotOriginated(UnlockToolkit.DB,true);
            
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "funded_not_originated", funded_not_originated);

            double? sold_not_funded = BadgerLib.Banking.SoldNotFunded(UnlockToolkit.DB, true);
            
            if (xlh.RangeExists("sold_not_funded"))
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "sold_not_funded", sold_not_funded);

            double? unlock_unsold_inv = BadgerLib.Banking.OriginatedNotSold(UnlockToolkit.DB, true);
            
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "unlock_unsold_inv", unlock_unsold_inv);

            double? originated_not_funded = BadgerLib.Banking.OriginatedNotFunded(UnlockToolkit.DB, true);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "originated_not_funded", originated_not_funded);

            
            double? sold_not_settled = BadgerLib.Banking.SoldNotSettled(UnlockToolkit.DB, true);
            if(xlh.RangeExists("unlock_sold_not_settled_not_including_today"))
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "unlock_sold_not_settled_not_including_today", sold_not_settled);
            xlh.WriteStatusBar(null);

            double? monthly_origination = BadgerLib.Closing.HistoricalOrigination(UnlockToolkit.DB, DateTime.Today.AddMonths(-1), DateTime.Today);
            if (xlh.RangeExists("assumed_monthly_production"))
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "assumed_monthly_production", monthly_origination);

            double? monthly_origination_prior = BadgerLib.Closing.HistoricalOrigination(UnlockToolkit.DB, DateTime.Today.AddMonths(-2), DateTime.Today.AddMonths(-1));
            if (xlh.RangeExists("assumed_monthly_production_prior"))
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "assumed_monthly_production_prior", monthly_origination_prior);
            xlh.WriteStatusBar(null);

            double? all_production = BadgerLib.Closing.HistoricalOrigination(UnlockToolkit.DB, DateTime.Today.AddMonths(-100), DateTime.Today);
            if (xlh.RangeExists("all_time_production"))
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "all_time_production", all_production);

        }

    }
}

namespace Unlock_Toolkit.Buttons
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;

    public class Collections
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetFullTape()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;

            DateTime cutOff = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "period_end");
            DateTime periodStart = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "period_start");
            string account = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "account");

            DataTable results = BadgerLib.InvestorReporting.GetFullUnifiedTape(server, cutOff);

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "tape_all_assets");
            xlt.DumpData(results, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            #region Termination Data

            XLTable xltTerminations = new XLTable(xlh, "all_termination_data");

            DataTable resultsTerminated = results.AsEnumerable().Where(
                  row => row.Field<DateTime?>("final_disposition_date") != null
                  && row.Field<DateTime>("final_disposition_date") >= periodStart
                  && row.Field<DateTime>("final_disposition_date") <= cutOff)
                .OrderBy(row => row.Field<DateTime>("final_disposition_date"))
                .CopyToDataTable();

            xltTerminations.DumpData(resultsTerminated, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xltTerminations.TightenUpTable("max_id");

            #endregion

            #region Default + Delinquency Data

            XLTable xltDefaults = new XLTable(xlh, "defaults_all_data");

            DataTable resultsDefaults = results.AsEnumerable()
                .Where(row => row.Field<string>("combined_default_type") != null)
                .OrderBy(row => row.Field<string>("account"))
                .CopyToDataTable();

            DataTable resultsDefaultsSplit = new DataTable();
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("account", resultsDefaults.Columns["account"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("max_id", resultsDefaults.Columns["max_id"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("default_type", resultsDefaults.Columns["combined_default_type"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("default_subtype", resultsDefaults.Columns["combined_default_subtype"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("default_date", typeof(DateTime));
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("cure_date", resultsDefaults.Columns["combined_cure_dates"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("effective_date", resultsDefaults.Columns["effective_date"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("investment_payment_orig", resultsDefaults.Columns["investment_payment_orig"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("exercise_value_at_termination", resultsDefaults.Columns["exercise_value_at_termination"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("starting_home_value", resultsDefaults.Columns["starting_home_value"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("state", resultsDefaults.Columns["state"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("default_id", resultsDefaults.Columns["combined_default_ids"].DataType);
            resultsDefaultsSplit.Columns.Add("reporting_type", resultsDefaults.Columns["combined_default_reporting_type"].DataType);

            foreach (DataRow row in resultsDefaults.Rows)
            {
                string assetId = resultsDefaults.Columns.Contains("asset_id") ? row["asset_id"].ToString() : null;

                string[] defaultTypes = (row["combined_default_type"] == DBNull.Value || row["combined_default_type"] == null)
                    ? new string[] { }
                    : row["combined_default_type"].ToString().Split(new[] { '|' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
                string[] defaultsubTypes = (row["combined_default_subtype"] == DBNull.Value || row["combined_default_subtype"] == null)
                    ? new string[] { }
                    : row["combined_default_subtype"].ToString().Split(new[] { '|' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
                string[] defaultDates = (row["combined_default_dates"] == DBNull.Value || row["combined_default_dates"] == null)
                    ? new string[] { }
                    : row["combined_default_dates"].ToString().Split(new[] { '|' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
                string[] defaultIds = (row["combined_default_ids"] == DBNull.Value || row["combined_default_ids"] == null)
                    ? new string[] { }
                    : row["combined_default_ids"].ToString().Split(new[] { '|' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
                string[] cureDates = (row["combined_cure_dates"] == DBNull.Value || row["combined_cure_dates"] == null)
                    ? null
                    : row["combined_cure_dates"].ToString().Split(new[] { '|' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
                string[] defaultReportingTypes = (row["combined_default_reporting_type"] == DBNull.Value || row["combined_default_reporting_type"] == null)
                    ? new string[] { }
                    : row["combined_default_reporting_type"].ToString().Split(new[] { '|' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);

                if (defaultTypes.Length != defaultDates.Length)
                {
                    throw new Exception("Mismatch between number of default types and dates.");
                }

                for (int i = 0; i < defaultTypes.Length; i++)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        DataRow newRow = resultsDefaultsSplit.NewRow();
                        object repurchase = resultsDefaults.Columns.Contains("repurchase_account") ? row["repurchase_account"] : null;
                        newRow["account"] = (repurchase != null && repurchase != DBNull.Value && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(repurchase.ToString())) ? repurchase : row["account"];
                        newRow["max_id"] = row["max_id"];
                        newRow["default_id"] = defaultIds.Length > i ? (object)defaultIds[i].Trim() : DBNull.Value;
                        newRow["default_type"] = defaultTypes[i].Trim();
                        newRow["default_subtype"] = defaultsubTypes.Length > i ? (object)defaultsubTypes[i].Trim() : DBNull.Value;
                        newRow["reporting_type"] = defaultReportingTypes.Length > i ? (object)defaultReportingTypes[i].Trim() : DBNull.Value;
                        newRow["default_date"] = DateTime.Parse(defaultDates[i].Trim());
                        newRow["cure_date"] = (cureDates != null && cureDates.Length > i) ? (object)DateTime.Parse(cureDates[i].Trim()) : DBNull.Value;
                        newRow["effective_date"] = row["effective_date"];
                        newRow["investment_payment_orig"] = row["investment_payment_orig"];
                        newRow["exercise_value_at_termination"] = row["exercise_value_at_termination"];
                        newRow["starting_home_value"] = row["starting_home_value"];
                        newRow["state"] = row["state"];
                        resultsDefaultsSplit.Rows.Add(newRow);
                    }
                    catch (Exception ex)
                    {
                        string context = $"Error in defaults split loop. Index={i}, Account='{row["account"]}', MaxId='{row["max_id"]}', " +
                                         $"Types={defaultTypes.Length}, SubTypes={defaultsubTypes.Length}, Dates={defaultDates.Length}, " +
                                         $"Ids={defaultIds.Length}, CureDates={(cureDates == null ? 0 : cureDates.Length)}, ReportingTypes={defaultReportingTypes.Length}.";
                        throw new InvalidOperationException(context, ex);
                    }
                }
            }

            
            for (int i = resultsDefaultsSplit.Rows.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
            {
                var rt = resultsDefaultsSplit.Rows[i].Field<string>("reporting_type");
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(rt)) { resultsDefaultsSplit.Rows.RemoveAt(i); }
            }

            DataTable resultsDefaultsSplitSorted;
            if (resultsDefaultsSplit.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                resultsDefaultsSplitSorted = resultsDefaultsSplit.AsEnumerable()
                    .OrderBy(r => r.Field<string>("account"))
                    .ThenBy(r => r.Field<string>("reporting_type"))
                    .ThenBy(r => r.IsNull("default_date") ? DateTime.MaxValue : r.Field<DateTime>("default_date"))
                    .CopyToDataTable();
            }
            else
            {
                resultsDefaultsSplitSorted = resultsDefaultsSplit.Clone();
            }

            xltDefaults.DumpData(resultsDefaultsSplitSorted, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xltDefaults.TightenUpTable("account");

            #endregion

            #region Expenses Data

            
            
            
            

            
            XLTable xltReimbursable = new XLTable(xlh, "expenses_reimbursable_data");
            DataTable reimbursable = BuildReimbursableExpenses(results);
            xltReimbursable.DumpData(reimbursable, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xltReimbursable.TightenUpTable("account");

            #endregion
            Utils.GenericHideUnhideSheets();
            TightenAllCollectionsTables();
        }

        
        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Returns CPR remit metrics for the given account, sorted by latest Period End Date descending.")]
        public static object GetCPRRemitsForAccount()
        {
            try
            {
                
                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                string selected_account = null;
                try { selected_account = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "selected_account"); } catch {  }

                string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
                string sql = @"SELECT * FROM CPR_Remits WHERE Account = @account ORDER BY PeriodEndDate DESC";

                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@account", selected_account);
                DataTable CPRdt = q.ExecuteTable();
                XLTable xltCPRRemits = new XLTable(xlh, "CPR_Remits");
                xltCPRRemits.ClearAllButHeader(1);
                xltCPRRemits.DumpData(CPRdt, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
                return null;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                
                return new object[,] { { "Error: " + ex.Message } };
            }
        }
        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Fixes the Position Tape date in Bills-of-Sale VLOOKUP formulas (cols AB & AC) to match the reporting-month folder.")]
        public static void UpdateBillsOfSalePositionTapeLinks()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            
            var xlApp = (Application)ExcelDnaUtil.Application;
            Workbook wb = xlApp.ActiveWorkbook;

            string workbookDir = Path.GetDirectoryName(wb.FullName);
            string folderName  = Path.GetFileName(workbookDir); 

            if (folderName == null || folderName.Length != 6 || !int.TryParse(folderName, out _))
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"Expected the workbook to reside in a 6-digit YYYYMM folder, but found: '{folderName}'. " +
                    "Please save the workbook inside its monthly reporting folder before running this.");

            int year  = int.Parse(folderName.Substring(0, 4));
            int month = int.Parse(folderName.Substring(4, 2));

            
            DateTime lastDay    = new DateTime(year, month, DateTime.DaysInMonth(year, month));
            string   lastDayStr = lastDay.ToString("yyyy.MM.dd");                       
            string   newTapeFile = $"UNLOK 2024-1 - Position Tape - {lastDayStr}.xlsx"; 

            
            
            var tapeDateRx = new System.Text.RegularExpressions.Regex(
                @"UNLOK 2024-1 - Position Tape - \d{4}\.\d{2}\.\d{2}\.xlsx");

            
            var folderRx = new System.Text.RegularExpressions.Regex(
                @"(?<=/Monthly Reporting/)\d{6}(?=/)");

            
            const string targetSheet = "Bills of Sale - UNLOK";
            Worksheet ws = null;
            foreach (Worksheet s in wb.Worksheets)
            {
                if (string.Equals(s.Name, targetSheet, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                { ws = s; break; }
            }
            if (ws == null)
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"Sheet '{targetSheet}' was not found in the active workbook.");

            
            int[] targetCols = { 28, 29 }; 
            int firstRow     = 1;
            int lastRow      = ws.UsedRange.Row + ws.UsedRange.Rows.Count - 1;
            int updatedCount = 0;

            foreach (int col in targetCols)
            {
                Range colRange = ws.Range[ws.Cells[firstRow, col], ws.Cells[lastRow, col]];
                foreach (Range cell in colRange)
                {
                    string formula = cell.Formula as string;
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(formula) || !formula.Contains("VLOOKUP"))
                        continue;

                    string updated = tapeDateRx.Replace(formula, newTapeFile);
                    updated        = folderRx.Replace(updated, folderName);

                    if (updated != formula)
                    {
                        cell.Formula = updated;
                        updatedCount++;
                    }
                }
            }

            xlh.WriteStatusBar(
                $"Updated {updatedCount} VLOOKUP formula(s) in '{targetSheet}' (cols AB & AC) " +
                $"\u2192 Position Tape: {newTapeFile}");
        }

        private static DataTable SplitExpenses(DataTable results)
        {
            
            
            if (!results.Columns.Contains("combined_expense_ids") &&
                !results.Columns.Contains("combined_expense_types") &&
                !results.Columns.Contains("combined_expense_dates"))
            {
                
                DataTable empty = new DataTable();
                empty.Columns.Add("account", typeof(string));
                empty.Columns.Add("max_id", typeof(object));
                empty.Columns.Add("expense_id", typeof(string));
                empty.Columns.Add("expense_type", typeof(string));
                empty.Columns.Add("vendor_name", typeof(string));
                empty.Columns.Add("expense_date", typeof(DateTime));
                empty.Columns.Add("expense_amount", typeof(decimal));
                empty.Columns.Add("invoice_file", typeof(string));
                return empty;
            }

            
            var rowsWithExpenses = results.AsEnumerable()
                .Where(r => (r["combined_expense_ids"] != DBNull.Value && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(global::System.Convert.ToString(r["combined_expense_ids"]))) ||
                            (r["combined_expense_types"] != DBNull.Value && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(global::System.Convert.ToString(r["combined_expense_types"]))))

                .ToList();

            DataTable split = new DataTable();
            
            split.Columns.Add("account", results.Columns.Contains("account") ? results.Columns["account"].DataType : typeof(string));
            split.Columns.Add("max_id", results.Columns.Contains("max_id") ? results.Columns["max_id"].DataType : typeof(object));
            split.Columns.Add("expense_id", typeof(string));
            split.Columns.Add("expense_type", typeof(string));
            split.Columns.Add("vendor_name", typeof(string));
            split.Columns.Add("expense_date", typeof(DateTime));
            split.Columns.Add("expense_amount", typeof(decimal));
            split.Columns.Add("invoice_file", typeof(string));

            foreach (var row in rowsWithExpenses)
            {
                string[] expenseIds = RowSplit(row, "combined_expense_ids");
                string[] expenseTypes = RowSplit(row, "combined_expense_types");
                string[] vendorNames = RowSplit(row, "combined_vendor_names");
                string[] expenseDates = RowSplit(row, "combined_expense_dates");
                string[] expenseAmounts = RowSplit(row, "combined_expense_amounts");
                string[] invoiceFiles = RowSplit(row, "combined_invoice_files");

                
                if (expenseTypes.Length != expenseDates.Length)
                {
                    throw new Exception("Mismatch between number of expense types and dates.");
                }

                int lineCount = Math.Max(expenseTypes.Length, Math.Max(expenseIds.Length, expenseDates.Length));
                for (int i = 0; i < lineCount; i++)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        DataRow nr = split.NewRow();
                        nr["account"] = results.Columns.Contains("account") ? row["account"] : DBNull.Value;
                        nr["max_id"] = results.Columns.Contains("max_id") ? row["max_id"] : DBNull.Value;
                        nr["expense_id"] = expenseIds.Length > i ? expenseIds[i].Trim() : null;
                        nr["expense_type"] = expenseTypes.Length > i ? expenseTypes[i].Trim() : null;
                        nr["vendor_name"] = vendorNames.Length > i ? vendorNames[i].Trim() : null;
                        nr["invoice_file"] = invoiceFiles.Length > i ? invoiceFiles[i].Trim() : null;

                        if (expenseDates.Length > i && DateTime.TryParse(expenseDates[i].Trim(), out DateTime dt))
                        {
                            nr["expense_date"] = dt;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            nr["expense_date"] = DBNull.Value;
                        }

                        if (expenseAmounts.Length > i && decimal.TryParse(expenseAmounts[i].Trim(), NumberStyles.Any, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out decimal amt))
                        {
                            nr["expense_amount"] = amt;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            nr["expense_amount"] = DBNull.Value;
                        }

                        split.Rows.Add(nr);
                    }
                    catch (Exception ex)
                    {
                        string context = $"Error splitting expenses. Index={i}, Account='{(results.Columns.Contains("account") ? row["account"] : "")}', MaxId='{(results.Columns.Contains("max_id") ? row["max_id"] : "")}', " +
                                         $"Ids={expenseIds.Length}, Types={expenseTypes.Length}, Vendors={vendorNames.Length}, Dates={expenseDates.Length}, Amounts={expenseAmounts.Length}, Files={invoiceFiles.Length}.";
                        throw new InvalidOperationException(context, ex);
                    }
                }
            }

            
            for (int i = split.Rows.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
            {
                bool remove = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(split.Rows[i].Field<string>("expense_type")) &&
                              split.Rows[i].IsNull("expense_amount") &&
                              split.Rows[i].IsNull("expense_date");
                if (remove) split.Rows.RemoveAt(i);
            }

            DataTable sorted;
            if (split.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                sorted = split.AsEnumerable()
                    .OrderBy(r => r.Field<string>("account"))
                    .ThenBy(r => r.IsNull("expense_date") ? DateTime.MaxValue : r.Field<DateTime>("expense_date"))
                    .CopyToDataTable();
            }
            else
            {
                sorted = split.Clone();
            }
            return sorted;
        }

        private static DataTable BuildReimbursableExpenses(DataTable results)
        {
            
            string[] columnsNeeded = new[]
            {
                "reimbursable_expenses_uoo_open",
                "reimbursable_expenses_uoo_cumulative",
                "reimbursable_expenses_uoo_repaid_to_trust_cumulative",
                "reimbursable_expenses_admin_advance_open",
                "reimbursable_expenses_admin_advance_cumulative",
                "reimbursable_expenses_extraordinary_advance_open",
                "reimbursable_expenses_extraordinary_advance_cumulative"
            };

            DataTable dt = new DataTable();
            
            dt.Columns.Add("account", results.Columns.Contains("account") ? results.Columns["account"].DataType : typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("max_id", results.Columns.Contains("max_id") ? results.Columns["max_id"].DataType : typeof(object));

            foreach (var colName in columnsNeeded)
            {
                Type t = typeof(object);
                if (results.Columns.Contains(colName))
                    t = results.Columns[colName].DataType;
                dt.Columns.Add(colName, t);
            }

            IEnumerable<DataRow> sourceRows = results.AsEnumerable();
            
            sourceRows = sourceRows.Where(r => columnsNeeded.Any(c =>
            {
                if (!results.Columns.Contains(c)) return false;
                var val = r[c];
                if (val == null || val == DBNull.Value) return false;
                var s = val.ToString();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s)) return false;
                
                return true;
            }));

            if (!sourceRows.Any())
            {
                
                return dt;
            }

            foreach (var r in sourceRows)
            {
                var nr = dt.NewRow();
                nr["account"] = results.Columns.Contains("account") ? r["account"] : DBNull.Value;
                nr["max_id"] = results.Columns.Contains("max_id") ? r["max_id"] : DBNull.Value;
                foreach (var colName in columnsNeeded)
                {
                    if (results.Columns.Contains(colName))
                        nr[colName] = r[colName];
                    else
                        nr[colName] = DBNull.Value;
                }
                dt.Rows.Add(nr);
            }

            
            DataTable sorted;
            try
            {
                sorted = dt.AsEnumerable()
                    .OrderBy(r => r.Field<string>("account"))
                    .ThenBy(r => r["max_id"]) 
                    .CopyToDataTable();
            }
            catch
            {
                sorted = dt; 
            }

            return sorted;
        }

        private static string[] RowSplit(DataRow row, string columnName)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(columnName)) return new string[0];
            object val = row[columnName];
            if (val == DBNull.Value || val == null) return new string[0];
            string s = val.ToString();
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s)) return new string[0];
            return s.Split(new[] { '|' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void TightenAllCollectionsTables()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            Dictionary<string, string> dctTables = new Dictionary<string, string>
            {
                { "investor_terminations_data", "max_id" },
                { "investor_default_data", "max_id" },
            };

            foreach (string table in dctTables.Keys)
            {
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, table);
                xlt.TightenUpTable(dctTables[table]);
            }
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\DebtManagement.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;

    public class DebtManagement
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetTradeLineMapping()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            

            int paymentThreshold = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "paymentThreshold");
            int balanceThreshold = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "balanceThreshold");
            int openDateThreshold = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "openDateThreshold");
            bool updateMappings = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "updateMappings");


            List<string> includeOnlyAssets = new List<string>();
            
            

            if(updateMappings)
            {
                var msg = XtraMessageBox.Show("This will update the mappings in the database. Are you sure you want to continue?", "Warning", System.Windows.Forms.MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                if (msg.ToString() == "No")
                    return;

            }


            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Starting Tradeline mapping");

            DataSet tradeLineMappings = Debt.TradeLineMapping(UnlockToolkit.DB, paymentThreshold, balanceThreshold, openDateThreshold, updateMappings, includeOnlyAssets);

            
            DataTable mappingSummary = tradeLineMappings.Tables[0];
            DataTable mappingThresholds = tradeLineMappings.Tables[2];      
            DataTable mappingLastCreditDate = tradeLineMappings.Tables[4];  
            DataTable mappingDuplicates = tradeLineMappings.Tables[5];      
            DataTable proposedMappings = tradeLineMappings.Tables[7];       

            XLTable xla = xlh.XLTable("proposedMappings");
            xla.DumpData(proposedMappings, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlh.WriteStatusBar(null);
        }
    }
}

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CatapultIntoBadger()
        {
            
            
            var dr = System.Windows.Forms.MessageBox.Show("You sure you want to inhale this fellow?", "Question...", System.Windows.Forms.MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
            if (dr != System.Windows.Forms.DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                return;
            }
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);

            string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_agreement_num").Trim();




            bool exists_in_closing = BadgerLib.Closing.ClosingExists(UnlockToolkit.DB,asset_id);
            if(!exists_in_closing)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Asset Doesn't existing in Closing Table - Tell Dan");
                return;
            }

            bool exists = BadgerLib.Assets.AssetExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (!exists)
            {
                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel,UnlockToolkit.DB,"uam_insert_1");
            }

            string app_email = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_applicant_1_email", false);
            bool applicant_exists = BadgerLib.Applicants.ApplicantExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, app_email);
            xlh.ClearRangeContents(null, "uam_applicant_1,uam_applicant_2");
            if (!applicant_exists)
            {
                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_2");



                int last_applicant = BadgerLib.Applicants.LastApplicantId(UnlockToolkit.DB);
                string sql_2 = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_insert_2", false);

                int num_applicants = 1;
                if (File.Exists(sql_2))
                    num_applicants = File.ReadAllText(sql_2).Split("insert").Length - 1;

                for (int i = 0; i != num_applicants; i++)
                {
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "uam_applicant_" + (i + 1), last_applicant - num_applicants + i + 1);
                }
            }

            bool map_exists = BadgerLib.Applicants.MapExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (!map_exists)
            {
                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_3");
            }

            bool mortgages_exist = BadgerLib.Debt.MortgagesExist(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (!mortgages_exist)
            {
                string active_lender = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_lender");
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(active_lender))
                    BadgerLib.Lenders.GetLenderId(UnlockToolkit.DB, true, active_lender, 2);

                string active_lender_2 = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_lender_2");
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(active_lender_2))
                    BadgerLib.Lenders.GetLenderId(UnlockToolkit.DB, true, active_lender_2, 2);


                
                XLTable lt = new XLTable(xlh, "uam_lenders");
                    
                DataTable lenders = BadgerLib.Lenders.GetLenderLookupTable(UnlockToolkit.DB);
                
                lt.DumpData(lenders, true, null);

                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_4");
            }

            bool underwriting_exists = BadgerLib.Underwriting.Exists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (!underwriting_exists)
            {
                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_5");
            }


            
            
            
            
            

            bool prop_info_exists = BadgerLib.PropertyInfo.PropertyInfoExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (!prop_info_exists)
            {
                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_7");
            }

            bool payoffs_exist = BadgerLib.Payoffs.PayoffsExist(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (!payoffs_exist)
            {
                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_8");
            }


            bool valuations_exist = BadgerLib.Valuations.ValuationsExistHack(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (!valuations_exist)
            {
                BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_9");
            }

        

        
        
        CopyFolders:
            {
                
                
                string folder_name = BadgerControls.Helpers.TransferAssetFoldersUPS_UAM(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id, null, false);
                string folder_name_only = Path.GetFileName(folder_name);
                BadgerLib.Assets.WriteGenericAssetElement(UnlockToolkit.DB, "Assets", "folder_name_ups", folder_name_only, "id", asset_id);
            }

            BadgerLib.Files.NormalizeAssetDirectory(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id,false);

            AddUAMTasksInternal(false);

            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!");
        }

        public static string GetLabelFromAddress(string address_raw)
        {
            if (null == address_raw)
                return null;
            string address = address_raw.Trim();
            address = address.Replace(".", "");
            address = address.Replace("  ", " ");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("CT", "C");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("COURT", "C");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("STREET", "S");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("DRIVE", "D");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("TRAIL", "TR");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("CIRCLE", "CIR");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("POINT", "PT");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("ROAD", "R");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("LN", "L");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("LANE", "L");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("EAST", "E");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("WEST", "W");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("NORTH", "N");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("SOUTH", "S");

            string label = BadgerLib.Pipeline.NameFromAddressIgnoreDupes(UnlockToolkit.DB, address.Trim(),true);
            if (null == label)
                label = BadgerLib.Pipeline.NameFromAddressIgnoreDupes(UnlockToolkit.DB, address_raw.Trim(), true);
            return label;
        }

    }
}

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CheckForApplicants()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            long max_id = xlh.GetRange<long>(null, "max_id_to_import");

            xlh.WriteRange(null, "Start_Time", DateTime.Now);
            MaxLib.Utils.Max_Update_Application_Data(max_id.ToString(), UnlockToolkit.DB_SNOWFLAKE, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "End_Time", DateTime.Now);
            int Exists = 0;

            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            string sql = "exec sp_MAX_Badger_Import_Check_For_Applicant @max_id, @p_Exists output, 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
            q.AddParameter("@p_Exists|OUT", Exists);
            DataTable dt = q.ExecuteTable();

            int new_Exists = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@p_Exists"]);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "applicant_exists", "");
            if (new_Exists > 0)
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "applicant_exists", "Applicant exists");
            else
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "applicant_exists", "New Applicant");

            XLTable xlt_applicant_status = new XLTable(xlh, "applicant_status");
            xlt_applicant_status.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt_applicant_status.DumpData(dt, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            
            
            
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void AddToBadger()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            long max_id = xlh.GetRange<long>(null, "max_id_to_import");

            bool exists_in_closing = BadgerLib.Closing.ClosingExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, max_id.ToString());

            if (exists_in_closing)
            {
                
                DataTable dtMAX_Badger_Import_All_dt = MaxLib.Utils.AddToBadger(UnlockToolkit.DB, max_id.ToString(), System.Environment.UserName.ToString());

                
                string folder_name = BadgerControls.Helpers.TransferAssetFoldersUPS_UAM(UnlockToolkit.DB, max_id.ToString(), null, false);
                string folder_name_only = Path.GetFileName(folder_name);

                
                BadgerLib.Assets.WriteGenericAssetElement(UnlockToolkit.DB, "Assets", "folder_name_ups", folder_name_only, "id", max_id.ToString());

                BadgerLib.Files.NormalizeAssetDirectory(UnlockToolkit.DB, max_id.ToString(), false);

                
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Asset Folder " + folder_name_only+" has been added");

            }
            else
            {
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "asset_in_closing_table", "No");
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Asset Doesn't existing in Closing Table - Tell Dan");
            }
        }

        public static string GetLabelFromAddress(string address_raw)
        {
            if (null == address_raw)
                return null;
            string address = address_raw.Trim();
            address = address.Replace(".", "");
            address = address.Replace("  ", " ");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("CT", "C");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("COURT", "C");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("STREET", "S");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("DRIVE", "D");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("TRAIL", "TR");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("CIRCLE", "CIR");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("POINT", "PT");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("ROAD", "R");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("LN", "L");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("LANE", "L");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("EAST", "E");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("WEST", "W");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("NORTH", "N");
            address = address.ToUpper().Replace("SOUTH", "S");

            string label = BadgerLib.Pipeline.NameFromAddressIgnoreDupes(UnlockToolkit.DB, address.Trim(),true);
            if (null == label)
                label = BadgerLib.Pipeline.NameFromAddressIgnoreDupes(UnlockToolkit.DB, address_raw.Trim(), true);
            return label;
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\FundingBudget.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public class FundingBudget
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void FundingBudget_DoAll()
        {

            try
            {
                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);
                var summary_task = Task.Run(() => BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetPipelineSummary(UnlockToolkit.DB));
                var last_pipeline_update_task = Task.Run(() => BadgerLib.Pipeline.LastPipelineUpdate(UnlockToolkit.DB));
                xlh.WriteStatusBar("Loading Pending Scheduling");

                Unlock_Toolkit.CashMoney.CashMoney_LoadClosing();

                var include = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<string>(null, "pipeline_include", true);
                var pipeline_task = Task.Run(() => BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetPipeline(UnlockToolkit.DB, include));


                xlh.WriteStatusBar("Loading Trades");
                DataTable trades = BadgerLib.Trades.GetTradeSummary(UnlockToolkit.DB);
                DataTable top5 = trades.Rows.Cast<System.Data.DataRow>().Take(5).CopyToDataTable();
                XLTable xl_trades = xlh.XLTable("funding_trades");

                xl_trades.DumpData(top5, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
                

                xlh.WriteStatusBar("Loading Bank Balance");
                double cash = BankLib.Accounts.GetUnlockBankBalance(UnlockToolkit.DB);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "unlock_cash", cash);

                xlh.WriteStatusBar("Getting most stale bank load");
                DateTime earliest_load = BankLib.Accounts.GetUnlockEarliestLoad(UnlockToolkit.DB);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "earliest_bank_load", earliest_load.AddHours(-4));

                xlh.WriteStatusBar("Getting Pipeline Last Update Time");

                xlh.WriteRange(null, "last_pipeline_update", last_pipeline_update_task.Result.AddHours(3));


                var s_include = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<string>(null, "summary_stages", true);
                summary_task.Result.FilterRowsNotIn<string>("sub_stage", s_include);
                var xls = new XLTable(xlh, "pipeline_summary");
                xls.DumpData(summary_task.Result, true, null, null);
                

                XLTable xlp = xlh.XLTable("customer_pipeline");
                xlp.DumpData(pipeline_task.Result, true, null, null);
                xlh.WriteStatusBar("Loading Pipeline Summary");

                double trade_hitting_today = BadgerLib.Trades.TradeProceedsHitToday(UnlockToolkit.DB);
                if (xlh.RangeExists("money_hit"))
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "money_hit", trade_hitting_today);

                xlh.WriteStatusBar(null);
            }catch (Exception n)
            {
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n, null, null, null);
            }
        }

    }
}

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class InvestorReporting
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PullAssets()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            List<int> account_ids = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id", false).ToListSingle<int>();
            DateTime begin_coll = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "begin_coll");
            DateTime end_coll = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "end_coll");
            DateTime hpi_asof = BadgerLib.HPI.GetLatestAsOf(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "hpi_asof ", hpi_asof);

            DataSet assets = BadgerLib.InvestorReporting.GetValuationTables(UnlockToolkit.DB, account_ids, begin_coll, end_coll);

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "asset_inputs");
            xlt.DumpData(assets.Tables[0], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar, null);

            XLTable xlo = new XLTable(xlh, "asset_output_ids");
            xlo.DumpData(assets.Tables[2], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar, null);

            XLTable xlterms = new XLTable(xlh, "asset_terminations");
            xlterms.DumpData(assets.Tables[1], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar, null);
            

            XLTable xl_coll = new XLTable(xlh, "collections");
            xl_coll.DumpData(assets.Tables[3], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar, null);
            
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void ResetValuationSheet()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            new XLTable(xlh, "asset_inputs").ClearAllButHeader(1);
            new XLTable(xlh, "asset_output_ids").ClearAllButHeader(1);
            new XLTable(xlh, "asset_terminations").ClearAllButHeader(1);
            new XLTable(xlh, "collections").ClearAllButHeader(1);
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SaveandSpawnValuationPDF()
        {


            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");
            string account_name = BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountName(UnlockToolkit.DB, account_id);
            DateTime end_coll = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "end_coll");
            string filename = $"{account_name} - Performance Report - {end_coll:M.d.yyyy}";
            

            CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel, "Performance", filename, false, null);
        }

    }

namespace Unlock_Toolkit

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void LoadPricingPortfolio()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "pricer_account_id");
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "pricing_all");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);

            DataTable assets = BadgerLib.Portfolio.GetFullPortfolioTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, account_id);
            
            ETA eta = new ETA(assets.Rows.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            int i = 0;
            foreach (var asset in assets.Rows)
            {
                DataRow dr = assets.Rows[i];
                XLTableRow row = xlt.GetXLRow(i + 2);
                row.Update("asset_id", dr["asset_id"]);
                row.Update("effective_date", dr["effective_date"]);
                row.Update("cost_limit", dr["cost_limit"]);
                row.Update("cost_limit_basis", dr["cost_limit_basis"]);
                row.Update("buyout_active_date", dr["buyout_active_date"]);
                row.Update("investment_payment", dr["investment_payment"]);
                row.Update("exchange_rate", dr["exchange_rate"]);
                row.Update("starting_home_value", dr["starting_home_value"]);
                row.Update("home_value_hpi_latest", dr["home_value_hpi_latest"]);
                row.Update("buyout_active_date", dr["buyout_active_date"]);
                row.Update("price", System.Convert.ToDouble(dr["price"]) / 100.0);
                row.Update("settle_date", dr["settle_date"]);
                row.Update("term", dr["term"]);

                eta.IncrementAndReport(1, 20);
                i++;
            }
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);
        }
        public static CashflowSet LoadCurrentCashflowInternal(bool report_individually)
        {

            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "cashflows_all");

            var rows = xlt.AllRows("MONTH");
            ETA eta = new ETA(rows.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            CashflowSet cfs = new CashflowSet();

            foreach (var cf in rows)
            {

                DateTime date = cf.GetValue<DateTime>("DATE");
                var s = cfs.GetCashflowSingle(date);
                
                s.month_num = cf.GetValue<int>("MONTH");
                s.remaining_bom_pct = cf.GetValue<double>("BOM REMAINING %");
                s.remaining_eom_pct = cf.GetValue<double>("EOM REMAINING %");
                s.remaining_after_default_pct = cf.GetValue<double>("REMAINING AFTER DEFAULT %");
                s.num_contracts_orig = cf.GetValue<double>("NUM CONTRACTS");
                s.unlock_share_bom_orig = cf.GetValue<double>("UNLOCK SHARE FINAL");
                s.unlock_share_eom_orig = cf.GetValue<double>("END UNLOCK SHARE");
                s.defaulted_unlock_share = cf.GetValue<double>("DEFAULTED UNLOCK SHARE");
                s.prepay_unlock_share = cf.GetValue<double>("PREPAY UNLOCK SHARE");
                s.recovery_month = cf.GetValue<double>("RECOVERED UNLOCK SHARE");
                s.inv_cashflow_aum = cf.GetValue<double>("INV CASHFLOW W/AUM");
                s.avg_life_calc = cf.GetValue<double>("AVG LIFE CALC");
                s.avg_life_calc_dollars = cf.GetValue<double>("AVG LIFE CALC $");

                s.prepay_month_pct = s.remaining_after_default_pct - s.remaining_eom_pct;
                


                s.num_contracts_orig_single_month = (s.month_num == 0) ? s.num_contracts_orig : 0;
                s.exchange_rate = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "model_exchange_rate");



                s.DoCalcs();

                if (report_individually)
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }

            if (report_individually)
                xlh.WriteStatusBar("DONE!");
            return cfs;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PriceYieldMult()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string pricing_input = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "price_yield_mult_input", false);
            string solve_for = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "price_yield_mult_solve_for", false);
            string type = UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyLetters(pricing_input);
            double? num = UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyNumbersDbl(pricing_input).Value;
            switch (type)
            {
                case "Y":
                    {
                        num = num.Value / 100.0;
                        break;
                    }
            }
            switch (solve_for)
            {
                case "EXCHANGE RATE":
                    {
                        solve_for = "model_exchange_rate";
                        break;
                    }
            }
            if (null == solve_for)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Need an input first");
                return;
            }

            xlh.GoalSeek("hec_inv_yield_aum_perf", num.Value, solve_for);


        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object InvYield(double raw_yield, double? aum, double? hurdle_pref_return, double? lp_share, bool catch_up)
        {


            double yield_net_aum = raw_yield - aum.Value;

            double optimal_gp = yield_net_aum * lp_share.Value;

            double net_inv_yield = Math.Min(Math.Max(yield_net_aum - optimal_gp, hurdle_pref_return.Value), yield_net_aum);

            

            

            

            
            

            return net_inv_yield;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CopyResults()
        {

            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var before = xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);
            int grid_rows = 12;
            int grid_cols = 12;
            int squares = grid_rows * grid_cols;
            ETA eta = new ETA(squares, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);
            xlh.ClearDataGridWithOffsets(null, new string[] { "grid_output_yield", "grid_output_wal", "grid_output_exit_month_12", "grid_output_exit_month_24", "grid_output_yield_no_perf", "grid_output_exchange_rate", "grid_output_price", "grid_output_port_comp" }, grid_rows, grid_cols);
            bool combine_cashflows = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "grid_yield_combine_cashflows");
            double? yield_mult_solver = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<double>("grid_yield_mult_solver");
            double? grid_only_do_exchange_rate = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<double>("grid_only_do_exchange_rate");

            List<CashflowSet> cfs = new List<CashflowSet>();
            for (int r = 0; r != grid_rows; r++)
            {
                for (int c = 0; c != grid_cols; c++)
                {

                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "grid_solver_row", r + 1);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "grid_solver_column", c + 1);

                    eta.IncrementAndReport();

                    object cpr = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "grid_input_cpr", false);
                    object cdr = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "grid_input_cdr", false);
                    object sev = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "grid_input_sev", false);
                    double? exchange_rate = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<double>("grid_input_exchange_rate");
                    object port_pct = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "grid_input_port_pct", false);


                    if (0 == exchange_rate.Value || (null != grid_only_do_exchange_rate && grid_only_do_exchange_rate != exchange_rate.Value))
                        continue;



                    xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_cpr", cpr);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_cdr", cdr);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_sev", sev);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "model_exchange_rate", exchange_rate);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_num_contracts", port_pct);

                    xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);

                    if (null != yield_mult_solver)
                    {
                        xlh.GoalSeek("hec_inv_yield_aum_perf", yield_mult_solver.Value, "model_exchange_rate");
                    }

                    object yield = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "hec_inv_yield_aum_perf");
                    object wal = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "hec_wal");
                    object exit_12 = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "hec_exited_month_12");
                    object exit_24 = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "hec_exited_month_24");
                    object grid_output_yield_no_perf = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "hec_inv_yield_aum");
                    object grid_output_exchange_rate = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "model_exchange_rate");
                    object grid_output_price = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "hec_price_calc");

                    if (null != yield & yield.ToString().Contains("-2"))
                    {
                        yield = null;
                        wal = null;
                        exit_12 = null;
                        exit_24 = null;
                    }
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_yield", r + 2, c + 2, yield);
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_wal", r + 2, c + 2, wal);
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_exit_month_12", r + 2, c + 2, exit_12);
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_exit_month_24", r + 2, c + 2, exit_24);
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_yield_no_perf", r + 2, c + 2, grid_output_yield_no_perf);
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_exchange_rate", r + 2, c + 2, grid_output_exchange_rate);
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_price", r + 2, c + 2, grid_output_price);
                    xlh.WriteRangeRow("grid_output_port_comp", r + 2, c + 2, port_pct);
                    if (combine_cashflows)
                    {
                        CashflowSet cf = LoadCurrentCashflowInternal(false);
                        cfs.Add(cf);
                    }

                }
            }

            if (combine_cashflows)
            {
                CashflowSet combined = Analytics.Utils.CombineCashflows(cfs);
                XLTable cf = new XLTable(xlh, "combined_cashflows");
                cf.DumpObject<CashflowSingle>(combined.AllFlows.Values.ToList());
            }
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Done!");

        }
