        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void ExchangeSolver()
        {

            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var before = xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);

            XLTable inputs = new XLTable(xlh, "exchange_solver");

            var rows = inputs.AllRows("EXCHANGE RATE");

            string[] cprs = xlh.GetRangeArray<string>(null, "solver_cpr", false);
            string[] cdrs = xlh.GetRangeArray<string>(null, "solver_cdr", false);
            string[] sevs = xlh.GetRangeArray<string>(null, "solver_sev", false);
            string[] hpis = xlh.GetRangeArray<string>(null, "solver_hpi", false);
            string[] orig_fee = xlh.GetRangeArray<string>(null, "solver_orig_fee", false);
            string last_cpr = null;
            string last_cdr = null;
            string last_sev = null;
            string last_hpi = null;
            string last_orig_fee = null;
            for (int i = 0; i != 5; i++)
            {
                inputs.ClearColumn((i + 1).ToString());
            }
            for (int i = 0; i != 5; i++)
            {

                if (null == cprs[i] && null == cdrs[i] && null == sevs[i] && null == hpis[i] && null == orig_fee[i])
                {
                    continue;
                }
                if (null != cprs[i])
                    last_cpr = cprs[i];
                if (null != cdrs[i])
                    last_cdr = cdrs[i];
                if (null != sevs[i])
                    last_sev = sevs[i];
                if (null != hpis[i])
                    last_hpi = hpis[i];
                if (null != orig_fee[i])
                    last_orig_fee = orig_fee[i];
                ;
                ETA eta = new ETA(rows.Count(), xlh.WriteStatusBar);
                foreach (var row in rows)
                {
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();

                    xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);

                    double? exchange = row.GetValueNullable<double>("EXCHANGE RATE");
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "model_exchange_rate", exchange);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "orig_fee", last_orig_fee);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_cpr", last_cpr);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_cdr", last_cdr);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_sev", last_sev);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "model_hpi_increase", last_hpi);

                    xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);
                    double? yield = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "hec_inv_yield");
                    row.Update((i + 1).ToString(), yield);

                }
            }
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(before);

            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Done!");
        }


        [ExcelFunction]

        public static void LoadCurrentCashflow()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            List<CashflowSet> cfs = new List<CashflowSet>();
            LoadCurrentCashflowInternal(false);
            
            {
                CashflowSet c = LoadCurrentCashflowInternal(false);
                cfs.Add(c);
            }

            
            CashflowSet combined = Analytics.Utils.CombineCashflows(cfs);
            
            XLTable cf = new XLTable(xlh, "combined_cashflows");
            cf.DumpObject<CashflowSingle>(combined.AllFlows.Values.ToList());
            xlh.ActivateSheet("Combine Cashflows");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static async void PriceAllApi()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var before = xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);
            XLTable pricing_all = new XLTable(xlh, "pricing_all");
            
            var rows = pricing_all.AllRows("effective_date");
            ETA eta = new ETA(rows.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            double default_cpr = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "pricing_default_cpr", false);
            double default_cdr = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "pricing_default_cdr", false);
            double default_sev = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "pricing_default_sev", false);
            double default_hpi = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "pricing_default_hpi", false);

            double default_price = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "pricing_default_price", false);
            DateTime default_settle_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "pricing_default_settle_date", false);

            pricing_all.ClearColumns("PX_WAL_COLLAT,PX_TOTAL_CONTRACT_CASH,PX_INVESTOR_GROSS_NET_CASH,PX_INV_YIELD_GROSS,PX_PRICE_TIME,PX_ERROR");
            List<PricingEngine> pe_all = new List<PricingEngine>();
            List<PricingOutput> pe_output = new List<PricingOutput>();
            foreach (var row in rows)
            {
                try
                {
                    Asset a = new Asset();
                    string asset_id = row.GetValue<string>("ASSET_ID");
                    DateTime effective_date = row.GetValue<DateTime>("EFFECTIVE_DATE");
                    double starting_home_value = row.GetValue<double>("STARTING_HOME_VALUE");
                    double current_home_value = row.GetValue<double>("CURRENT_HOME_VALUE", starting_home_value);
                    double cost_limit = row.GetValue<double>("COST_LIMIT");
                    double cost_limit_basis = row.GetValue<double>("COST_LIMIT_BASIS");
                    DateTime? buyout_active_date = row.GetValueNullable<DateTime>("BUYOUT_ACTIVE_DATE");
                    double investment_payment = row.GetValue<double>("INVESTMENT_PAYMENT");
                    double exchange_rate = row.GetValue<double>("EXCHANGE_RATE");
                    int term_months = row.GetValue<int>("TERM");

                    a.PopulateAsset(asset_id, effective_date, starting_home_value, cost_limit, cost_limit_basis, buyout_active_date, investment_payment, exchange_rate, term_months, current_home_value);


                    double cpr = row.GetValue<double>("CPR", default_cpr);
                    double cdr = row.GetValue<double>("CDR", default_cdr);
                    double sev = row.GetValue<double>("SEV", default_sev);
                    double hpi = row.GetValue<double>("HPI", default_hpi);
                    CashflowInputs cfi = new CashflowInputs();
                    cfi.Populate(cpr, cdr, sev, hpi);
                    CashflowSet cfs = Analytics.CashflowEngine.RunCashflows(a, cfi);

                    double price = row.GetValue<double>("PRICE", default_price);
                    DateTime settle_date = row.GetValue<DateTime>("SETTLE_DATE", default_settle_date);

                    PricingInput pi = new PricingInput();
                    pi.Populate(settle_date, price);
                    
                    PricingEngine pe = new PricingEngine();
                    ExcelOutputHelper peh = new ExcelOutputHelper(row);
                    PricingEngine.PricingOutputDelegate poe = new PricingEngine.PricingOutputDelegate(peh.WriteOutput);
                    poe = null;
                    pe.SetInputs(poe, cfs, pi);
                    pe.asset_id = a.asset_id;
                    
                    
                    pe_all.Add(pe);

                    

                    
                    
                    

                    
                    

                }
                catch (Exception n)
                {
                    row.Update("PX_ERROR", n.Message);
                }

     
            }
            List<Task> tasks = new List<Task>();
            foreach (PricingEngine pea in pe_all)
            {

                
                
                
                
                await pea.Price();
            }
            
            
            
            
            string elap = eta.GetElapsedTime("s") + " seconds";
            XtraMessageBox.Show(elap, "Finito..");
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(before);
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("DONE!");            
        }



        public class ExcelOutputHelper
        {
            XLTableRow _row;
            PricingInput _pi;
            public ExcelOutputHelper(XLTableRow row)
            {
                _row = row;
            }
 
            public void WriteOutput(PricingOutput po)
            {
                _row.Update("PX_TOTAL_CONTRACT_CASH", po.cfs.total_contract_cashflow);
                _row.Update("PX_INVESTOR_GROSS_NET_CASH", po.investor_gross_net_cash);
                _row.Update("PX_PRICE_TIME", po.price_time);

                _row.Update("PX_INV_YIELD_GROSS", po.investor_gross_yield);
                _row.Update("PX_WAL_COLLAT", po.cfs.wal);
            }

        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

        

        private class ExcelPricingOutputHelper
        {
            PricingOutput _po = null;
            XLTableRow _row = null;
            public ExcelPricingOutputHelper(PricingOutput po,XLTableRow row)
            {
                _po = po;
                _row = row;
            }
            private void WriteOutput()
            {
                _row.Update("PX_TOTAL_CONTRACT_CASH", _po.cfs.total_contract_cashflow);
                _row.Update("PX_INVESTOR_GROSS_NET_CASH", _po.investor_gross_net_cash);
                _row.Update("PX_PRICE_TIME", _po.price_time);

                _row.Update("PX_INV_YIELD_GROSS", _po.investor_gross_yield);
                _row.Update("PX_WAL_COLLAT", _po.cfs.wal);
            }
        }
        

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PriceAll()
        {
            

            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            XLTable inputs = new XLTable(xlh, "pricing_all");
            XLTable outputs = new XLTable(xlh, "pricing_output"); 
            
            var input_rows = inputs.AllRows("effective_date");
            ETA eta = new ETA(input_rows.Count,xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            
            bool do_calc_flags = (inputs.AllRows("calc_flag").Count > 0);
            if(!do_calc_flags)
                ClearPricingOutput();
            bool combine_cashflows = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "pricing_combine_cashflows", false);
            bool use_base_assumptions = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "use_base_assumptions", false);
            bool process_overrides = true;
            bool use_pricing_grid_assumptions = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "use_pricing_grid_assumptions", false);
            bool use_hpi_calc = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "use_hpi_calc", false);
            bool use_api_pricing = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "use_api_pricing", false, false);
            List<CashflowSet> cfs = new List<CashflowSet>();

            int? cashflow_settle_date_offset = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("cashflow_settle_date_offset");

            double? full_price = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<double>("hec_price_default");
            double? default_premium = (full_price / 100.00)-1.0;
            

            var before = xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);

            foreach (XLTableRow row in input_rows)
            {
                
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
                
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                
                bool calc = DoCalcCheck(do_calc_flags,row["calc_flag"]);
               
                
                if (!calc)
                {
                    continue;
                }
                else
                {
                    var corresponding = outputs.GetXLRow(row.one_based_row_index, false);
                    corresponding.Clear(null);
                    
                }

                row.SelectEntireRow();
                row.Update("px_price_time", DateTime.Now);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "model_home_value", row["HOME_VALUE_HPI_LATEST"]);
                DateTime settle_date = row.GetValue<DateTime>("SETTLE_DATE");


                if (null != cashflow_settle_date_offset)
                    settle_date = settle_date.AddMonths(cashflow_settle_date_offset.Value);
                

                

     

                xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_settle", settle_date);
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                



                
                
                
                
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);


                
                
                

                

                if (use_base_assumptions)
                {
                    CopyBaseAssumptions();
                }
                if (use_pricing_grid_assumptions)
                {
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRange(null, "pricing_grid_cpr_calc", "hec_cpr");
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRange(null, "pricing_grid_cdr_calc", "hec_cdr");
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRange(null, "pricing_grid_sev_calc", "hec_sev");
                }
                if (use_hpi_calc)
                {
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRange(null, "hpi_forecast_calc", "model_hpi_increase");
                }
                if(process_overrides)
                {
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    


                    xlh.WriteRangeIfNotNull(null, "hec_cpr", row["cpr"]);
                    xlh.WriteRangeIfNotNull(null, "hec_cdr", row["cdr"]);
                    xlh.WriteRangeIfNotNull(null, "hec_sev", row["sev"]);
                    xlh.WriteRangeIfNotNull(null, "model_hpi_increase", row["hpi"]);
                    xlh.WriteRangeIfNotNull(null, "model_exchange_rate", row["exchange_rate"]);
                    xlh.WriteRangeIfNotNull(null, "hec_markup", System.Convert.ToDouble(row["price"])/100.0);

                }

                if (!use_base_assumptions)
                {
                    
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRangeWithOverride(null, "prepay_rate_calc", row["hec_cpr"], "hec_cpr");
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRangeWithOverride(null, "cdr_rate_calc", row["hec_cdr"], "hec_cdr");
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRangeWithOverride(null, "sev_calc", row["hec_sev"], "hec_sev");
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRangeWithOverride(null, "home_app_calc", row["home_app"], "model_hpi_increase");
                    xlh.WriteRangeFromOtherRangeWithOverride(null, "exchange_rate_calc", row["exchange_rate"], "model_exchange_rate");

                    double? premium_override = row.GetValueNullable<double>("hec_price");
                    if (null != premium_override)
                        premium_override = (premium_override / 100.00) - 1.0;
                    else
                        premium_override = default_premium;
                    
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "hec_markup", premium_override);
                    
                    
                    
                    
                }

                

                

                
                
                
                





                
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);

                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_property_pass", "model_property_pass_fail");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_homeowner_pass", "model_homeowner_pass_fail");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_master_pass", "model_master_pass_fail");


                CashflowInputs pi = new CashflowInputs();
                
                
                

                
                
                
                
                
                
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);


                row.UpdateIfRowBlankOnly("px_loan_id", row.one_based_row_index);
                
                
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_inv_yield", "hec_inv_yield_aum_perf");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_wal", "hec_wal");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_exchange_ratio", "model_exchange_rate");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_hpi", "model_hpi_increase");
                
                
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_inv_yield_gross", "hec_inv_yield_gross");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_inv_yield_aum", "hec_inv_yield_aum");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "net_inv_aum_proceeds", "net_inv_aum_proceeds");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_inv_yield_disposition", "px_inv_yield_disposition"); 

                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_cpr", "hec_cpr");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_cdr", "hec_cdr");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_sev", "hec_sev");
                
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_cpr_pct", "model_cpr_ramp_pct");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_cdr_pct", "model_cdr_ramp_pct");
                inputs.UpdateFromRange(row, "px_model_ultv", "model_ultv");

                




                if (combine_cashflows)
                {
                    CashflowSet c = LoadCurrentCashflowInternal(false);
                    cfs.Add(c);
                }

                

                
                



                xlh.ScreenUpdating(true);
            }

            if (combine_cashflows)
            {
                

                xlh.ToggleScreenUpdating(true);
                CashflowSet combined = Analytics.Utils.CombineCashflows(cfs);
                
                XLTable cf = new XLTable(xlh, "combined_cashflows");
                cf.DumpObject<CashflowSingle>(combined.AllFlows.Values.ToList());
                
            }
            
            inputs.SelectEntireRow(1);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(before);
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Pricing Done!");
        }

        public static bool DoCalcCheck(bool should_do_calc, object calc)
        {
            bool calc_flag = true;
            if (!should_do_calc)
                return calc_flag;

            if (null != calc)
            {
                string which = calc.ToString();
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(which))
                    return true;
                if (which.ToUpper() == "N" || which.ToUpper() == "FALSE")
                    return false;
            }
            else
            {
                return false;
            }
            return calc_flag;
        }
        public static void ClearRangeInternal(string range)
        {
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel, range);
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(null);
        }
    }
}

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;

    public class MSR
    {

    [ExcelFunction(Category = "Unlock Toolkit", Name = "MSR", Description = "MSR")]
    public static void GetCounterpartyTradesAsOf(DateTime asOf)
    {
        XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            DateTime start = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "dailyProductionAsOf");
            DataTable results = BadgerLib.Trades.GetCounterpartyTradesAsOf(server, start);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "historicTrades");
            xlt.DumpData(results, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
        }
    }
}

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public class QualityChecklist
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SendQCReport()
        {
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteRange(null,"mail_sendmail", false);
            Unlock_Toolkit.Utils.GenericExport();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SendQCReportAuto()
        {
            
            Unlock_Toolkit.Utils.GenericExport();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void DoAllAndSend()
        {
            RunAllQC();
            SendQCReportAuto();
        }
        
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void RunAllQC()
        {
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling Production...");
            PopulateAllProduction();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling Closed & Corrected Critical Exceptions...");
            PopualteCriticalExceptions();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling Closed & Corrected Non-Critical Exceptions...");
            PopualteOtherExceptions();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling Open Exceptions...");
            PopualteOpenExceptions();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling Integrity Checks...");
            PopulateIntegrityChecks();
            PopulateAllIntegrityChecks();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling Document Custodian...");
            PopulateDocCustodian();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling User's Exceptions...");
            PopulateExceptionsByUser();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void RunUsersChecks()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteRange(null, "mail_sendmail", false);
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Pulling Users Exceptions...");
            List<string> user_ids = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "user_ids", false, "")?.Split(",").ToList();
            if (user_ids.IsNullOrEmpty())
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Please populate at least one User ID");
            else
            {
                foreach (var user in user_ids)
                {
                    xlh.WriteRange("BREAKDOWN-USER", "user_id", user);
                    PopulateExceptionsByUser();
                    var email = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "user_email", false);
                    xlh.WriteRange("SETUP", "mail_to", email);
                    xlh.WriteRange("SETUP", "mail_sheets", "BREAKDOWN-USER");
                    xlh.WriteRange("SETUP", "mail_filebase", "=\"User Breakdown - \" & user_firstname & \" \" & user_lastname");
                    Unlock_Toolkit.Utils.GenericExport();
                }
            }
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]

            xlh.WriteRange("SETUP", "mail_sheets", "REPORT CARD");

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateAllProduction()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            DateTime begin = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "exceptions_begin");
            DateTime end = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "exceptions_end");
            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Assets.GetAllProductionTimeframe(UnlockToolkit.DB, begin, end);
            PopulateTableGeneric("production_tbl", "ASSET_ID", tbl);

            DataTable all = BadgerLib.Assets.GetAllProductionTimeframe(UnlockToolkit.DB, begin.AddYears(-5), end.AddYears(5));

            double total_investment = System.Convert.ToDouble(all.Compute("SUM(investment_payment)", string.Empty));
            int total_count = all.Rows.Count;
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "origination_all_time", total_investment);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "origination_all_time_count", total_count);

        }

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateIntegrityChecks()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? priority_level = xlh.GetRange<Int32>(null, "priority_level");
            DataTable checks = BadgerLib.IntegrityChecks.GetIntegrityCheckTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, priority_level);


            var nodumpcols = new List<string> { "INF_CLOSED", "INF_OPEN", "USER1", "USER2", "USER3", "USER4", "USER5", "USER6", "USER7", "USER8", "USER9", "USER10" };
            
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, true);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "integrity_tbl");

            xlt.DumpData(checks, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar, nodumpcols);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("CHECK_NAME");
            string sheet_of_range = xlh.GetSheetNameFromRange("integrity_tbl");
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(sheet_of_range, false);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateAllIntegrityChecks()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? priority_level = xlh.GetRange<Int32>(null, "priority_level");

            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Assets.GetConsolidatedDataIntegrityIssues(UnlockToolkit.DB, null, false, true, null, priority_level);
            PopulateTableGeneric("integrityall_tbl", "ASSET_ID", tbl);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateAllUserInfo()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Exceptions.GetAllUsersInfo(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            PopulateTableGeneric("users_tbl", null, tbl);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateDocCustodian()
        {
            DataTable checks = BadgerLib.Custody.GetCustodyExceptions(UnlockToolkit.DB, false, true);
            PopulateTableGeneric("custody_tbl", "ASSET_ID", checks);
        }

        public static void PopulateExceptionsInternal(string table_range, bool include_open, bool include_closed, bool only_corrected, List<int> filter_ids, bool remove_ids_if_not_in, int? monday_id)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            DateTime begin = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "exceptions_begin");
            DateTime end = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "exceptions_end");
            int? priority_level = xlh.GetRange<Int32>(null, "priority_level");

            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Exceptions.PopualteQCExceptions(UnlockToolkit.DB, begin, end, include_open, include_closed, only_corrected, monday_id, priority_level);
            if (null != filter_ids)
            {
                tbl.RemoveRowsInternal<int>("qc_integritycheck_id", filter_ids, remove_ids_if_not_in);
            }
            PopulateTableGeneric(table_range, "ASSET_ID", tbl);
        }

        public static void PopulateTableGeneric(string table_range,string tighten_field,DataTable tbl)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, true);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, table_range);
            
            xlt.DumpData(tbl, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable(tighten_field);
            string sheet_of_range = xlh.GetSheetNameFromRange(table_range);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(sheet_of_range, false);
        }
    }
}

namespace Unlock_Toolkit.Buttons

    public class SeniorMortgageTape

        [ExcelFunction]

        public static void GenerateSeniorMortgageTape()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            DateTime cutOffDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "cutoff_date");

            XLTable assetsList = new XLTable(xlh, "settings_asset_filter_list_header");
            List<string> assets = assetsList.AllRows().Select(n => n["ASSET_ID"]).Where(n => n != null).Distinct().ToList(); 

            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Debt.SeniorMortgageDebt(UnlockToolkit.DB, cutOffDate, assets);

            
            XLTable xlt_snrMtgTape = new XLTable(xlh, "senior_mortgage_tape");

            MessageBox.Show("Senior Mortgage Tape Generated");
        }
    }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\Servicing.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class Servicing
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateServicingReport()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string src_sheet = "CASHFLOW";
            string sheet_identifier = "SVC-";
            string summary_sheet = "SUMMARY";
            string active_sheet = xlh.GetActiveSheet();
            xlh.ActivateSheet(src_sheet);
            xlh.DeleteAllSheetsContaining(sheet_identifier);

            string[] all_tasks = xlh.GetRangeArray<string>(null, "all_tasks", true);
            bool copy_all_sheets = false;
            xlh.ToggleDisplayAlerts(true);
            var before = xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC_WITHOUT_TABLES);
            xlh.DeleteSheet(summary_sheet);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "executive_summary");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(2);
            
            List<string> copy_over_ranges = new List<string>(new string[] { "svc_cashflow" });
            bool do_executive_summary = true;
            bool do_detailed_summary = true;

            int task_num = 0;
            foreach (string task in all_tasks)
            {
                xlh.ActivateSheet(src_sheet);
                xlh.WriteRange(src_sheet, "task_num", task);
                string task_name = xlh.GetRange<string>(src_sheet, "task_name");
                foreach (string range2copy in copy_over_ranges)
                {
                    if (do_detailed_summary)
                    {
                        if (task_num == 0)
                        {
                            xlh.CopySheet(src_sheet, summary_sheet);
                            xlh.CopyOverSpecial(summary_sheet, range2copy, summary_sheet, range2copy, XLHelper.PasteType.VALUES, XLHelper.PasteOperation.NONE);
                        }
                        else
                            xlh.CopyOverSpecial(src_sheet, range2copy, summary_sheet, range2copy, XLHelper.PasteType.VALUES, XLHelper.PasteOperation.ADD);
                    }
                    if (do_executive_summary)
                    {
                        xlt.CopyRowValues(1, task_num + 2);
                    }
                }
                

                if (copy_all_sheets)
                {
                    string new_tab_name = sheet_identifier + task_name;
                    xlh.CopySheet(src_sheet, new_tab_name);
                }
                task_num++;
            }

            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("EXECUTIVE SUMMARY", false);
            xlh.ActivateSheet(active_sheet);
        }
        

    }
}

        {

                {

                    UtilsLib.FileLib.CopySmart(file, final_name);
                    file = final_name;
                }

                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(file, true);
            }catch(Exception n)
            {

                    XtraMessageBox.Show(n.Message, "Uh oh....");
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateWiresAndTrades()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            double net_amount = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "wire_amount_input");

            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetFRBCollTransactions(UnlockToolkit.DB, net_amount, 1, 80018953081);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "frb_incomingwires_tbl");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(tbl, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("frbinv_id");

            string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_agreement_lookup", false);
            DataTable trades = BadgerLib.Trades.GetAssetTradeDetail(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "trade_history");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(trades, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("account");

            DataTable settlement_request = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetSettlementRequest(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "settlementrequest_tbl");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(settlement_request, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            bool settlement_exists = BadgerLib.Settlements.SettlementExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (settlement_exists)
            {
                var settlement_id = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetSettlementID(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "settlement_id", settlement_id);
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void AddIncomingWireToSettlementTrans()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_agreement_lookup", false);
            bool settlement_exists = BadgerLib.Settlements.SettlementExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "frb_cashreceived_tbl");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);

            if (settlement_exists)
            {
                var settlement_id = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetSettlementID(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "settlement_id", settlement_id);
                var cash = BadgerLib.Settlements.CashReceived(UnlockToolkit.DB, int.Parse(settlement_id));
                if (cash.Rows.Count == 0)
                    BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_incomingwire_insert");
                else
                    xlt.DumpData(cash, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SendCollectionsTransferEmail()
        {
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.SendCollectionsTransferEmail(UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel, server);
        }

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "settlement_request_insert");
        }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\SettlementCalculator.cs ---
using static DevExpress.XtraPrinting.Native.ExportOptionsPropertiesNames;
using static DevExpress.Utils.Diagnostics.GUIResources;

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class SettlmentCalc
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateQuickPDFHCS()
        {
            
            
            
            GeneratePDFInternal("HFL", 35, false);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateQuickPDPayoff()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            
            string settlementExists = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "settlement_exists", false);
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(settlementExists))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("A settlement already exists. Clear the existing settlement before generating a Settlement Statement.", "Settlement Exists");
                return;
            }

            
            string simpleInterestRequired = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "simple_interest_required", false);
            string waSettlementTemplate = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "wa_settlement_template", false);

            bool IsTrue(string v)
            {
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(v)) return false;
                v = v.Trim().ToLowerInvariant();
                return v == "true" || v == "1" || v == "yes" || v == "y";
            }

            if (IsTrue(simpleInterestRequired) && !IsTrue(waSettlementTemplate))
            {
                string msg = "Settlement must be generated in the Washington Simple Interest Template.";
                XtraMessageBox.Show(msg, "Settlement Template Error");
                throw new InvalidOperationException(msg);
            }

            
            if (!IsTrue(simpleInterestRequired) && IsTrue(waSettlementTemplate))
            {
                string msg = "Settlement must be generated using the normal Settlement Request template.";
                XtraMessageBox.Show(msg, "Settlement Template Error");
                throw new InvalidOperationException(msg);
            }

            string settlementType = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "settlement_type", false);
            string settlementReason = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "settlement_reason", false);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementType) &&
                settlementType.Trim().Equals("FORECLOSURE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                !((settlementReason ?? string.Empty).Trim().Equals("FORECLOSURE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
            {
                string msg = "When Settlement Type is FORECLOSURE, Settlement Reason must also be FORECLOSURE.";
                XtraMessageBox.Show(msg, "Settlement Validation");
                throw new InvalidOperationException(msg);
            }

            PopulateSettlementRequests();
            GeneratePDFInternal("Settlement Statement", 27, false);

            string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "asset_id", false);
            string filename_xlsx = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), asset_id + "_PRS.xlsx");
            string[] worksheet_2_export = new string[] { "Settlement Statement", "Settlement Details", "Future Settlement Payments" };
            int uoo = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "unpaid_owner_obligations", false);
            if (uoo > 0)
                worksheet_2_export[3] = "Expenses";
            string full_path_xls = xlh.ExportSelectedSheetStandard(false, worksheet_2_export, XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX, true, filename_xlsx);
            xlh.OpenSheet(full_path_xls, false);
            xlh.RemoveImagesFromSheet("Settlement Statement");
            xlh.SaveActiveWorkbook();
            string final_name = BadgerLib.Docs.FigureOutFullDocName(UnlockToolkit.DB, full_path_xls, asset_id, 27, false, false, true);
            UtilsLib.FileLib.CopySmart(filename_xlsx, final_name);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateQuickPDPayoffDraft()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            
            string settlementExists = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "settlement_exists", false);
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(settlementExists))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("A settlement already exists. Clear the existing settlement before generating a Settlement Statement.", "Settlement Exists");
                return;
            }
            GeneratePDFInternal("Settlement Statement", 27, false, true);
        }

        public static void GeneratePDFInternal(string pdf_print_select, int document_number, bool silent, bool draft)
        {
            if (!draft)
                GeneratePDFInternal(pdf_print_select, document_number, silent);
            else
            {
                try
                {
                    XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "pdf_print_select", pdf_print_select);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_acct_name", String.Empty);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_acct_num", String.Empty);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_routing_num", String.Empty);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_bank_name", String.Empty);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_bank_addr", String.Empty);

                    string file = CommandBar.GenerateQuickPDFInternal(false, true, silent, true);
                    string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "asset_id", false);
                    DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Copy also to Homeowner Folder?", "Salutations...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                    if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
                    {
                        string final_name = BadgerLib.Docs.FigureOutFullDocName(UnlockToolkit.DB, file, asset_id, document_number, false, false, true);
                        UtilsLib.FileLib.CopySmart(file, final_name);
                        file = final_name;
                    }
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(file, true);

                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_acct_name", "=wire_acct_name_lookup");
                    xlh.RefreshFormula(null, "wire_acct_name");
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_acct_num", "=wire_acct_num_lookup");
                    xlh.RefreshFormula(null, "wire_acct_num");
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_routing_num", "=wire_routing_num_lookup");
                    xlh.RefreshFormula(null, "wire_routing_num");
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_bank_name", "=wire_bank_name_lookup");
                    xlh.RefreshFormula(null, "wire_bank_name");
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "wire_bank_addr", "=wire_bank_addr_lookup");
                    xlh.RefreshFormula(null, "wire_bank_addr");
                }
                catch (Exception n)
                {
                    if (!silent)
                        XtraMessageBox.Show(n.Message, "Uh oh....");
                }
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void MoveTopAssetToSettlementCalculator()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string top_asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "top_asset_id");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "asset_id", top_asset_id);

            DateTime top_statement_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "top_statement_date");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "statement_date", top_statement_date);

            DateTime top_closing_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "top_closing_date");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "projected_close_date", top_closing_date);

            string top_settlement_type = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "top_settlement_type");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "settlement_type", top_settlement_type);

            string top_settlement_reason = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "top_settlement_reason");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "settlement_reason", top_settlement_reason);

            string top_sales_price = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "top_sales_price");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "ending_home_value", top_sales_price);

            DataTable next = new DataTable();
            next = xlh.GetRangeDataTable("PRS List", "settlement_inputs");
            next.Rows.RemoveAt(0);

            XLTable xlt_fundings = new XLTable(xlh, "settlement_inputs");
            xlt_fundings.DumpData(next, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            PopulateAsset();
            GenerateQuickPDPayoff();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateWiresAndTrades()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            double net_amount = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "wire_amount_input");

            PopulateTCBWires();

            string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_agreement_lookup", false);
            DataTable trades = BadgerLib.Trades.GetAssetTradeDetail(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);

            
            trades.DefaultView.Sort = "settle_date DESC";
            trades = trades.DefaultView.ToTable();

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "trade_history");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(trades, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("account");

            
            string isPartial = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "is_partial_template", false);
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(isPartial) && isPartial.Trim() == "1")
                return;

            DataTable settlement_request = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetSettlementRequest(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "settlementrequest_tbl");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(settlement_request, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            bool settlement_exists = BadgerLib.Settlements.SettlementExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (settlement_exists)
            {
                var settlement_id = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetSettlementID(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "settlement_id", settlement_id);
            }

            xlh.ClearRangeContents(null, "expense_info", false);
            bool uoo_exists = BadgerLib.Expenses.UnpaidOwnerObligationExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            if (uoo_exists)
            {
                DataTable expenses = BadgerLib.Expenses.GetUnpaidOwnerObligations(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
                xlh.WriteRange("expense_info", expenses.Transpose(), true);
            }

            CalculateTerminationFees();
            CalculateNetSettlementPayment();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateTCBWires()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            double net_amount = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "wire_amount_input");
            if (net_amount == 0d)
                return;

            long bankacct_id = xlh.GetRange<long>(null, "tcb_bankacct_id", false);

            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetTCBTransactions(UnlockToolkit.DB, net_amount, 1, bankacct_id);
            
            
            if (tbl.Rows.Count > 1)
            {
                DataTable firstRowTable = tbl.Clone();
                firstRowTable.ImportRow(tbl.Rows[0]);
                tbl = firstRowTable;
            }
            
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "tcb_incomingwires_tbl");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(tbl, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("tcbinv_id");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void AddIncomingWireToSettlementTrans()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_agreement_lookup", false);
            bool settlement_exists = BadgerLib.Settlements.SettlementExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "cashreceived_tbl");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);

            if (settlement_exists)
            {
                var settlement_id = BadgerLib.Settlements.GetSettlementID(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "settlement_id", settlement_id);
                var cash = BadgerLib.Settlements.CashReceived(UnlockToolkit.DB, int.Parse(settlement_id));
                if (cash.Rows.Count == 0)
                    BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_incomingwire_insert");
                else
                    xlt.DumpData(cash, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void AddIncomingWireToPartialPaymentTrans()

            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CopySettlementDataToFirstEmptyRow()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var workbook = xlh.ActiveWorkbook();
            var settlementData = xlh.GetRange("Wires-Trades", "current_settlement_datarow");
            string targetSheetName = xlh.GetRange<string>("SQL", "current_month_sheet");
            var targetSheet = workbook.Sheets[targetSheetName];
            int firstEmptyRow = xlh.LastUsedRow(targetSheetName, "A") + 1;            
            var targetRange = targetSheet.Rows[firstEmptyRow];
            int columnCount = settlementData.Columns.Count;

            for (int col = 1; col <= columnCount; col++)
            {
                targetRange.Cells[1, col].Value = settlementData.Cells[1, col].Value;
            }
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CopyPartialPaymentDataToTrackers()
        {
            const string relativeSubPath = @"Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\05 - Initiatives\Settlement Quick Publisher";
            const string jpmFileName = "SettlementQuickPublish - JPM_Formatted.xlsm";
            const string transactionFileName = "Customer Settlements & Refunds Tracker.xlsx";

            try
            {
                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

                
                string targetDirectory = ResolveSettlementQuickPublishDirectory(relativeSubPath);
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetDirectory))
                    return;

                
                var settlementDataRow = xlh.GetRange("Wires-Trades", "current_settlement_datarow");
                var transactionDataRow = xlh.GetRange("Wires-Trades", "current_settlement_transactions_datarow");
                string monthlySheetName = xlh.GetRange<string>("Lookup", "current_month_sheet");
                string transactionSheetName = xlh.GetRange<string>("Lookup", "transaction_tracker_sheet");

                if (settlementDataRow == null && transactionDataRow == null)
                    return;

                string originalWorkbookName = null;
                try { originalWorkbookName = xlh.ActiveWorkbookName(); } catch { }

                
                if (settlementDataRow != null && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(monthlySheetName))
                {
                    string jpmWorkbookPath = Path.Combine(targetDirectory, jpmFileName);
                    if (File.Exists(jpmWorkbookPath))
                    {
                        xlh.OpenSheet(jpmWorkbookPath, false);
                        var jpmWorkbook = xlh.ActiveWorkbook();
                        CopyRangeToFirstEmptyRow(xlh, jpmWorkbook, settlementDataRow, monthlySheetName);
                        try { xlh.SaveActiveWorkbook(); } catch { }
                    }
                }

                
                if (transactionDataRow != null && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(transactionSheetName))
                {
                    string transactionWorkbookPath = Path.Combine(targetDirectory, transactionFileName);
                    if (File.Exists(transactionWorkbookPath))
                    {
                        xlh.OpenSheet(transactionWorkbookPath, false);
                        var transactionWorkbook = xlh.ActiveWorkbook();
                        CopyRangeToFirstEmptyRow(xlh, transactionWorkbook, transactionDataRow, transactionSheetName);
                        try { xlh.SaveActiveWorkbook(); } catch { }
                    }
                }

                
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(originalWorkbookName))
                {
                    try { xlh.ActivateWorkbook(originalWorkbookName); } catch { }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                try { XtraMessageBox.Show(ex.Message, "Copy Partial Payment Data"); } catch { }
            }
        }
        private static string ResolveSettlementQuickPublishDirectory(string relativeSubPath)
        {
            var userProfile = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.UserProfile);
            
            
            string[] candidates = new[]
            {
                Path.Combine(userProfile, relativeSubPath),
                Path.Combine(userProfile, "OneDrive - " + relativeSubPath),
                Path.Combine(userProfile, "OneDrive", relativeSubPath),
                Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables($@"C:\Users\%username%\{relativeSubPath}")
            };

            foreach (var candidate in candidates)
            {
                if (Directory.Exists(candidate))
                    return candidate;
            }

            return null;
        }
        private static void CopyRangeToFirstEmptyRow(XLHelper xlh, dynamic targetWorkbook, dynamic sourceRange, string targetSheetName)
        {
            try
            {
                var targetSheet = targetWorkbook.Sheets[targetSheetName];
                if (targetSheet == null)
                    return;

                int firstEmptyRow;
                try
                {
                    firstEmptyRow = xlh.LastUsedRow(targetSheetName, "A") + 1;
                    if (firstEmptyRow < 1) firstEmptyRow = 1;
                }
                catch
                {
                    firstEmptyRow = 1;
                }

                var targetRow = targetSheet.Rows[firstEmptyRow];
                int columnCount = sourceRange.Columns.Count;

                for (int col = 1; col <= columnCount; col++)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        targetRow.Cells[1, col].Value = sourceRange.Cells[1, col].Value;
                    }
                    catch
                    {
                        
                    }
                }
            }
            catch
            {
                
            }
        }



        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CalculateTerminationFees()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            double latest_proceeds_amount = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "latest_proceeds_amount", false);
            double unlock_share_estimate = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "unlock_share_estimate", false);
            double investment_payment = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "investment_payment", false);
            double price = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "price", false)/100;
            int age = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "age", false);

            double hurdleAmount = latest_proceeds_amount * Math.Pow(1.08, age / 365.0);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "incentive_fee_hurdle", hurdleAmount);

            double dispositionFee = unlock_share_estimate > (investment_payment * (price + 0.01)) ? investment_payment * 0.01 : 0;
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "disposition_fee", dispositionFee);
            
            double incentiveFee = Math.Max(unlock_share_estimate - hurdleAmount - dispositionFee - Math.Floor(age / 30.0) / 12 * 0.0075 * investment_payment, 0) * 0.10;
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "incentive_fee", incentiveFee);

            double premiumRecapture = unlock_share_estimate >= (investment_payment * price) ? 0 : unlock_share_estimate - (investment_payment * price);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "premium_recapture", premiumRecapture);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CalculateNetSettlementPayment()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            
            string assetId = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "uam_agreement_lookup", false);
            DateTime closingDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "closing_date", false);
            double costLimitBasis = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "cost_limit_basis", false);
            double costLimit = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "cost_limit", false);
            DateTime effectiveDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "effective_date", false);
            double shareableValue = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "shareable_value", false);
            double unlockPct = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "unlock_pct", false);
            double investmentPayment = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "investment_payment", false);
            decimal settlementCosts = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null, "settlement_costs", false);
            decimal otherExpenses = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null, "other_expenses", false);
            decimal unpaidOwnerObligations = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null, "unpaid_owner_obligations", false);
            decimal credits = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null, "credits", false);

            
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM dbo.CalcNetSettlementPaymentDetails(@asset_id, @closing_date, @cost_limit_basis, @cost_limit, @effective_date, @shareable_value, @unlock_pct, @investment_payment, @settlement_costs, @other_expenses, @unpaid_owner_obligations, @credits)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", assetId);
            q.AddParameter("@closing_date", closingDate);
            q.AddParameter("@cost_limit_basis", costLimitBasis);
            q.AddParameter("@cost_limit", costLimit);
            q.AddParameter("@effective_date", effectiveDate);
            q.AddParameter("@shareable_value", shareableValue);
            q.AddParameter("@unlock_pct", unlockPct);
            q.AddParameter("@investment_payment", investmentPayment);
            q.AddParameter("@settlement_costs", settlementCosts);
            q.AddParameter("@other_expenses", otherExpenses);
            q.AddParameter("@unpaid_owner_obligations", unpaidOwnerObligations);
            q.AddParameter("@credits", credits);

            DataTable result = q.ExecuteTable();

            
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "payment_details");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(result, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CopySettlementTransactionsfromQuickPublisher()
        {
            const string relativeSubPath = @"Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\05 - Initiatives\Settlement Quick Publisher";
            const string targetFileName = "Customer Settlements & Refunds Tracker.xlsx";

            try
            {
                
                string targetDirectory = ResolveSettlementQuickPublishDirectory(relativeSubPath);
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetDirectory))
                    return;

                string workbookPath = Path.Combine(targetDirectory, targetFileName);
                if (!File.Exists(workbookPath))
                    return;

                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                string originalWorkbookName = null;
                try { originalWorkbookName = xlh.ActiveWorkbookName(); } catch { }

                
                var settlementData = xlh.GetRange("Wires-Trades", "current_settlement_transactions_datarow");
                if (settlementData == null)
                    return;

                string targetSheetName = xlh.GetRange<string>("SQL", "transaction_tracker_sheet");

                xlh.OpenSheet(workbookPath, false);
                var targetWorkbook = xlh.ActiveWorkbook();

                
                CopyRangeToFirstEmptyRow(xlh, targetWorkbook, settlementData, targetSheetName);

                
                try { xlh.SaveActiveWorkbook(); } catch { }

                
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(originalWorkbookName))
                {
                    try { xlh.ActivateWorkbook(originalWorkbookName); } catch { }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                try { XtraMessageBox.Show(ex.Message, "Copy Settlement Transactions"); } catch { }
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CalcNetSettlementPaymentDetails()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            string assetId                  = xlh.GetRange<string>(null,  "asset_id_input", false);
            DateTime closingDate            = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "closing_date_input", false);
            decimal costLimitBasis          = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null,  "cost_limit_basis_input", false);
            double costLimit                = xlh.GetRange<double>(null,   "cost_limit_input", false);
            DateTime effectiveDate          = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "effective_date_input", false);
            double shareableValue           = xlh.GetRange<double>(null,   "shareable_value_input", false);
            double unlockPct                = xlh.GetRange<double>(null,   "unlock_pct_input", false);
            double investmentPayment        = xlh.GetRange<double>(null,   "investment_payment_input", false);
            decimal settlementCosts         = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null,  "settlement_costs_input", false);
            decimal otherExpenses           = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null,  "other_expenses_input", false);
            decimal unpaidOwnerObligations  = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null,  "unpaid_owner_obligations_input", false);
            decimal credits                 = xlh.GetRange<decimal>(null,  "credits_input", false);

            string sql = "SELECT * FROM dbo.CalcNetSettlementPaymentDetails(@asset_id, @closing_date, @cost_limit_basis, @cost_limit, @effective_date, @shareable_value, @unlock_pct, @investment_payment, @settlement_costs, @other_expenses, @unpaid_owner_obligations, @credits)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id",                     assetId);
            q.AddParameter("@closing_date",                 closingDate);
            q.AddParameter("@cost_limit_basis",             costLimitBasis);
            q.AddParameter("@cost_limit",                   costLimit);
            q.AddParameter("@effective_date",               effectiveDate);
            q.AddParameter("@shareable_value",              shareableValue);
            q.AddParameter("@unlock_pct",                   unlockPct);
            q.AddParameter("@investment_payment",           investmentPayment);
            q.AddParameter("@settlement_costs",             settlementCosts);
            q.AddParameter("@other_expenses",               otherExpenses);
            q.AddParameter("@unpaid_owner_obligations",     unpaidOwnerObligations);
            q.AddParameter("@credits",                      credits);

            DataTable result = q.ExecuteTable();

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "payment_details");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(result, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
        }
