namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public class Strats
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void DoAllStrats()
        {
            string base_folder = BillOfSale.GetTradeBaseFolder();
            DoAllStratsInternal(base_folder);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void DoAllStratsGeneric()
        {
            string base_folder = Path.GetTempPath();
            DoAllStratsInternal(base_folder);
        }

        public static void DoAllStratsInternal(string base_folder)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strats_do_tape", false);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strat_inc_closed", true);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strats_do_prepays", true);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strats_do_credit_change", false);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strats_do_hpi", false);
            Strats.GenerateStrats();

            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strat_inc_closed", false);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strats_do_prepays", false);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strats_do_credit_change", true);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "strats_do_hpi", true);
            Strats.GenerateStrats();
            UtilsLib.FileLib.SpawnProcess(base_folder, true);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("DONE!");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateStrats()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            bool do_prepay = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Strats", "strats_do_prepays");
            bool do_hpi = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Strats", "strats_do_hpi");
            bool do_tape = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Strats", "strats_do_tape");
            bool do_credit_change = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Strats", "strats_do_credit_change");
            bool export_to_excel = (xlh.GetRange<string>("Settings", "export_to_excel")?.ToUpper() == "Y") ? true : false;
            XLTable account_list = new XLTable(xlh,"strat_accts_list");
            if (account_list.AnyRowPopulated("Run?"))
            {
                foreach (XLTableRow row in account_list.AllRows("Run?"))
                {
                    string account_name = row["Run?"].ToString();
                    xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strat_accts", account_name);
                    GenerateStratsInternal(do_prepay, do_hpi, do_tape, do_credit_change, export_to_excel);
                }
            }
            else
            {
                string combined_strat_accts_list = xlh.GetRange<string>("Settings", "combined_strat_accts_list");
                xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strat_accts", combined_strat_accts_list);
                GenerateStratsInternal(do_prepay, do_hpi, do_tape, do_credit_change, export_to_excel);
            }
        }
        
        public static void GenerateStratsInternal(bool do_prepay, bool do_hpi, bool do_tape, bool strats_do_credit_change, bool export_to_excel)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            var bucketsToRun = xlh.GetRange<string>("Strats", "strat_buckets");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(bucketsToRun))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show($"Please select buckets from the settings tab","Bro - choose some buckets");
                return;
            }
            List<string> buckets = bucketsToRun.Split(',').ToList();
            List<int> accounts = new List<int>();
            var acctsInput = xlh.GetRange<string>("Strats", "strat_accts");

            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(acctsInput))
            {
                accounts = xlh.GetRange<string>("Strats", "strat_accts")?.Split(',')?.Select(n => System.Convert.ToInt32(n)).ToList();
            }            
            
            bool closed_assets = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Strats", "strat_inc_closed");
            bool remove_paid_off_even_if_no_reported = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Strats", "remove_paid_off_even_if_no_reported", false, false);
            int? guideline_id_override = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("strat_guideline_override");
            XLTable filter = new XLTable(xlh, "settings_asset_filter_list");
            List<string> assets = filter.AllRows().Select(n => n["ASSET_ID"]).Where(n => n != null).Distinct().ToList(); 
            string account_name = xlh.GetRange<string>("Strats", "account_label",false);
            DateTime cutoff = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>("Strats", "input_cutoff");
            DateTime hpi_asof = BadgerLib.HPI.GetLatestAsOf(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "hpi_asof ", hpi_asof);

            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Strats", true);
            string base_folder = Path.GetTempPath();
            List<string> prepay_files = new List<string>();
            List<string> prepay_calendar_files = new List<string>();
            List<string> hpi_calendar_files = new List<string>();
            List<string> seasoning_generic_files = new List<string>();

            
            List<string> prepay_xl_files = new List<string>();
            List<string> prepay_xl_calendar_files = new List<string>();
            List<string> hpi_xl_calendar_files = new List<string>();
            List<string> seasoning_xl_generic_files = new List<string>();

            ETA eta = new ETA(buckets.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            DataTable tape = null;

            foreach (string bucket in buckets)
            {
                string which = bucket.Replace("bucket_", "");
                DataSet strats = GetStrat(UnlockToolkit.DB, accounts, guideline_id_override, which, closed_assets, assets, remove_paid_off_even_if_no_reported, cutoff);
                DataTable strat = strats.Tables[0];
            
                ProcessStratInternal("'Strats'!" + bucket, strat);

                if (null == tape)
                    tape = strats.Tables[13];

                xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strat_processing_table", which);
                string PREPAY_NAME = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "PREPAY_name", false, null, false);
                string nice_name = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExist<string>("PREPAY_CURRENT_PROCESS",null);
                
                if (do_prepay)
                {
                    List<string> extra_tighten_tables = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<string>(null, "cpr_extra_tighten_tables", true);
                    string cpr_table_range = "cpr_" + which;

                    ProcessStratInternal("cpr_bucket_generic", strats.Tables[2]);
                    ProcessStratInternal("cpr_bucket_generic_outstanding", strats.Tables[3]);
                    ProcessStratInternal("cpr_bucket_generic_payoffs", strats.Tables[4]);
                    xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Prepay Generic", false);
                    TightenExtra(extra_tighten_tables);

                    string final_name = CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh,"Prepay Generic", PREPAY_NAME + " - " + nice_name, true, base_folder, export_to_excel);
                    prepay_files.Add(final_name);

                    ProcessStratInternal("cpr_month_bucket_generic", strats.Tables[5]);
                    ProcessStratInternal("cpr_month_bucket_generic_outstanding", strats.Tables[6]);
                    ProcessStratInternal("cpr_month_bucket_generic_payoffs", strats.Tables[7]);
                    xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Prepay Calendar Generic", false);
                    TightenExtra(extra_tighten_tables);

                    string final_calendar_name = CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh, "Prepay Calendar Generic","CALENDAR - "+ PREPAY_NAME + " - " + nice_name, true, base_folder, export_to_excel);
                    prepay_calendar_files.Add(final_calendar_name);

                    if (export_to_excel)
                    {
                        string final_xl_name = final_name.Replace(".pdf", ".xlsx");
                        prepay_xl_files.Add(final_xl_name);
                        string final_xl_calendar_name = final_calendar_name.Replace(".pdf", ".xlsx");
                        prepay_xl_calendar_files.Add(final_xl_calendar_name);
                    }

                    SaveandSpawnStratsInternal(true, base_folder, "Prepay Calendar Generic");                 
                }
                
                if (do_hpi)
                {
                    List<string> extra_tighten_tables = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<string>(null, "hpi_extra_tighten_tables", true);

                    ProcessStratInternal("hpi_month_bucket_generic", strats.Tables[8]);
                    ProcessStratInternal("hpi_month_bucket_generic_outstanding", strats.Tables[9]);
                    xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("HPI Calendar Generic", false);
                    TightenExtra(extra_tighten_tables);

                    string final_calendar_name = CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh,"HPI Calendar Generic", "HPI - " + account_name + " - " + nice_name, true, base_folder, export_to_excel);
                    hpi_calendar_files.Add(final_calendar_name);
                    if (export_to_excel)
                    {
                        string final_xl_name = final_calendar_name.Replace(".pdf", ".xlsx");
                        hpi_xl_calendar_files.Add(final_xl_name);
                    }
                }
                
                if (strats_do_credit_change)
                {
                    List<string> extra_tighten_tables = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<string>(null, "seasoning_generic_extra_tighten_tables", true);

                    ProcessStratInternal("seasoning_bucket_generic", strats.Tables[11]);
                    ProcessStratInternal("seasoning_bucket_generic_outstanding", strats.Tables[12]);
                    xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Seasoning Generic", false);
                    TightenExtra(extra_tighten_tables);

                    string final_calendar_name = CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh, "Seasoning Generic", "CREDIT CHANGE - " + account_name + " - " + nice_name, true, base_folder, export_to_excel);
                    seasoning_generic_files.Add(final_calendar_name);
                    if (export_to_excel)
                    {
                        string final_xl_name = final_calendar_name.Replace(".pdf", ".xlsx");
                        seasoning_xl_generic_files.Add(final_xl_name);
                    }
                }
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }

            
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Strats", false);
            SaveandSpawnStratsInternal(true, base_folder, "Strats");

            
            if (do_tape)
            {
                XLTable xltape = new XLTable(xlh, "strats_tape");
                
                xltape.DumpData(tape, true, null, null);
            }
            
            if (prepay_files.Count > 0)
            {
                string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"PREPAY - Seasoning - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.MergePDFs(combined_file, prepay_files);
                prepay_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
            }
            if(prepay_calendar_files.Count > 0)
            {
                string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"PREPAY - Calendar - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.MergePDFs(combined_file, prepay_calendar_files);
                prepay_calendar_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
            }
            if (hpi_calendar_files.Count > 0)
            {
                string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"HPI - Calendar - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.MergePDFs(combined_file, hpi_calendar_files);
                hpi_calendar_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
            }
            if(seasoning_generic_files.Count > 0)
            {
                string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"CREDIT CHANGE - Seasoning - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.MergePDFs(combined_file, seasoning_generic_files);
                seasoning_generic_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
            }

            if (export_to_excel)
            {
                if (prepay_xl_files.Count > 0)
                {
                    string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"PREPAY - Seasoning - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.xlsx");
                    xlh.CombineExcelFiles(prepay_xl_files, combined_file);
                    prepay_xl_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
                }
                if (prepay_xl_calendar_files.Count > 0)
                {
                    string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"PREPAY - Calendar - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.xlsx");
                    xlh.CombineExcelFiles(prepay_xl_calendar_files, combined_file);
                    prepay_xl_calendar_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
                }
                if (hpi_xl_calendar_files.Count > 0)
                {
                    string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"HPI - Calendar - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.xlsx");
                    xlh.CombineExcelFiles(hpi_xl_calendar_files, combined_file);
                    hpi_xl_calendar_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
                }
                if (seasoning_xl_generic_files.Count > 0)
                {
                    string combined_file = Path.Combine(base_folder, $"CREDIT CHANGE - Seasoning - {account_name} - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.xlsx");
                    xlh.CombineExcelFiles(seasoning_xl_generic_files, combined_file);
                    seasoning_xl_generic_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
                }
            }



            ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectory(base_folder,false);

            xlh.SelectSheetFromRange("Strats","A1");
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Strats", false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Prepay", false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Prepay Generic", false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Prepay Calendar Generic", false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("HPI Calendar Generic", false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Seasoning Generic", false);
        }

        public static DataSet GetStrat(string server, List<int> accts, int? guideline_id_override, string which, bool include_paid_off, List<string> only_include_assets, bool remove_paid_off_even_if_not_investor_reported, DateTime cutoff)
        {
            if (null == only_include_assets)
                only_include_assets = new List<string>();
            string sql = "exec dbo.GenerateStrats @accts=@accts, @guideline_id_override=@guideline_id_override,@which=@which, @include_paid_off=@include_paid_off,@only_include_assets=@only_include_assets,@remove_paid_off_even_if_not_investor_reported=@remove_paid_off_even_if_not_investor_reported,@cutoff=@cutoff";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@accts", accts);
            q.AddParameter("@guideline_id_override", guideline_id_override);
            q.AddParameter("@which", which);
            q.AddParameter("@include_paid_off", include_paid_off);
            q.AddParameter("@only_include_assets", only_include_assets);
            q.AddParameter("@remove_paid_off_even_if_not_investor_reported", remove_paid_off_even_if_not_investor_reported);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff", cutoff);

            return q.Execute();
        }

        public static void ProcessStratInternal(string range,DataTable strat)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, range);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
            xlh.SelectSheetFromRange(null,range);
            
            xlt.ClearColumnsExcept("IGNORE");
            xlt.UnhideAllTable();
            string which = range.Replace("bucket_", "");
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Processing: " + which);
            xlt.DumpData(strat, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("#");
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);
        }

        public static void TightenExtra(List<string> tables)
        {
            if (null == tables)
                return;
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            foreach (string table in tables)
            {
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, table);
                xlt.TightenUpTable("#");
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SaveandSpawnStrats()
        {
            SaveandSpawnStratsInternal(false, null, "Strats");
        }

        public static void SaveandSpawnStratsInternal(bool queit, string base_folder,string sheet)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            string name = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "strat_name");
            CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh,sheet, name, queit,base_folder);
        }

        #region Methods for Settings tab

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void ClearAssetFilterList()
        {
            Generic.ClearRangeContents("settings_asset_filter_list_no_header");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SelectAllStrats()
        {
            SetStratsValue("Y");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void UnSelectAllStrats()
        {
            SetStratsValue("N");
        }

        private static void SetStratsValue(string value)
        {
            Generic.SetSingleValueToRange("settings_strat_run_flag", value);
        }

        #endregion


    }
}

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    using static DevExpress.XtraPrinting.Native.ExportOptionsPropertiesNames;
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;

    public class Tape
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateTape()
        {
            GenerateTapeInternal();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateAllHistoricMonthEndTapes()
        {
            GenerateAllHistoricMonthEndTapesInternal();
        }

        public static void GenerateAllHistoricMonthEndTapesInternal()
        {
            try
            {
                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

                DateTime startDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>("Inputs", "inputs_cutoff");
                
                string inputAccounts = xlh.GetRange<string>("Inputs", "inputs_accounts");
                List<int> accounts = new List<int>();
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(inputAccounts))
                    accounts = inputAccounts.Split(',').Select(n => System.Convert.ToInt32(n)).ToList();

                XLTable assetFilter = new XLTable(xlh, "Inputs!input_asset_list");
                List<string> assets = assetFilter.AllRows().Select(n => n["asset id"]).Where(n => n != null).Distinct().ToList();

                
                bool blankTrades = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_blank_trades");
                bool blankPrice = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_blank_price");
                bool tradeTD = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_trade_td");
                bool tradeSD = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_trade_sd");
                bool includeZeroPos = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_include_zero_pos");
                bool deleteTradesIfNotInvReported = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_del_trades_not_inv_reported");
                bool processExceptions = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_process_exceptions");
                bool includeExceptions = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_include_exceptions");
                
                DateTime cutoff;
                DataTable tape = null;

                for (DateTime date = startDate; date <= DateTime.Today; date = date.AddMonths(1))
                {
                    
                    cutoff = new DateTime(date.Year, date.Month, 1).AddMonths(1).AddDays(-1); ;
                    UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("Generating Tape: Cutoff [{0}]....", cutoff.ToShortDateString()));
                    DataSet tapeData = GetMonthEndTapeData(accounts, cutoff, assets, blankTrades, blankPrice, tradeTD, tradeSD, includeZeroPos, deleteTradesIfNotInvReported, processExceptions, includeExceptions);
                    if (tapeData == null || tapeData.Tables.Count == 0)
                    {
                        UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Failed to Generate Tape.  No Data Returned.");
                        return;
                    }


                    if (tape == null)
                      tape = tapeData.Tables[0];
                    else
                        tape.Merge( (tapeData.Tables.Count > 1) ? tapeData.Tables[2] :  tapeData.Tables[0]);
                }

                string range = "tape_data";
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, range);
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
                xlh.SelectSheetFromRange("Tape", range);
                xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
                xlt.ClearColumnsExcept("IGNORE");
                xlt.UnhideAllTable();
                xlt.DumpData(tape, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("Failed to Generate Tape.  Error: {0}", ex.Message));
            }
            finally
            {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);
            }

        }
        public static void GenerateTapeInternal()
        {
            try
            {
                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;


                
                string inputAccounts = xlh.GetRange<string>("Inputs", "inputs_accounts");
                List<int> accounts = new List<int>();
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(inputAccounts))
                    accounts = inputAccounts.Split(',').Select(n => System.Convert.ToInt32(n)).ToList();               
                
                XLTable assetFilter = new XLTable(xlh, "Inputs!input_asset_list");
                List<string> assets = assetFilter.AllRows().Select(n => n["asset id"]).Where(n => n != null).Distinct().ToList();

                DateTime cutoff = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>("Inputs", "inputs_cutoff");
                bool blankTrades = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_blank_trades");
                bool blankPrice = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_blank_price");
                bool tradeTD = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_trade_td");
                bool tradeSD = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_trade_sd");
                bool includeZeroPos = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_include_zero_pos");
                bool deleteTradesIfNotInvReported = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_del_trades_not_inv_reported");
                bool processExceptions = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_process_exceptions");
                bool includeExceptions = xlh.GetRange<bool>("Inputs", "inputs_include_exceptions");

                
                XLTable columnsToWrite = new XLTable(xlh, "Inputs!input_columns");

                Fields flds = new Fields(UnlockToolkit.DB, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);

                List<string> columnsToDisplay = new List<string>();
                List<string> columnsToExclude = new List<string>();
                foreach (var row in columnsToWrite.AllRows())
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(row["Include"]) && row["Include"].ToUpper() == "TRUE") 
                        columnsToDisplay.Add(row["Columns"]);
                    else 
                        columnsToExclude.Add(row["Columns"]);



                
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("Generating Tape: Cutoff [{0}]  Accounts [{1}]....", cutoff.ToShortDateString(), inputAccounts));
                DataSet tapeData = GetTapeData(accounts, cutoff, assets, blankTrades, blankPrice, tradeTD, tradeSD, includeZeroPos, deleteTradesIfNotInvReported, processExceptions, includeExceptions);
                if (tapeData == null || tapeData.Tables.Count == 0)
                {
                    UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Failed to Generate Tape.  No Data Returned.");
                    return;
                }
                DataTable tape = tapeData.Tables[0];
                DataTable dataDictionary = (tapeData.Tables.Count > 2) ? tapeData.Tables[2] : null; 

                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("Writing Tape Data: Cutoff [{0}]  Accounts [{1}]....", cutoff.ToShortDateString(), inputAccounts));

                

                string range = "tape_data";
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, range);
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
                xlh.SelectSheetFromRange("Tape", range);
                xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
                xlt.ClearColumnsExcept("IGNORE");
                xlt.UnhideAllTable();
                xlt.RemoveAllButTheseColumns(columnsToDisplay);
                xlt.DumpData(tape, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar, columnsToExclude, flds) ;

                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Removing unrequired columns...");

                
                
                
                
         
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Writing Data Dictionary...");

                

                dataDictionary = dataDictionary.AsEnumerable().Where(n => columnsToDisplay.Contains(n.Field<string>("field").ToUpper()))?.CopyToDataTable();

                string dataDictionaryRange = "data_dictionary";
                XLTable xltDataDict = new XLTable(xlh, dataDictionaryRange);
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
                xlh.SelectSheetFromRange("Data Dictionary", dataDictionaryRange);
                xltDataDict.ClearAllButHeader(1);
                xltDataDict.ClearColumnsExcept("IGNORE");
                xltDataDict.UnhideAllTable();
                xltDataDict.DumpData(dataDictionary, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);


            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {                  
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("Failed to Generate Tape.  Error: {0}", ex.Message));
            }
            finally
            {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateBalanceSheetTape()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            DateTime cutoff = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>("Inputs", "inputs_cutoff");

            DataSet tapeData = GetBalanceSheetTape(cutoff);
            if (tapeData == null || tapeData.Tables.Count == 0)
            {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar("Failed to Generate Tape.  No Data Returned.");
                return;
            }
            DataTable tape = tapeData.Tables[2];

            

            string range = "tape_data";
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, range);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
            xlh.SelectSheetFromRange("Tape", range);
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.ClearColumnsExcept("IGNORE");
            xlt.UnhideAllTable();
            xlt.DumpData(tape, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
        }

        public static DataSet GetMonthEndTapeData(List<int> accounts, DateTime cutoff, List<string> assets, bool blankTrades = true, bool blankPrice = true, bool tradeTD = true, bool tradeSD = false, bool includeZeroPos = true, bool deleteTradesIfNotInvReported = false, bool processExceptions = false, bool includeExceptions = false)
        {
            try
            {
                DataSet tapeData = BadgerLib.Portfolio.GetMontEndTape(UnlockToolkit.DB, accounts, cutoff, assets, blankTrades, blankPrice, tradeTD, tradeSD, includeZeroPos, deleteTradesIfNotInvReported, processExceptions, includeExceptions);
                DataTable tape = tapeData.Tables[0];
                return tapeData;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("Failed to Get Month End Tape Data. Error: {0}", ex.Message));
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static DataSet GetTapeData(List<int> accounts, DateTime cutoff, List<string> assets, bool blankTrades = true , bool blankPrice = true, bool tradeTD = true, bool tradeSD =false, bool includeZeroPos = true, bool deleteTradesIfNotInvReported = false, bool processExceptions = false, bool includeExceptions = false )
        {
            try
            {
                DataSet tapeData = BadgerLib.Portfolio.GetTape(UnlockToolkit.DB, accounts, cutoff, assets, blankTrades, blankPrice, tradeTD, tradeSD, includeZeroPos, deleteTradesIfNotInvReported, processExceptions, includeExceptions);
                DataTable tape = tapeData.Tables[0];
                return tapeData;
            } catch (Exception ex) {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar(string.Format("Failed to Get Tape Data. Error: {0}", ex.Message));
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static DataSet GetBalanceSheetTape(DateTime cutoff)
        {
            DataSet tapeData = BadgerLib.Portfolio.GetBalanceSheetTape(UnlockToolkit.DB,cutoff);
            DataTable tape = tapeData.Tables[0];
            return tapeData;

        }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\TheMath.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class TheMath
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void TestMaxCash()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel, "test_max_cash");
            xlt.ClearColumns("MAX E/R,NET CASH,REJECT NOTE");
            var rows = xlt.AllRows("HOME VALUE");
            ETA eta = new ETA(rows.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            foreach (XLTableRow row in rows)
            {
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "total_debt", row["DEBT"]);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "home_value", row["HOME VALUE"]);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "home_state", row["HOME STATE"]);
                xlh.WriteRangeWithDefaultRangeIfNull(null, "homeowner_fico", row["FICO"], "default_fico");
                xlh.WriteRangeWithDefaultRangeIfNull(null, "homeowner_occupancy", row["OO"],"default_oo");
                row.UpdateFromXLRange("NET CASH", "max_net_cash");
                row.UpdateFromXLRange("MAX E/R", "max_exchange_rate");
                row.UpdateFromXLRange("REJECT NOTE", "reject_note");
                
                eta.IncrementAndReport(null,50);
            }
            xlh.WriteStatusBar("DONE");
                
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Buttons\Watchlist.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{

    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public class Watchlist
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void UpdateWatchlist()
        {

            try
            {
                var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;


                DateTime cutoff = BadgerLib.Utils.GetCutoffDate(UnlockToolkit.DB);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "cutoff", cutoff);

                DataTable watchlist_only = GetWatchlistAssetTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, WHICH_PROBLEMS.WATCHLIST_ONLY);
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "watchlist_summary");
                xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, true);
                xlt.DumpData(watchlist_only, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
                xlt.TightenUpTable("asset_id");

                DataTable concern = GetWatchlistAssetTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, WHICH_PROBLEMS.CONCERN_ONLY);
                XLTable xlc = new XLTable(xlh, "concern_summary");
                xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, true);
                xlc.DumpData(concern, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
                xlc.TightenUpTable("asset_id");

                DataTable all = GetWatchlistAssetTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, WHICH_PROBLEMS.ALL);
                XLTable xld = new XLTable(xlh, "watchlist_detail");
                xld.DumpData(all, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

                List<int> accts = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<int>(null, "accts", true);
                DataTable position_strats = BadgerLib.Portfolio.GetPositionStrats(UnlockToolkit.DB, accts, false);
                XLTable xlp = new XLTable(xlh, "portfolio_summary");
                xlp.ClearColumns("ACCOUNT,INVESTED_DOLLARS");
                xlp.DumpData(position_strats, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
                xlp.TightenUpTable("ACCOUNT");
                xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, false);
            }
            catch(Exception n)
            {
                System.Windows.Forms.MessageBox.Show(n.Message);
            }
        }

        public enum WHICH_PROBLEMS { WATCHLIST_ONLY, CONCERN_ONLY, ALL}
        public static DataTable GetWatchlistAssetTable(string server, WHICH_PROBLEMS p)
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            int i = 0;
            i++;
            string s = i.ToString();
            int months_back = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "months_back");
            
            double threshold_pct = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "threshold_pct");
            double coll_acct_thresh = xlh.GetRange<double>(null, "coll_acct_thresh");
            List<int> accts = xlh.GetRangeListCSV<int>(null, "accts",true);
            DataTable watchlist = BadgerLib.Watchlist.GetWatchlistTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, months_back, threshold_pct, coll_acct_thresh,accts);
            DataTable watchlist_only = watchlist.Copy();
            DataTable concern = watchlist.Copy();
            watchlist_only.FilterRowsNotIn<string>("trg", new List<string>(new string[] { "WATCHLIST" }));
            concern.FilterRowsOut<string>("trg", new List<string>(new string[] { "WATCHLIST" }));

            if (p == WHICH_PROBLEMS.ALL)
                return watchlist;
            if (p == WHICH_PROBLEMS.WATCHLIST_ONLY)
                return watchlist_only;
            if (p == WHICH_PROBLEMS.CONCERN_ONLY)
                return concern;
            return null;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateWatchlistStratsPDF()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strats_do_hpi", false);
            xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strats_do_prepays", false);
            xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strats_do_tape", false); 


            DataTable watchlist_only = GetWatchlistAssetTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, WHICH_PROBLEMS.WATCHLIST_ONLY);
            GenerateWatchlistStratsPDFInternal(watchlist_only, "Watchlist Only");

            DataTable concern_only = GetWatchlistAssetTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, WHICH_PROBLEMS.CONCERN_ONLY);
            GenerateWatchlistStratsPDFInternal(concern_only, "Assets of Concern Only");

            DataTable all = GetWatchlistAssetTable(UnlockToolkit.DB, WHICH_PROBLEMS.ALL);
            GenerateWatchlistStratsPDFInternal(all, "Watchlist + Assets of Concern");
        }
        public static void GenerateWatchlistStratsPDFInternal(DataTable tbl, string file_name_base)
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            DateTime cutoff = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>("Strats", "cutoff");
            string second_base = $"SGALT B + UNLOK + WL1 - {file_name_base}";
            string base_file_name = $"{cutoff.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")} - {second_base}";


            xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strat_desc_override", second_base);

            
            xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strat_accts",null);
            xlh.WriteRange("Strats","strat_base_folder", null);
            

            
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "Strats!strat_asset_filter");
            xlh.WriteRange("Strats", "strat_name_override", file_name_base);
            xlt.DumpData(tbl, true, null);
            Strats.GenerateStrats();
            string base_folder_strats = xlh.GetRange<string>("Strats", "strat_base_folder", false);
            CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh,"Strats", base_file_name, false, base_folder_strats);
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Cashflows.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public static class CashflowLib
    {

       

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static double TotalPrincipal(string ticker, double oface, DateTime settle_1,double cpr,DateTime month_to_pick_flow_from)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsValidInput(ticker))
                return -99999999999;
            return Cashflows.TotalPrincipal(ticker, oface, settle_1, cpr, month_to_pick_flow_from);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object ScheduledPrincipal(string ticker, double oface, DateTime settle_1)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsValidInput(ticker) || (null != ticker && ticker.Substring(0,2).ToUpper() == "T "))
                return "";
            DateTime next_cash = settle_1.AddMonths(1);
            return Assets.Cashflows.GetSingleCashflowNumber<double>("PRINCIPAL PAID",ticker, oface, settle_1, 0,next_cash);
        }
        
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object ScheduledInterest(string ticker, double oface, DateTime settle_1,double cpr,DateTime month_to_pick_flow_from)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsValidInput(ticker) || (null != ticker && ticker.Substring(0,2).ToUpper() == "T "))
                return "";
            
            return Cashflows.ScheduledInterest(ticker, oface, settle_1, cpr, month_to_pick_flow_from);
        }
                
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object ScheduledCoupon(string ticker, double oface, DateTime settle_1,double cpr)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsValidInput(ticker) || (null != ticker && ticker.Substring(0,2).ToUpper() == "T "))
                return "";
            return Cashflows.GetSingleCashflowNumber<double>("COUPON",ticker, oface, settle_1, cpr);
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object ScheduledBalance(string ticker, double oface, DateTime settle_1,double cpr, DateTime? pick_cashflow = null)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsValidInput(ticker) || (null != ticker && ticker.Substring(0,2).ToUpper() == "T "))
                return "";
            return Cashflows.GetSingleCashflowNumber<double>("PRINCIPAL BALANCE",ticker, oface, settle_1, cpr,pick_cashflow);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object[] CashFlowRow(string ticker, double oface, DateTime settle,double cpr)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsValidInput(ticker))
                return null;
            DataRow row = Cashflows.GetSingleCashflowRow(ticker, oface, settle, cpr);
            return row?.ItemArray;
        }

    }
}

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object GetFundingDateHack(string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select max(history.MODIFIED_AT) [latest_modify] from api_activityhistory history, API_APPLICATION app where history.RESOURCE_UUID= app.UUID AND HISTORY.resource_name = 'Application' AND JSON_VALUE(history.new_content, '$.application_state') = 'pending-recording' AND app.EXTERNAL_ID = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.UseCache = true;
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<object>("latest_modify");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object GetBadgerEntryDate(string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select dbo.NYTime(added_to_badger) [added_to_badger] from Assets a where a.id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.UseCache = true;
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<object>("added_to_badger");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FundingDate(string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select funding_date from vClosingEx a where a.ASSET_ID = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.UseCache = true;
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<object>("funding_date");
        }
        [ExcelFunction]

        public static object FundingMatchSingle(string amount)
        {
            string sql = "select date from vBankTrans a where a.amount = @amount";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.UseCache = true;
            q.AddParameter("@amount", amount);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (tbl.Rows.Count == 1)
                return tbl.Rows[0]["date"];
            return "";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void PopulateBulkFundingData()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string funding_acct = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "funding_acct");
            string value_date_str = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetRange<string>(null, "value_date");
            DateTime value_date;
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(value_date_str, out value_date))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Invalid Funding Date");
                return;
            }

            DataTable summary = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetBulkFundingData(UnlockToolkit.DB, true, value_date);
            DataTable funding_email_data = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetBulkFundingData(UnlockToolkit.DB, false, value_date);

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "funding_summary");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(summary, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            
            DataTable clearedge_dt = funding_email_data.Clone();
            foreach (DataRow row in funding_email_data.Rows)
            {
                if (row["TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY"]?.ToString() == "ClearEdge Title")
                    clearedge_dt.ImportRow(row);
            }
            xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "clearedge_breakdown_data");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(clearedge_dt, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            
            DataTable fa_nonhi_dt = funding_email_data.Clone();
            DataTable fa_hi_dt = funding_email_data.Clone();
            foreach (DataRow row in funding_email_data.Rows)
            {
                var title = row["TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY"] as string;
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(title) && title.StartsWith("First American", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                {
                    bool isHI = false;
                    if (funding_email_data.Columns.Contains("is_HI") && row["is_HI"] != DBNull.Value)
                    {
                        object v = row["is_HI"];
                        if (v is bool b) isHI = b;
                        else if (v is byte by) isHI = by != 0;
                        else if (v is short s) isHI = s != 0;
                        else if (v is int i) isHI = i != 0;
                        else if (v is string sv) isHI = sv.Equals("true", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || sv == "1";
                    }

                    if (isHI)
                        fa_hi_dt.ImportRow(row);
                    else
                        fa_nonhi_dt.ImportRow(row);
                }
            }
            
            xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "firstamerican_breakdown_data");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(fa_nonhi_dt, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            
            xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "firstamhi_breakdown_data");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(fa_hi_dt, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            if (funding_acct == "UF2")
                PopulateTCBDrawRequestData();
        }

        public static void PopulateTCBDrawRequestData()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt_unfunded = new XLTable(xlh, "unfunded_assets");
            DataTable dt_unfunded = xlt_unfunded.GetDataTable(true);
            DataColumn dc_asset_id = dt_unfunded.Columns["ASSET_ID"];
            
            List<string> asset_ids = dt_unfunded.AsEnumerable().Select(r => r.Field<string>(dc_asset_id)).Where(s => !string.IsNullOrEmpty(s)).ToList();

            string value_date_str = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetRange<string>(null, "value_date");
            DateTime value_date;
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(value_date_str, out value_date))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Invalid Funding Date");
                return;
            }

            DataTable tcb_draw_data = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetTCBDrawRequestData(UnlockToolkit.DB, value_date, asset_ids);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "tcb_draw_data");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xlt.DumpData(tcb_draw_data, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetFundingBank_Potential_Matches()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "FUNDING_RECON_POTENTIAL_MATCHES");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);

            string used_range = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetActiveReferenceAsRange();
            float Amount = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetRange<float>(null, used_range);
            used_range = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetActiveReferenceAsRange("A");
            string Funding_date_str = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetRange<string>(null, used_range);
            DateTime Funding_date;
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(Funding_date_str, out Funding_date))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Invalid Funding Date");
                return;
            }

            DataTable dt = BadgerLib.Closing.FundingReconPotentialBankTransactions(UnlockToolkit.DB, Funding_date, Amount);
            xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "FUNDING_RECON_POTENTIAL_MATCHES");

            xlt.DumpData(dt, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            xlh.ActivateSheet("Recon_Map_Transaction");
            xlh.FullForceCalc();
        }

        public static void GetFundingBankReconReport_Detail()

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            string Funding_date_str = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetRange<string>(null, used_range);

            DateTime Funding_date;
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(Funding_date_str, out Funding_date))

            xlt.DumpData(dt, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);



            xlh.ActivateSheet("Detail_For_Date");
            xlh.FullForceCalc();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SaveConveyanceTapeAndEmail()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string export = null;
            string ext = ".pdf";

            string file_base = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "mail_filebase");
            string file_type = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "mail_filetype");
            string file_save_location = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "save_directory");

            List<string> sheets = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "mail_sheets", false, "")?.Split(',').ToList();
            string filename = FileLib.GetQuickUniqueFile(file_base, ext, false, false);

            export = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.ExportSelectedSheetStandard(false, sheets,XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.PDF, true, filename);

            
            
            bool saveFile = true;

            string final_full = Path.Combine(file_save_location, file_base + ext);

            if (System.IO.File.Exists(final_full))
            {
                var msg = DXHelper.DXMessageBox.Show("Conveyance tape already exists for today.  Overrwrite?", "Quick Question", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                saveFile = (msg == DialogResult.Yes);   
            }

            if (saveFile)
                UtilsLib.FileLib.CopyFileToDirectorySmartly(filename, file_save_location, true);

            
            Utils.GenericExport();

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetFundingBankReconReport()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string StartDate_str = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "REPORT_START_DATE");
            string EndDate_str = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "REPORT_END_DATE");
            DateTime StartDate, EndDate;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "FUNDING_RECON_REPORT");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);

            if (!DateTime.TryParse(StartDate_str, out StartDate))
            { 
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Invalid Start Date");
                return;
            }

            if (!DateTime.TryParse(EndDate_str, out EndDate))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Invalid End Date");
                return;
            }

            string sql = "exec sp_Funding_Bank_Recon_Report @StartDate, @EndDate";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.UseCache = true;
            q.AddParameter("@StartDate", StartDate);
            q.AddParameter("@EndDate", EndDate);
            DataTable dt = q.ExecuteTable();

            xlt.DumpData(dt, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            
        }

        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "DocGen Generic", MenuText = "Lets go...")]
        public static void DocGeneGeneric()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "docgen_table");
            List<string> errors = new List<string>();
            
            var rows = xlt.AllRows("TEMPLATE");
            if (xlt.ContainsColumn("ERROR"))
                xlt.ClearColumn("ERROR");
            bool spawn_when_done = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "docgen_spawn_when_done", true, false);

            UtilsLib.ETA eta = new UtilsLib.ETA(rows.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            var f = Fields.GetInstance(UnlockToolkit.DB, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            foreach (XLTableRow row in rows)
            {
                try
                {

                    Dictionary<string, object> doc_vars = new Dictionary<string, object>();
                    foreach (var col in xlt._header_indexes)
                    {
                        if (col.Key.ContainsIns("V_"))
                        {
                            string var = col.Key.Substring(2, col.Key.Length - 2);
                            doc_vars.Add(var, row[col.Key]);
                        }
                    }
                    string source_file = row["TEMPLATE"];
                    string full_destination_filename = row["FINAL NAME"];
                    List<string> errors_local = new List<string>();

                    
                    errors_local = UtilsLib.Docs.GenerateDoc(doc_vars, source_file, full_destination_filename, f,null);
                    errors.AddRange(errors_local);
                }
                catch (Exception n)
                {
                    errors.Add(n.Message);
                }
                finally
                {
                    string error_long = String.Join(" | ", errors.ToArray());
                    row.Update("ERROR", error_long);
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();
                }
            }
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Finito.");
        }


        public static string GenerateQuickPDFInternal(bool spawn_directory,bool spawn_file,bool silent)
        {
            string pdf = null;
            try
            {
                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                string base_directory = Path.GetTempPath();
                string base_filename = xlh.GetActiveFilenameOnlyNoExtension();
                string file_base = base_filename + " - TEMP";
                if (xlh.RangeExistsAndPopulated("pdf_name"))
                    file_base = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "pdf_name");
                pdf = Path.Combine(base_directory, file_base) + ".pdf";
                if (File.Exists(pdf))
                    File.Delete(pdf);
                
                string[] csv_worksheets = new string[] { xlh.ActiveWorksheetName() };
                if (xlh.RangeExists("quickpdf_sheets"))
                    csv_worksheets = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "quickpdf_sheets").Split(',');
                xlh.SaveWorksheetAsPDF(csv_worksheets.ToList(), pdf, false);                             

                if (spawn_file)
                {
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnAsync(pdf);
                }
                if (spawn_directory)
                {
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(pdf, true);
                }
            }
            catch(Exception n)
            {
                if(!silent)
                    XtraMessageBox.Show(n.Message,"Uh oh...");
            }

            return pdf;
        }

        public static string GenerateQuickPDFInternal(bool spawn_directory, bool spawn_file, bool silent, bool draft)
        {
            if (!draft)
                return GenerateQuickPDFInternal(spawn_directory, spawn_file, silent);
            
            string pdf = null;
            try
            {
                XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                string base_directory = Path.GetTempPath();
                string base_filename = xlh.GetActiveFilenameOnlyNoExtension();
                string file_base = base_filename + " - TEMP";
                if (xlh.RangeExistsAndPopulated("pdf_name"))
                    file_base = "DRAFT - " + xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "pdf_name");
                pdf = Path.Combine(base_directory, file_base) + ".pdf";
                if (File.Exists(pdf))
                    File.Delete(pdf);
                string[] csv_worksheets = new string[] { xlh.ActiveWorksheetName() };
                if (xlh.RangeExists("quickpdf_sheets"))
                    csv_worksheets = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "quickpdf_sheets").Split(',');
                xlh.SaveWorksheetAsPDF(csv_worksheets.ToList(), pdf, false, true);

                if (spawn_file)
                {
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnAsync(pdf);
                }
                if (spawn_directory)
                {
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(pdf, true);
                }
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                if (!silent)
                    XtraMessageBox.Show(n.Message, "Uh oh...");
            }

            return pdf;
        }

        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "Trash", MenuText = "Copy Underwriting")]
        public static void CopyUnderwriting()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            


            
            string macro = @"c:\TEMP\File Worksheets - Macros.xlsm";
            string source = @"C:\File Worksheets-BEFORE\";
            

            string destination = @"C:\Users\DanFoster\Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\05 - Initiatives\File Worksheet Underwriting-AFTER\";
            



            string search_pattern = "00 - File Worksheet -*.xlsx";
            
            
            
            
            
            var files = Directory.GetFiles(source,search_pattern,SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            UtilsLib.ETA eta = new UtilsLib.ETA(files.Count(), xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            foreach (string filew in files)
            {
                
                
                
                
                string file = filew;
                if (file.Contains(".bak."))
                    continue;
                
                string backup_name = Path.Combine(Path.GetDirectoryName(file), Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(file) + $".bak.xlsx");

                File.Copy(file, backup_name,true);
                xlh.OpenSheet(file, true);
                string workbook_name = xlh.ActiveWorkbookName();
                xlh.OpenSheet(macro,true);
                string macro_workbook = xlh.ActiveWorkbookName();
                eta.IncrementAndReport();

                bool sheet_exists = xlh.SheetExists(workbook_name,"Underwriting");
                if (sheet_exists)
                {
                    xlh.ActivateWorkbook(workbook_name);
                    xlh.ActivateSheet("Underwriting");
                    string check_if_upgraded = xlh.GetRange<string>("Underwriting", "B139");
                    if(null != check_if_upgraded && check_if_upgraded.Contains("Los Angeles"))
                    {
                        xlh.CloseWorkbook(workbook_name, false);
                        xlh.CloseWorkbook(macro_workbook, false);
                        continue;
                    }
                    string comments = xlh.GetRange<string>("Underwriting", "I122");
                    if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(comments))
                    {

                    }

                    xlh.ActivateWorkbook(macro_workbook);
                    xlh.CutRangeToClipboard(null, "'Underwriting'!B118:N324");
                    object before = null;
                    


                    xlh.ActivateWorkbook(workbook_name);
                    
                    xlh.ActivateRange("Underwriting", "B121");

                    object ICS_homeValue_before = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "ICS_homeValue", false, null, false);
                    object ICS_finalCostAppraisal_before = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "ICS_finalCostAppraisal", false, null, false);
                    object property_legal_description_before = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "property_legal_description", false, null, false);
                    object ICS_finalCostInspection_before = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "ICS_finalCostInspection", false, null, false);
                    

                    xlh.SelectAndPasteFromCut("Underwriting", "B118");
                    xlh.CreateNamedRange("Underwriting", "C121", "ICS_homeValue");
                    xlh.CreateNamedRange("Underwriting", "C122", "ICS_finalCostAppraisal");
                    xlh.CreateNamedRange("Underwriting", "C131", "property_legal_description");
                    xlh.CreateNamedRange("Underwriting", "C143", "ICS_finalCostInspection");

                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "ICS_homeValue", ICS_homeValue_before);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "ICS_finalCostAppraisal", ICS_finalCostAppraisal_before);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "property_legal_description", property_legal_description_before);
                    xlh.WriteRange(null, "ICS_finalCostInspection", ICS_finalCostInspection_before);

                    xlh.WriteRange("Underwriting", "I119", comments);
                    xlh.SetWordWrap("Underwriting", "I119", true);
                }
                else
                {

                    xlh.CopySheetToDiffWorkbook(macro_workbook,workbook_name, "Underwriting", "Underwriting",false);
                    xlh.ClearAllLinkedNameRanges();
                    xlh.RemoveExternalLinksFromFormulas();
                }
                string filename_only = Path.GetFileName(file);
                string dest_location = Path.Combine(destination, filename_only);

                
                xlh.ActivateWorkbook(workbook_name);
                
                xlh.SaveActiveWorkbook();

                xlh.CloseWorkbook(workbook_name,false);
                xlh.ActivateWorkbook(macro_workbook);
                xlh.CloseWorkbook(macro_workbook, false);
                
                
                
            }
            }

        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "Trash", MenuText = "Unlock Insurance")]
        public static void Insurance()
        {
            string source_real = @"C:\Users\DanFoster\Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\02 - Assets\";
            string search_pattern = "*Unlock*mortgage*";
            var files = Directory.GetFiles(source_real, search_pattern, SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            List<string> list_of_files = new List<string>();
            foreach (string filew in files)
            {
                string directory = Path.GetFileName(Path.GetDirectoryName(filew));
                if (!list_of_files.Contains(directory))
                    list_of_files.Add(directory);
            }

            string all = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, list_of_files);
        }

        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "Trash", MenuText = "Beat Paul")]
        public static void BeatPaul()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            
            
            
            
            
            string source_real = @"C:\Users\DanFoster\Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\02 - Assets\";
            
            
            
            string search_pattern = "00 - File Worksheet -*.xlsx";
            string output_file = @"C:\trash\answer.txt";
            
            
            string header = "asset_id\tpartner_email\tpartner_commission\tpartner_name\tpartner_company";
            File.WriteAllText(output_file, header);

                    continue;

                {

                    string just_folder = Path.GetFileName(directory).Replace("Â"," ");
  
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    {
                      
                    }
                }
                catch { continue; }

                xlh.ToggleDisplayAlerts(false);
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
                xlh.OpenSheet(file, true);

                pipeline_id = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetPipelineIdFromLabel(UnlockToolkit.DB, label, true, true);

                bool range_exists = xlh.RangeExists("ICS_final_offerInvestment");

                
                string directory_name = filename_only.Replace("00 - File Worksheet - ", "");
                string directory_name_full = Path.Combine(source_real , directory_name + @"\");
                string directory_name_one_back = "";
                



                DateTime? createDate = null;
                DateTime? last_modified = null;

                object ie_fico = xlh.GetRange <object>(null, "IE_fico");
                object secured_debt = xlh.GetRange<object>(null, "property_unpaid_principle_balance_estimated");

                object avm_variation = xlh.GetRange<object>(null, "'Deal Structuring'!C17", false);
                object avm_confidence = xlh.GetRange<object>(null, "'Deal Structuring'!C18", false);
                object appraised_home_value = xlh.GetRange<object>(null, "ICS_homeValue", false);
                object exchange_rate = xlh.GetRange<object>(null, "IE_override_offerEr", false);
                string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "property_apn", false);
                string name = xlh.GetRange<string>("Closing Statement", "H5", false);
                string uam_commentary_1 = xlh.GetRange<string>("Deal Structuring", "I30", false);
                string uam_commentary_2 = xlh.GetRange<string>("Deal Structuring", "I31", false);
                string uam_commentary = uam_commentary_1;
                if (null == uam_commentary)
                    uam_commentary = uam_commentary_2;
                string sales_commentary = xlh.GetRange<string>("Deal Structuring", "E26", false);
                string escrow_file_num = xlh.GetRange<string>("Underwriting", "O43", false);
                string legal_description = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "property_legal_description", false);
                string outreach_link = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "outreach_link", false);
                string partner_email = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "partnerEmail", false);
                string partner_commission = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "'UAM Import'!E30", false);
                string partner_name = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "partnerName", false);
                string partner_company = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "partnerCompany", false);

                DateTime? first_contact = null;
                string monday_group = null;

                double? avm_convidence_high = null;
                if (null != avm_confidence && avm_confidence.ToString().Split('-').Length == 2)
                {
                    double high;
                    double low;
                    Double.TryParse(avm_confidence.ToString().Split('-')[1].Trim(), out high);
                    Double.TryParse(avm_confidence.ToString().Split('-')[0].Trim(), out low);
                    avm_convidence_low = low;
                    avm_convidence_high = high;

                if (null != pipeline_id)
                {
                    monday_stage = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetAttributeInternal<string>(UnlockToolkit.DB, pipeline_id.Value, "sub_stage");
                    first_contact = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetAttributeInternal<DateTime?>(UnlockToolkit.DB, pipeline_id.Value, "first_contact");

                    outreach_id = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetAttributeInternal<int?>(UnlockToolkit.DB, pipeline_id.Value, "internal_id");

                }

                {
                    string[] file_attr = Directory.GetFiles(source_real, filename_only + ".xlsx",SearchOption.AllDirectories);

  
                    if (null != file_attr && file_attr.Length == 1)
                    {
                        FileInfo fi = new FileInfo(file_attr[0]);
                        createDate = fi.CreationTime;
                        last_modified = fi.LastWriteTime;
                        directory_name_one_back = Directory.GetParent(fi.FullName).Parent.Name;
                    }
                }


                xlh.ToggleAppVisible(true);
                
                
                string output = $"{asset_id}\t{partner_email}\t{partner_commission}\t{partner_name}\t{partner_company}";

                File.AppendAllText(output_file, output + Environment.NewLine);

                
                
                
                
                
                
                xlh.CloseWorkbook(null, false);
            }
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!");
        }


       

        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "Trash", MenuText = "Update Valuations")]
        public static void UpdateValuations()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string source = @"w:\Valuations\";

            var files = Directory.GetFiles(source, "*", SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            UtilsLib.ETA eta = new UtilsLib.ETA(files.Count(), xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            try
            {
                foreach (string filew in files)
                {
                    string file = filew;

                    
                    xlh.OpenSheet(file, true);

                    eta.IncrementAndReport();

                    bool range_exists = xlh.RangeExists("avmCorelogicConsumerOrderId");

                    if (range_exists)
                    {

                        FileWorksheet.SetupFundingSheetNEW();


                        bool agreement_id_exists = xlh.RangeExists(null, "'UAM IMPORT'!UAM_AGREEMENT_NUM");
                        if (!agreement_id_exists)
                        {
                            xlh.CloseWorkbook(null, false);
                            continue;
                        }

                        string asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "'UAM IMPORT'!UAM_AGREEMENT_NUM");
                        if (null == asset_id)
                        {
                            xlh.CloseWorkbook(null, false); ;
                            continue;
                        }
                        bool valuations_exist = BadgerLib.Valuations.ValuationsExistHack(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);

                        if (!valuations_exist)
                            BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_9", true);

                    }
                    BadgerXLHelper.XLBadger.DoSimpleQuery(xlh, UnlockToolkit.DB, "uam_insert_10", true);
                    xlh.CloseWorkbook(null, false);
                }
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n);
            }
        }

        [ExcelCommand(MenuText = "Breakout Sheet")]
        public static void BreakOutSheet()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string breakout_range = xlh.GetRange<string>(null,"breakout_range");
            string breakout_column = xlh.GetRange<string>(null,"breakout_column");
            string breakout_print = null;
            if (xlh.RangeExists("breakout_print"))
                breakout_print = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "breakout_print");
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, breakout_range);
            List<string> ranges = xlt.UniqueValues<string>(breakout_column, true, false).ToList();

            List<string> breakout_tables = new List<string>();
            if (xlh.RangeExists("breakout_tables"))
                breakout_tables = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "breakout_tables").Split(',').ToList();

            Dictionary<string, string> breakout_hides = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            if (xlh.RangeExists("breakout_hides"))
                breakout_hides = xlh.GetDictionary("breakout_hides");

            string full_filename_orig = xlh.GetActiveFilename();
            string base_directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(full_filename_orig);
            string ext = Path.GetExtension(full_filename_orig);
            string base_filename = xlh.GetActiveFilenameOnlyNoExtension();
            string breakout_title_range_orig = null;
            if (xlh.RangeExists("breakout_field"))
                breakout_title_range_orig = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "breakout_field");
            
           
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "breakout_field", null);
            foreach (string unique in ranges)
            {
                xlh.OpenSheet(full_filename_orig, true);
                xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
                string unique_file = UtilsLib.Clean.CleanFilename(unique, true);
                string file_base = base_filename + " - " + unique_file;
                string new_filename_full = Path.Combine(base_directory, file_base) + ext;
                XLTable local_tbl = new XLTable(xlh, breakout_range);
                local_tbl.SetWriter(xlh.WriteStatusBar);


                xlh.WriteRange(null, "breakout_field", unique);

                List<string> others = ranges.ToArray().ToList();
                others.Remove(unique);
                local_tbl.ActivateWorksheet();
                local_tbl.DeleteAllRowsContaining(breakout_column, others );

                
                xlh.FullForceCalc();

                foreach (string table in breakout_tables)
                {
                    if(!xlh.RangeExists(table))
                        continue;
                    XLTable tbl_break = new XLTable(xlh, table);
                    tbl_break.ActivateWorksheet();
                    tbl_break.UnhideAllTable();
                    foreach (KeyValuePair<string,string> hide in breakout_hides)
                    {
                        tbl_break.HideRowsContaining(hide.Key, new List<string>(new string[] {hide.Value}));
                    }
                }

                if (null != breakout_print)
                {
                    xlh.ActivateSheet(breakout_print);
                    string pdf = Path.Combine(base_directory, file_base) + ".pdf";
                    if (File.Exists(pdf))
                        File.Delete(pdf);
                    xlh.SaveWorksheetAsPDF(breakout_print, pdf, false);
                }

                if (File.Exists(new_filename_full))
                    File.Delete(new_filename_full);
                xlh.SaveActiveWorkbookAs(new_filename_full, true);
                string active_wb_name = xlh.ActiveWorkbookName();
                xlh.CloseWorkbook(active_wb_name, false);
                
            }

            
            
            
        }

        
        public static void ArchiveActiveSheetInternal(bool display_alerts)
        {
            string archive_dir = Path.Combine(System.IO.Path.GetDirectoryName(UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetActiveFilename()), "Archive");
            if(!Directory.Exists(archive_dir))
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(archive_dir);
            }
            string location = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.ArchiveActiveSheet(archive_dir);
            if(display_alerts)
                XtraMessageBox.Show(location, "Archived");
        }

        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "Normalize", MenuText = "Selected Ranges")]
        public static void NormalizeRange()
        {
            Dictionary<string, object> maps = Assets.Mapping.GetMappingTable(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            string active = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetSelectedRangeNameUsed();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.NormalizeRange(null, active, maps, null);
        }

        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "Normalize", MenuText = "Selected Ranges - Proper Case")]
        public static void NormalizeRangeProperCase()
        {
            Dictionary<string, object> maps = Assets.Mapping.GetMappingTable(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            string active = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetSelectedRangeNameUsed();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.NormalizeRange(null, active, maps,Extensions.StringHelper.TitleCase);
        }
        [ExcelCommand(MenuName = "Normalize", MenuText = "Selected Ranges - Upper Case")]
        public static void NormalizeRangeUpper()
        {
            Dictionary<string, object> maps = Assets.Mapping.GetMappingTable(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            string active = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.GetSelectedRangeNameUsed();
            UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.NormalizeRange(null, active, maps, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentCulture.TextInfo.ToUpper);
        }
    }

namespace Unlock_Toolkit

    public static class Convert
