        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object TicDec(string price_in_tics)
        {
            Nullable<double> px = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.TicDec(price_in_tics);
            if (null == px)
                return "";
            return px.Value;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object CreateVector(double[] nums,string format)
        {
            List<string> vector = new List<string>();
            foreach(double d in nums)
            {
                string fmt = d.ToString(format);
                vector.Add(fmt);
            }
            return String.Join(" ", vector.ToArray());
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object SMMtoCPR(double smm)
        {
            return UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.SMMtoCPR(smm);
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object HedgeMapFull(string cusip)
        {
            return MapHedgeInternal(cusip, true);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object MapHedge(string cusip)
        {
            return MapHedgeInternal(cusip, false);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string FullCusip(string cusip)
        {
            string final = UtilsLib.Validate.CalcCusipCheckDigit(cusip);
            return $"{final}".Trim();
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object PickHeader(string[] values,string[] headers)
        {
            if (values.Length != headers.Length)
                throw new Exception("Wrong Length");
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Length; i++)
            {
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(values[i]))
                    return headers[i];
            }

            return "";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FirstNonBlank(string[] values)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Length; i++)
            {
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(values[i]))
                    return values[i];
            }
            return "";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object AssetIDToUSB(string usb_key)
        {
            return USBankUtils.CollateralKeyToAssetId(UnlockToolkit.DB, usb_key);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FirstNonZero(string[] values)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Length; i++)
            {
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(values[i]) && values[i] != "0")
                    return values[i];
            }
            return "";
        }



        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FirstNegativeZeroBasedIndex(double[] values)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Length; i++)
            {
                if (values[i] < 0)
                    return i;
            }
            return "";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FirstFalseZeroBasedIndex(object[] values)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Length; i++)
            {
                bool b;
                if (Boolean.TryParse(values[i].ToString(), out b))
                {
                    if(!b)
                        return i;
                }
            }
            return "";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FirstTrueZeroBasedIndex(object[] values)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Length; i++)
            {
                bool b;
                if (Boolean.TryParse(values[i].ToString(), out b))
                {
                    if (b)
                        return i;
                }
            }
            return "";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object Clean(string value)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
                return "";
            else
                return value.Trim();
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object ToBool(string value)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(value))
                return "";
            value = value.ToUpper();
            List<string> trues = new List<string>();
            trues.Add("TRUE");
            trues.Add("YES");
            if (trues.Contains(value))
                return true;
            return false;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object LastNonBlank(string[] values)
        {
            for (int i = values.Length; i != 0; i--)
            {
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(values[i]))
                    return values[i];
            }
            return "";
        }

            return UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.PriceTalkToPrice(talk);
        }


        
        
        
        
        


        [ExcelFunction]

        public static object VectorConvertSMM(string str, int one_based_position, string num_format = null)
        {
            double num = (double)VectorConvert(str, one_based_position, num_format);

            return UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.CPRtoSMM(num);
        }

            [ExcelFunction]

        public static object VectorConvert(string str,int one_based_position,string num_format = null)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(str))
                return null;
            double test;
            int length = 600;
            str = str.ToUpper();
            str = str.Replace("\t", " ");

            List<double> ret = new List<double>();
            
                ret.AddRange(UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.RampToVector(str, length));
            
            
            
            

            if (ret.Count == 0)
                return -99999999999;
            if(ret.Count <= length)
            {
                double last = ret[ret.Count-1];
                for(int i = ret.Count; i != length;i++)
                {
                    ret.Add(last);
                }
            }
            if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(num_format))
            {
                double raw_dog = ret[one_based_position - 1];
                string num = raw_dog.ToString(num_format);
                return num;
            }


            return ret[one_based_position-1];

        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object IntexRampToBBG(string intex_ramp)
        {
            if (intex_ramp.Split(' ').Length <= 3)
                return intex_ramp;
            string start_value = intex_ramp.Split(' ')[0];
            string over_how_many = intex_ramp.Split(' ')[2];
            string final_value = intex_ramp.Split(' ')[3];
            string value =  $"{start_value} {over_how_many}R {final_value}";
            
            
            return value;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object NormalizeHedge(string name, string[] shelf_range)
        {
            foreach(string s in shelf_range)
            {
                if(name.Split(' ').Length > 1 && name.Split(' ')[0].ToString().ToUpper().Contains(s.ToUpper()))
                {
                    string last = name.Split(' ')[name.Split(' ').Length-1];
                    string first = name.Substring(0, name.LastIndexOf(' ')).Trim();
                    double d;
                    if(Double.TryParse(last, out d))
                    {
                        return String.Format("{0} {1:0.0}", first, d);
                    }
                }
            }
            return name.ToUpper();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object Map(object val)
        {
            Dictionary<string, object> maps = Assets.Mapping.GetMappingTable(UnlockToolkit.DB);
            if (null != val)
            {
                if (maps.ContainsKey(val.ToString()))
                    return maps[val.ToString()];
            }
            return val;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object MapHedgeInternal(string cusip,bool full)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsCusip(cusip))
                return "";
            if (cusip.Substring(0, 3) == "912")
            {
                
                double years_to_maturity = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<double>(cusip + " govt", "MTY_YEARS_TDY"); 
                int round = (int)Math.Round(years_to_maturity, 0);
                return "GT" + round;
            }
            else
            {
                string collat_type = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<string>(cusip + " mtge", "COLLAT_TYP");
                double cpn = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<double>(cusip + " mtge", "cpn");
                string tba = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<string>(cusip + " mtge", "SECURITY_TYP2");
                if (tba != "TBA")
                    return "";
                if(full)
                {
                    DateTime settle = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<DateTime>(cusip + " mtge", "FIRST_SETTLE_DT");
                    return String.Format("{0} {1:0.0} {2:M/yy}", collat_type, cpn, settle);
                }
                return String.Format("{0} {1:0.0}", collat_type, cpn);
            }
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object SurvivalToAgeBasedCPR(double survivalRate, int age)
        {
            return UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.SurvivalToAgeBasedCPR(survivalRate, age);
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object SelectOnlyNumbers(string obj)
        {
            return UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyNumbers(obj);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object CPRtoSMM(double cpr)
        {
            return UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.CPRtoSMM(cpr);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object DecTic(double price)
        
        {
            if (Math.Abs(price) < .0000000001)
                price = 0;
            return UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.DecTic(price);
        }
    }

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public static class CreditLibHelper
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void MapDebt(int debt_id, int craccount_id)
        {
            BadgerLib.Debt.MapCreditTradeLine(UnlockToolkit.DB, debt_id, craccount_id);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetDebtLienData()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var asset_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "asset_id");
            System.Data.DataTable lienData = BadgerLib.Debt.GetLienData(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            XL.XLTable xlt = new XL.XLTable(xlh, "lienData");
            xlt.DumpData(lienData, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar, null);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static int InsertCRQueues(int filenum,int applicant_id,string applicant_co_id,DateTime? asOf)
        {
            int? queue = CreditLib.Queue.QueueExistsFromFileNum(UnlockToolkit.DB,filenum);
            if(null == queue)
                queue = CreditLib.Queue.InsertQueue(UnlockToolkit.DB, filenum, 1, applicant_id, applicant_co_id.AsInt(), null, "Pending", "Manual Entry",asOf);
            var s = CreditLib.Load.FileNumExists(UnlockToolkit.DB,filenum);
            if (!s)
            {
                CreditLib.CreditReport c = new CreditReport();
                c.InsertCreditFile(UnlockToolkit.DB, filenum, null);
            }
            return null == queue ? -1 : queue.Value;
        }



        
        
        
        
        

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void BackfilleFile(int filenum, string applicants)
        {
            bool exists = CreditLib.Load.FileNumExists(UnlockToolkit.DB, filenum);
            if(!exists && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(applicants))
            {
                int applicant_id = applicants.Split('|')[0].AsInt().Value;
                int? applicant_co_id = null;
                if (applicants.Split('|').Length == 2)
                    applicant_co_id = applicants.Split('|')[1].AsInt().Value;
                CreditLib.Queue.InsertQueue(UnlockToolkit.DB, filenum, 1, applicant_id, applicant_co_id, null, "pending", null,null);
            }
            
        }

        }

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    internal static class Custody
    {
        
        [ExcelFunction(Name = "Collateral_Status_USBank")]
        public static string Collateral_Status_USBank(string asset_id)
        {
            DataTable dt = new DataTable();
            dt = BadgerLib.Custody.Collateral_Status_USBank(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            return dt.Rows[0]["collateral_exist_status_code"].ToString()+", "+ dt.Rows[0]["release_notation"].ToString() + ", " + dt.Rows[0]["request_date"].ToString();
        }

        
        [ExcelFunction(Name = "Collateral_Status_WSFS")]
        public static object CollateralStatus_WSFS(string asset_id)
        {
            DataTable dt = new DataTable();
            dt = BadgerLib.Custody.Collateral_Status_WSFS(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id);
            string retval = "";
            if (dt.Rows.Count == 0)
                retval = "Asset ID Not Found";
            else
            {
                retval = dt.Rows[0]["WSFS_Certification_Status"].ToString();
                if (retval.ToLower() == "not certified")
                {
                    DateTime sla_date = new DateTime();
                    DateTime.TryParse(dt.Rows[0]["SLA_Certifcation_Date"].ToString(), out sla_date);
                    retval += " ETA " + sla_date.ToShortDateString();
                }
            }


            return retval;
        }
    }
}

        {

            DateTime asOf = DateTime.FromOADate(s);

            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime xd = new UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime(asOf);

            return xd.Date;

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object AddBdays(Nullable<DateTime> asOf, int biz_days)
        {
            
            
            if (null == asOf)
                asOf = DateTime.Today;

            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime xd = new UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime(asOf.Value);
            xd.AddBusinessDays(biz_days);
            return xd.Date;
        }





        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object ConvertTD(string str,Nullable<DateTime> asOf)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(str))
                return "<input error>";
            string clean = str.ToUpper().Trim().Replace(":","");
            int days = -9999;

            if(clean.Contains("T+") || clean.Contains("T-"))
            {
                if (clean.Contains('+'))
                    days = System.Convert.ToInt32(clean.Split('+')[1]);
                else
                    days = -System.Convert.ToInt32(clean.Split('-')[1]);
            }
 
            if (clean.Contains("PREV"))
                days = -1;
            if (clean.Contains("LIVE"))
                days = 0;
            if (null == asOf)
                asOf = DateTime.Today;

            if (days == -9999)
                return str;
            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime xd = new UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime(asOf.Value);
            xd.AddBusinessDays(days);
            return xd.Date;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FormatDate(string raw, string date_format)
        {
            return DateTime.ParseExact(raw, date_format, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]

        public static object CheckIfBDayOrGetNext(DateTime start)
        {
            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime xd = new UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime(start);
            return xd.CheckIfBDayorGetNext();
 
            
        }

        }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\DBUtils.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public static class DBUtils
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void TestDB()
        {
            Query q = new Query("select @@version", "test942.database.windows.net");
            var table = q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string ColumnName([ExcelArgument(AllowReference = true)] object rng)
        {
            ExcelReference r = (ExcelReference)rng;
            return UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.ColumnNumberToLetter(r.ColumnFirst);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string CreateDBTable(string table_name, object[,] table)
        {
            System.Data.DataTable sc14matrix = UtilsLib.Excel.ArrayToDataTable(table, true);
            UtilsLib.GenerateSchema g = new UtilsLib.GenerateSchema();
            UtilsLib.TableClass t = new UtilsLib.TableClass(typeof(double));

            return t.CreateTableScript(table_name, sc14matrix.DataSet);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string GenerateFunctionFromTable(string table, string base_object, string key)
        {
            
            

            string sql = $"select * from {table} where 1=2";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            Dictionary<string, string> columns = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            List<string> ignores = new List<string>(new string[] { "update_by", "update_time", "id" });
            Dictionary<string, string> db_columns = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            foreach (DataColumn col in t.Columns)
            {
                if (!ignores.Contains(col.Caption))
                {
                    columns.Add(col.Caption, col.DataType.FullName.Replace("System.", "").ToLower() + (!col.DataType.IsOfNullableType() ? "?" : ""));
                    string db_type = Database.DBUtils.FindDBTypeForSQL(col.DataType);
                    db_columns.Add(col.Caption, db_type.ToString().ToLower());
                }
            }


            string declaration = $"public static void InsertUpdate{table}(string server,";

            string insert_function = $"\tstring sql = \"insert into {table} (@{String.Join(",", columns.Keys)}) values ({String.Join(", @", columns.Keys)})\";";

            string add_params = "\tQuery q = new Query(sql,server);" + Environment.NewLine;


            string row_get_values = "";
            string update_string = $"\t
            string call_function = "MyFunction(";
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, string> col in columns)
            {
                declaration += col.Value + " " + col.Key + ",";
                add_params += $"\tq.AddParameter(\"@{col.Key}\", {base_object}{col.Key.Replace("?", "")});" + Environment.NewLine;

                update_string += $"a.{col.Key}=@{col.Key}, ";
                if (col.Value.ContainsIns("string"))
                    row_get_values += $"string {col.Key} = row[\"{col.Key}\"] as string;{Environment.NewLine}";
                else
                    row_get_values +=
                        $"{col.Value} {col.Key} = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.NullIfNot<{col.Value.Replace("?", "")}>(row[\"{col.Key}\"]);{Environment.NewLine}";

                call_function += col.Key + ",";
            }

            call_function = call_function.Substring(0, call_function.Length - 1) + ");" + Environment.NewLine;

            update_string = update_string.Substring(0, update_string.Length - 1) + $" from  {table} where {key} = @{key}";

            declaration = declaration.Substring(0, declaration.Length - 1) + ")" + Environment.NewLine + "{" + Environment.NewLine;

            add_params += "\tq.Execute();" + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine;

            add_params += "}" + Environment.NewLine;
            string proc = $"

            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, string> kvp in db_columns)
            {
                proc += $"@{kvp.Key} {kvp.Value},";
            }

            proc = proc.Substring(0, proc.Length - 1) + $"{Environment.NewLine}as{Environment.NewLine}begin{Environment.NewLine}{Environment.NewLine}END{Environment.NewLine}";


            string final_answer = declaration + insert_function + Environment.NewLine + add_params +
                                  Environment.NewLine + update_string + Environment.NewLine + proc +
                                  Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + row_get_values + Environment.NewLine +
                                  Environment.NewLine + call_function;
            string temp = Path.GetTempFileName();
            File.WriteAllText(temp, final_answer);
            return temp;
        }



    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Funding.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class Funding
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetAssetsOnLineSummary()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "funding_summary_data");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);

            DateTime startDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "funding_start_date");
            DateTime endDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "funding_end_date");

            DataTable dtFundingSummary = new DataTable();
            dtFundingSummary.Columns.Add("Date", typeof(DateTime));
            dtFundingSummary.Columns.Add("Asset Count", typeof(int));
            dtFundingSummary.Columns.Add("Funded Investment Payment", typeof(double));
            dtFundingSummary.Columns.Add("Advance", typeof(double));
            dtFundingSummary.Columns.Add("Margin", typeof(double));
            dtFundingSummary.Columns.Add("Daily Funding", typeof(double));
            dtFundingSummary.Columns.Add("Trade Settle", typeof(double));


            for (DateTime fundingDate = startDate; fundingDate <= endDate; fundingDate = (DateTime)Dates.NextBday(fundingDate))
            {
                DataTable dt = BadgerLib.Fundings.GetUF2FundedAssets(UnlockToolkit.DB, fundingDate, true);
                if (!(dt is null) && dt.Rows.Count == 1)
                {
                    DataRow dr = dtFundingSummary.NewRow();
                    dr["Date"] = fundingDate;
                    dr["Asset Count"] = dt.Rows[0]["count"];
                    dr["Funded Investment Payment"] = dt.Rows[0]["Funded Investment Payment"];
                    dr["Advance"] = dt.Rows[0]["Advance Amount"];
                    dr["Margin"] = dt.Rows[0]["Margin Amount"];
                    dr["Daily Funding"] = dt.Rows[0]["Daily Funding"];
                    dr["Trade Settle"] = dt.Rows[0]["Trade Settle"];

                    dtFundingSummary.Rows.Add(dr);
                }
            }


            xlt.DumpData(dtFundingSummary, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("Date");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetAssetsOnLineForDate()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "funding_by_day_data");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(1);

            DateTime fundingDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "funding_date");

            DataTable dtFundedByDate = BadgerLib.Fundings.GetUF2FundedAssets(UnlockToolkit.DB, fundingDate, false);

            xlt.DumpData(dtFundedByDate, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("ASSET_ID");

        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetAssetMonthlyFundingBreakdown()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xltFundingData = new XLTable(xlh, "funding_data");
            XLTable xltFundingSummary = new XLTable(xlh, "funding_summary");

            xltFundingData.ClearAllButHeader(1);
            xltFundingSummary.ClearAllButHeader(1);

            DateTime month = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "input_month");

            DataSet funding = BadgerLib.Fundings.GetAssetMonthlyFundingBreakdown(UnlockToolkit.DB, month);

            xltFundingData.DumpData(funding.Tables[0], false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xltFundingSummary.DumpData(funding.Tables[1], false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xltFundingSummary.TightenUpTable("app_submit_month");


            
                }
    }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Generic.cs ---
using static DevExpress.XtraPrinting.Native.ExportOptionsPropertiesNames;


namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class Generic
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void RunGenericSql()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var sql = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "sql");
            var outputRange = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "outputRange");

            RunGenericSqlWithParameters(sql, outputRange);
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void ClearRangeContentsGeneric()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var range = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "range_to_clear");
            ClearRangeContents(range);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void RunGenericSqlWithParameters(string sql, string outputRange)
        {

            
            if (sql.ToLower().Contains("insert") || sql.ToLower().Contains("update"))
                return;

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var server = UnlockToolkit.DB;
            var results = GenericSql(server, sql);

            ExcelAsyncUtil.QueueAsMacro(() => {
                XLTable xlt = xlh.XLTable(outputRange);
                xlt.DumpData(results, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            });
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void TightenTable()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string tableRange= xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "table_to_tighten");
            string keyColumn = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "table_to_tighten_column");

            TightenTable(tableRange, keyColumn);
        }

        #region Excel Generic Helper Methods

        private static void TightenTable(string tableRange, string keyColumn)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = xlh.XLTable(tableRange);
            xlt.TightenUpTable(keyColumn);
        }

        public static void ClearRangeContents(string range)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.ClearRangeContents(null, range);
        }

        public static void SetSingleValueToRange(string range, string value)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.WriteSingleValueToRange(range, value);
        }

        public static DataTable GenericSql(string server, string sql)
        {
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        #endregion
    }
}

        public static object GetTradeTicket(int trade_id)
        {
            string dir = @"C:\temp\audit\Trade Tickets";
            string trade_dir = @"C:\Users\DanFoster\Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\04 - Investors";
            string search_string = $"*Forward*#{trade_id}*executed*.pdf";
            var folders = Directory.GetFiles(trade_dir, search_string, SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            string folder = folders.FirstOrDefault();
            foreach(string f in folders)
                File.Copy(f, Path.Combine(dir, Path.GetFileName(f)), true);
            
            return Path.GetDirectoryName(folder);
        }

            string dir = @"C:\temp\audit\";
            if(null != fsea)
            {
                string new_file = $"{asset_id} - {name_simple}.pdf";
                string new_path = Path.Combine(dir, new_file);
                if(!File.Exists(new_path))
                    File.Copy(fsea, new_path);
                return new_file;
            }
            else
            {
                return "no match";
            }
                
        }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\HECM.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public static class HECM
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string CollatBreakdown(string ticker)
        {
            DataTable tbl = (DataTable) Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetDataBulk(ticker + " mtge", "MTG_AGE_DISTRIBUTION", null).Rows[0]["MTG_AGE_DISTRIBUTION"];
            Dictionary<string, double> products = new Dictionary<string, double>();
            DateTime collat_as_of = Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<DateTime>(ticker + " mtge", "MTG_COLLAT_DT");
            
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                int month_min = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["LOWER THRESHOLD WALA VALUE"]);
                int month_max = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["UPPER THRESHOLD WALA VALUE"]);
                int age = (month_min + month_max) / 2;
                DateTime avg_orig = collat_as_of.AddMonths(-age);
                double balance_pct = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["PERCENTAGE OF DEAL CURRENT BALANCE"]);
                string product = PickProduct(avg_orig, null, null, null);
                if (!products.ContainsKey(product))
                    products.Add(product, balance_pct);
                else
                    products[product] += balance_pct;
            }

            string msg = "";
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, double> kvp in products)
            {
                msg += $"({kvp.Key} - {kvp.Value:0.00}%) ";
            }

            return msg;

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string CMOProducts(string ticker)
        {
            var v = CMOGetUnderlying(ticker,true);
            string msg = "";
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, double> kvp in v.product_type_breakdown)
            {
                msg += $"({kvp.Key} - {kvp.Value:0.0}%) ";
            }
            return msg;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object UnderlyingPoolPrice(string ticker)
        {
            var v = CMOGetUnderlying(ticker,true);
            return v.wavg_price;
        }


        public class HECMCMO
        {
            public Dictionary<string, double> product_type_breakdown = new Dictionary<string, double>();
            public double balance_pct;
            public double? wavg_price = 0;
            public string product_type;
            public List<HECMCMO> underlying_pools = new List<HECMCMO>();
            
        }
        public static HECMCMO CMOGetUnderlying(string ticker,bool include_price)
        {
            DataTable tbl = (DataTable) Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetDataBulk(ticker + " mtge", "MTG_TOP_POOLS", null).Rows[0]["MTG_TOP_POOLS"];

            HECMCMO cmo = new HECMCMO();

            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                string pool = row["POOL TICKER AND NUMBER"].ToString();
                string product = Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<string>(pool + " mtge", "MTG_TYP");
                double balance_pct = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["PERCENTAGE OF DEAL CURRENT BALANCE"]);
                double? price = null;
                if (include_price)
                {
                    price = Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetDataNull<double>(pool + " mtge", "PX_MID");
                }

                HECMCMO hp = new HECMCMO {product_type = product, balance_pct = balance_pct, wavg_price = price};
                cmo.underlying_pools.Add(hp);
            }

            
            foreach (HECMCMO hp in cmo.underlying_pools)
            {
                if (!cmo.product_type_breakdown.ContainsKey(hp.product_type))
                    cmo.product_type_breakdown.Add(hp.product_type, hp.balance_pct);
                else
                    cmo.product_type_breakdown[hp.product_type] += hp.balance_pct;

                if (null != hp.wavg_price)
                    cmo.wavg_price += (hp.wavg_price * (hp.balance_pct/100.0));
            }
            return cmo;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object UnderlyingPool(string ticker)
        {
            return BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetDataBulkSingle<string>(ticker, "MTG_TOP_POOLS", "POOL TICKER AND NUMBER",null,false);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string PickProduct(DateTime orig_date, string saver_flag, double? mip, string underlying_index)
        {
            if (null != underlying_index && underlying_index.Contains("CMT"))
                return "Standard";
            if (orig_date <= System.Convert.ToDateTime("10/1/2013"))
            {
                if ((!String.IsNullOrEmpty(saver_flag) && saver_flag.ToUpper().Contains("Y")) || (null != mip && mip.Value == .5))
                    return "Saver";
                return "Standard";
            }

            if (orig_date >= System.Convert.ToDateTime("11/2/2017"))
                return "2017 HECM 60";


            if (orig_date >= System.Convert.ToDateTime("7/4/2014"))
                return "2014 HECM 60";

            if (orig_date > System.Convert.ToDateTime("10/1/2013") && orig_date < System.Convert.ToDateTime("7/4/2014"))
                return "2013 HECM 60";

            return "UNKNOWN";
        }
    }
}

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public static class ButtonWholeLoans
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string FICOBucket(Nullable<int> fico)
        {
            if (null == fico)
                return "UNKNOWN";
            if (fico > 700)
                return "700+";
            if (fico >= 660)
                return "660-700";
            if (fico >= 620)
                return "620-659";
            if (fico >= 600)
                return "600-619";
            if (fico < 600)
                return "<600";

            return "SHOULD NEVER SEE THIS";
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string PadZip(string zip)
        {
            return zip?.PadLeft(5,'0');
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string GeneratePaystring(double[] payments)
        {
            int months_dlq = 0;
            string pay = "";
            for(int i = payments.Length-1; i != -1;i--)
            {
                char single;
                if (null == payments[i] || payments[i] == 0)
                {
                    months_dlq++;
                    switch(months_dlq)
                    {
                        case 1:
                            single = '3';
                            break;
                        case 2:
                            single = '6';
                            break;
                        case 3:
                            single = '9';
                            break;
                        default:
                            single = 'D';
                            break;
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    months_dlq = 0;
                    single = 'C';
                }
                pay = pay.Insert(0, single.ToString());
            }
            return pay;
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string CurrentStatus(double[] payments)
        {
            string pay = GeneratePaystring(payments);
            return CurrentStatusNice(pay[0].ToString());
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string DLQFromPaystring(string paystring)
        {
            string last = paystring[0].ToString();
            return CurrentStatusNice(last);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string CurrentStatusNice(string status)
        {
            if (status.ContainsIns("C"))
                return "Current";
            if (status.Contains("3"))
                return "30";
            if (status.Contains("6"))
                return "60";
            if (status.Contains("9"))
                return "90";
            if (status.Contains("D"))
                return "90+";
            return "UNKNOWN";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string DLQfromPaystringAlt(string last_payment_entry)
        {
            if (last_payment_entry.Length > 0)
                last_payment_entry = last_payment_entry[0].ToString();
            last_payment_entry = last_payment_entry.ToUpper();
            if(last_payment_entry == "0")
                return "Current";
            if(last_payment_entry == "C")
                return "Current";
            if(last_payment_entry == "1")
                return "30";
            if(last_payment_entry == "2")
                return "60";
            if(last_payment_entry == "3")
                return "90";
            if(last_payment_entry == "4")
                return "90+";
            if(last_payment_entry == "5")
                return "90+";
            if(last_payment_entry == "6")
                return "90+";
            if(last_payment_entry == "7")
                return "90+";
            if(last_payment_entry == "8")
                return "90+";
            if(last_payment_entry == "9")
                return "90+";
            if (last_payment_entry.Contains("D"))
                return "90+";
            return "UNKNOWN";
        }




        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string GenericBucket(Nullable<double> number, double nearest,double decimals = 0)
        {
            if (null == number)
                return "UNKNOWN";

            double lowest = Math.Floor(number.Value / nearest) * nearest;
            double highest = Math.Ceiling(number.Value / nearest) * nearest;
            if(lowest == highest)
                lowest =  Math.Floor((number.Value-.0000001) / nearest) * nearest;
            double add = 1/(1*decimals);
            switch(decimals)
            {
                case 3:
                     return $"{lowest+.001:0.000}-{highest:0.000}";
                case 2:
                    return $"{lowest+.01:0.01}-{highest:0.00}";
                case 1:
                    return $"{lowest+.1:0.1}-{highest:0.0}";
                case 0:
                    return $"{lowest+1:#,###}-{highest:#,##0}";
            }

                
            
                return $"{lowest:#,##0}-{highest:#,##0}";

        }
    }
}

        private static DataTable RemoveEmptyRows(DataTable source)
        {
            DataTable dt1 = source.Clone(); 
            for (int i = 0; i <= source.Rows.Count - 1; i++) 
            {
                DataRow currentRow = source.Rows[i];  
                foreach (var colValue in currentRow.ItemArray)
                {
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(colValue.ToString())) 
                    {
                        dt1.ImportRow(currentRow);
                        break; 
                    }
                }
            }
            return dt1;
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Find Third Party Review Packages for asset IDs listed in named range 'TPR_assets'. Returns a 2-column array: AssetID, FilePath.")]
        public static object FindThirdPartyReviewPackages_Run(string destinationFolder = null)
        {
            try
            {
                var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                
                var assetIds = xlh.GetRangeArrayPopulated<string>(null, "TPR_assets");
                if (assetIds == null || assetIds.Length == 0)
                    return "No asset IDs found in named range 'TPR_assets'.";

                
                var distinctIds = assetIds.Where(s => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s))
                                          .Select(s => s.Trim())
                                          .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                                          .ToList();

                if (distinctIds.Count == 0)
                    return "No valid (non-blank) asset IDs in 'TPR_assets'.";

                
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(destinationFolder))
                {
                    destinationFolder = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "TPR_Packages");
                }
                Directory.CreateDirectory(destinationFolder);

                var dict = MaxLib.Assets.FindThirdPartyReviewPackages(UnlockToolkit.DB, distinctIds, destinationFolder);

                
                var rows = dict.Count + 1;
                var result = new object[rows, 2];
                result[0, 0] = "AssetID";
                result[0, 1] = "FilePath";

                int r = 1;
                foreach (var kvp in dict)
                {
                    result[r, 0] = kvp.Key;
                    result[r, 1] = string.IsNullOrEmpty(kvp.Value) ? "" : kvp.Value;
                    r++;
                }

                return result;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return $"Error: {ex.Message}";
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Find Recorded Security Instrument for asset IDs listed in named range 'FA_assets'. Opens destination folder when complete.")]
        public static object FindRecordedSecurityInstrument_Run(string destinationFolder = null)
        {
            try
            {
                var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
                var assetIds = xlh.GetRangeArrayPopulated<string>(null, "FA_assets");
                if (assetIds == null || assetIds.Length == 0)
                {
                    DXMessageBox.Show("No asset IDs found in named range 'FA_assets'.");
                    return "";
                }

                var distinctIds = assetIds.Where(s => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s))
                                          .Select(s => s.Trim())
                                          .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                                          .ToList();
                if (distinctIds.Count == 0)
                {
                    DXMessageBox.Show("No valid (non-blank) asset IDs in 'FA_assets'.");
                    return "";
                }

                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(destinationFolder))
                {
                    destinationFolder = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "Recorded_Security_Instruments");
                }

                
                if (Directory.Exists(destinationFolder))
                {
                    Directory.Delete(destinationFolder, true);
                }
                Directory.CreateDirectory(destinationFolder);

                MaxLib.Assets.FindRecordedSecurityInstrument(UnlockToolkit.DB, distinctIds, destinationFolder);

                
                string notFoundPath = Path.Combine(destinationFolder, "Assets_Not_Found.txt");
                string message = "Recorded Instrument Download Complete!";
                if (File.Exists(notFoundPath))
                {
                    var notFoundAssets = File.ReadAllLines(notFoundPath);
                    if (notFoundAssets.Length > 0)
                    {
                        message += $"\n\n{notFoundAssets.Length} asset(s) not found:\n" + string.Join(", ", notFoundAssets);
                    }
                }

                
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectory(destinationFolder, true);

                DXMessageBox.Show(message);
                return "";
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show($"Error: {ex.Message}");
                return "";
            }
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Find Recorded Package documents (by documentType attribute) for asset IDs listed in named range 'FA_assets'. Opens destination folder when complete.")]

                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(destinationFolder))

                return "";
            }
        }

        {

            Dictionary<string, string> column_map = new Dictionary<string, string>();

            column_map.Add("Loan ID", "Loan_ID");
            column_map.Add("Customer Loan ID", "Customer_Loan_ID");
            column_map.Add("Seller Loan ID", "Seller_Loan_ID");
            column_map.Add("Note Date", "Note_Date");
            column_map.Add("Original Loan Amount", "Original_Loan_Amount");
            column_map.Add("Initial Loan Rating", "Initial_Loan_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Final Loan Rating", "Final_Loan_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Initial Credit Rating", "Initial_Credit_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Final Credit Rating", "Final_Credit_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Initial Compliance Rating", "Initial_Compliance_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Final Compliance Rating", "Final_Compliance_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Initial Valuation Rating", "Initial_Valuation_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Final Valuation Rating", "Final_Valuation_Rating");
            column_map.Add("Initial Loan Grade (S&P)", "Initial_Loan_Grade_SP");
            column_map.Add("Final Loan Grade (S&P)", "Final_Loan_Grade_SP");
            column_map.Add("Initial Credit Grade (S&P)", "Initial_Credit_Grade_SP");
            column_map.Add("Final Credit Grade (S&P)", "Final_Credit_Grade_SP");
            column_map.Add("Initial Compliance Grade (S&P)", "Initial_Compliance_Grade_SP");
            column_map.Add("Final Compliance Grade (S&P)", "Final_Compliance_Grade_SP");
            column_map.Add("Initial Valuation Grade (S&P)", "Initial_Valuation_Grade_SP");
            column_map.Add("Final Valuation Grade (S&P)", "Final_Valuation_Grade_SP");

        }

using static DevExpress.XtraPrinting.Native.ExportOptionsPropertiesNames;

namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class Performance
    {
        [ExcelFunction(Name = "GetAllPerformanceData")]
        public static void GetAllPerformanceData()
        {

            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);

            var cutoff = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "cutoff");

            
            var performanceData = BadgerLib.Performance.GetAllPerformanceData(UnlockToolkit.DB, cutoff);

            XLTable xlt_assets = new XLTable(xlh, "performance_asset_data");
            xlt_assets.DumpData(performanceData.Tables[0], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            XLTable xlt_dlq = new XLTable(xlh, "performance_dlq_data");
            xlt_dlq.DumpData(performanceData.Tables[1], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            XLTable xlt_reo = new XLTable(xlh, "performance_reo_data");
            xlt_reo.DumpData(performanceData.Tables[2], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            XLTable xlt_defaults = new XLTable(xlh, "performance_defaults_data");
            xlt_defaults.DumpData(performanceData.Tables[3], true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);
        }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Registration\ArrayResizer.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    
    public static class ResizeTestFunctions
    {
        
        public static object[,] MakeArray(int rows, int columns)
        {
            object[,] result = new object[rows, columns];
            for (int i = 0; i < rows; i++)
            {
                for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
                {
                    result[i, j] = i + j;
                }
            }

            return result;
        }

        public static double[,] MakeArrayDoubles(int rows, int columns)
        {
            double[,] result = new double[rows, columns];
            for (int i = 0; i < rows; i++)
            {
                for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
                {
                    result[i, j] = i + (j / 1000.0);
                }
            }

            return result;
        }

        public static object MakeMixedArrayAndResize(int rows, int columns)
        {
            object[,] result = new object[rows, columns];
            for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
            {
                result[0, j] = "Col " + j;
            }
            for (int i = 1; i < rows; i++)
            {
                for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
                {
                    result[i, j] = i + (j * 0.1);
                }
            }

            return ArrayResizer.Resize(result);
        }

        
        public static object MakeArrayAndResize(int rows, int columns, string unused, string unusedtoo)
        {
            object[,] result = MakeArray(rows, columns);
            return ArrayResizer.Resize(result);

            
            
            
        }

        public static double[,] MakeArrayAndResizeDoubles(int rows, int columns)
        {
            double[,] result = MakeArrayDoubles(rows, columns);
            return ArrayResizer.ResizeDoubles(result);
        }
    }

    public class ArrayResizer : XlCall
    {
        
        
        public static object Resize(object[,] array)
        {
            var caller = Excel(xlfCaller) as ExcelReference;
            if (caller == null)
                return array;

            int rows = array.GetLength(0);
            int columns = array.GetLength(1);

            if (rows == 0 || columns == 0)
                return array;

            if ((caller.RowLast - caller.RowFirst + 1 == rows) &&
                (caller.ColumnLast - caller.ColumnFirst + 1 == columns))
            {
                
                return array;
            }

            var rowLast = caller.RowFirst + rows - 1;
            var columnLast = caller.ColumnFirst + columns - 1;

            
            if (rowLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxRows - 1 ||
                columnLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxColumns - 1)
            {
                
                
                return ExcelError.ExcelErrorValue;
            }

            
            ExcelAsyncUtil.QueueAsMacro(() =>
            {
                
                var target = new ExcelReference(caller.RowFirst, rowLast, caller.ColumnFirst, columnLast, caller.SheetId);
                DoResize(target); 
            });
            
            return array;
        }

        public static double[,] ResizeDoubles(double[,] array)
        {
            var caller = Excel(xlfCaller) as ExcelReference;
            if (caller == null)
                return array;

            int rows = array.GetLength(0);
            int columns = array.GetLength(1);

            if (rows == 0 || columns == 0)
                return array;

            if ((caller.RowLast - caller.RowFirst + 1 == rows) &&
                (caller.ColumnLast - caller.ColumnFirst + 1 == columns))
            {
                
                return array;
            }

            var rowLast = caller.RowFirst + rows - 1;
            var columnLast = caller.ColumnFirst + columns - 1;

            if (rowLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxRows - 1 ||
                columnLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxColumns - 1)
            {
                
                
                return null;
            }

            
            ExcelAsyncUtil.QueueAsMacro(() =>
            {
                
                var target = new ExcelReference(caller.RowFirst, rowLast, caller.ColumnFirst, columnLast, caller.SheetId);
                DoResize(target); 
            });
            
            return array;
        }

        static void DoResize(ExcelReference target)
        {
            
            using (new ExcelEchoOffHelper())
            using (new ExcelCalculationManualHelper())
            {
                ExcelReference firstCell = new ExcelReference(target.RowFirst, target.RowFirst, target.ColumnFirst, target.ColumnFirst, target.SheetId);

                
                string formula = (string)Excel(xlfGetCell, 41, firstCell);
                bool isFormulaArray = (bool)Excel(xlfGetCell, 49, firstCell);
                if (isFormulaArray)
                {
                    
                    using (new ExcelSelectionHelper(firstCell))
                    {
                        
                        Excel(xlcSelectSpecial, 6);
                        ExcelReference oldArray = (ExcelReference)Excel(xlfSelection);

                        oldArray.SetValue(ExcelEmpty.Value);
                    }
                }
                
                bool isR1C1Mode = (bool)Excel(xlfGetWorkspace, 4);
                string formulaR1C1 = formula;
                if (!isR1C1Mode)
                {
                    object formulaR1C1Obj;
                    XlReturn formulaR1C1Return = TryExcel(xlfFormulaConvert, out formulaR1C1Obj, formula, true, false, ExcelMissing.Value, firstCell);
                    if (formulaR1C1Return != XlReturn.XlReturnSuccess || formulaR1C1Obj is ExcelError)
                    {
                        string firstCellAddress = (string)Excel(xlfReftext, firstCell, true);
                        Excel(xlcAlert, "Cannot resize array formula at " + firstCellAddress + " - formula might be too long when converted to R1C1 format.");
                        firstCell.SetValue("'" + formula);
                        return;
                    }
                    formulaR1C1 = (string)formulaR1C1Obj;
                }
                
                object ignoredResult;
                
                XlReturn formulaArrayReturn = TryExcel(xlcFormulaArray, out ignoredResult, formulaR1C1, target);
                

                

                if (formulaArrayReturn != XlReturn.XlReturnSuccess)
                {
                    string firstCellAddress = (string)Excel(xlfReftext, firstCell, true);
                    Excel(xlcAlert, "Cannot resize array formula at " + firstCellAddress + " - result might overlap another array.");
                    
                    firstCell.SetValue("'" + formula);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    
    
    public class ExcelEchoOffHelper : XlCall, IDisposable
    {
        object oldEcho;

        public ExcelEchoOffHelper()
        {
            oldEcho = Excel(xlfGetWorkspace, 40);
            Excel(xlcEcho, false);
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            Excel(xlcEcho, oldEcho);
        }
    }

    public class ExcelCalculationManualHelper : XlCall, IDisposable
    {
        object oldCalculationMode;

        public ExcelCalculationManualHelper()
        {
            oldCalculationMode = Excel(xlfGetDocument, 14);
            Excel(xlcOptionsCalculation, 3);
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            Excel(xlcOptionsCalculation, oldCalculationMode);
        }
    }

    
    
    
    public class ExcelSelectionHelper : XlCall, IDisposable
    {
        object oldSelectionOnActiveSheet;
        object oldActiveCellOnActiveSheet;

        object oldSelectionOnRefSheet;
        object oldActiveCellOnRefSheet;

        public ExcelSelectionHelper(ExcelReference refToSelect)
        {
            
            oldSelectionOnActiveSheet = Excel(xlfSelection);
            oldActiveCellOnActiveSheet = Excel(xlfActiveCell);

            
            string refSheet = (string)Excel(xlSheetNm, refToSelect);
            Excel(xlcWorkbookSelect, new object[] { refSheet });

            
            oldSelectionOnRefSheet = Excel(xlfSelection);
            oldActiveCellOnRefSheet = Excel(xlfActiveCell);

            
            Excel(xlcFormulaGoto, refToSelect);
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            
            Excel(xlcSelect, oldSelectionOnRefSheet, oldActiveCellOnRefSheet);

            
            string oldActiveSheet = (string)Excel(xlSheetNm, oldSelectionOnActiveSheet);
            Excel(xlcWorkbookSelect, new object[] { oldActiveSheet });

            
            Excel(xlcSelect, oldSelectionOnActiveSheet, oldActiveCellOnActiveSheet);
        }
    }

}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Registration\CacheFunctionExecutionHandler.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    
    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.Method)]
    public class CacheAttribute : Attribute
    {
        public TimeSpan CacheTimeout;
        public CacheAttribute(int cacheTimeoutSeconds)
        {
            CacheTimeout = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(cacheTimeoutSeconds);
        }
    }

    
    public class CacheFunctionExecutionHandler : FunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        static readonly ObjectCache _cache = MemoryCache.Default;
        readonly TimeSpan _cacheTimeout;

        public CacheFunctionExecutionHandler(TimeSpan cacheTimeout)
        {
            _cacheTimeout = cacheTimeout;
        }

        public override void OnEntry(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            string key = GenerateKey(args);
            args.Tag = key;

            object result = _cache[key];
            if (result != null)
            {
                
                args.ReturnValue = result;
                args.FlowBehavior = FlowBehavior.Return;
            }
        }

        public override void OnSuccess(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            
            _cache.Add((string)args.Tag, args.ReturnValue, 
                new CacheItemPolicy { AbsoluteExpiration = DateTime.UtcNow + _cacheTimeout });
        }

        string GenerateKey(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            var keyBuilder = new StringBuilder(args.FunctionName);
            foreach (var arg in args.Arguments)
            {
                keyBuilder.Append('\0');    
                keyBuilder.Append(arg);
            }
            return keyBuilder.ToString();
        }
        

        
        public static FunctionExecutionHandler CacheHandlerSelector(ExcelFunctionRegistration functionRegistration)
        {
            
            if (functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<CacheAttribute>().Any())
            {
                
                var cacheAtt = functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<CacheAttribute>().First();
                functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.RemoveAll(att => att is CacheAttribute);

                return new CacheFunctionExecutionHandler(cacheAtt.CacheTimeout);
            }
            return null;
        }

    }

    
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Registration\InstanceMemberRegistration.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    
    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.All)]
    public class ExcelObjectAttribute : Attribute
    {
    }

    [ExcelObject]
    public class TestClass
    {
        string _content;

        public TestClass(string content)
        {
            _content = content;
        }

        public string GetContent()
        {
            return "Content is " + _content;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
    }

    class InstanceMemberRegistration
    {
        public static LambdaExpression WrapInstanceMethod(MethodInfo method)
        {
            
            
            
            

            var instanceParam = Expression.Parameter(method.DeclaringType, method.DeclaringType.Name);
            var callParams = method.GetParameters().Select(p => Expression.Parameter(p.ParameterType, p.Name)).ToList();
            var allParams = new List<ParameterExpression>();
            allParams.Add(instanceParam);
            allParams.AddRange(callParams);

            var callExpr = Expression.Call(instanceParam, method, callParams);
            return Expression.Lambda(callExpr, method.Name, allParams);
        }

        public static void TestInstanceRegistration()
        {
            var instanceMethod = typeof(TestClass).GetMethod("GetContent");
            var lambda = WrapInstanceMethod(instanceMethod);

            
            var paramConversionConfig = new ParameterConversionConfiguration()
                .AddParameterConversion((string content) => new TestClass(content));

            
            var reg = new ExcelFunctionRegistration(lambda);
            var processed = ParameterConversionRegistration.ProcessParameterConversions(new[] { reg }, paramConversionConfig);
            processed.RegisterFunctions();
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Registration\SuppressInDialogHandler.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    
    

    

    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.Method)]
    public class SuppressInDialogAttribute :  Attribute, IFunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        readonly string _dialogResult;
        public SuppressInDialogAttribute(string dialogMessage = "!!! NOT CALCULATED IN DIALOG !!!")
        {
            _dialogResult = dialogMessage;
        }

        public void OnEntry(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            if (ExcelDnaUtil.IsInFunctionWizard())
            {
                args.ReturnValue = _dialogResult;
                args.FlowBehavior = FlowBehavior.Return;
            }
            
        }

        
        public void OnSuccess(FunctionExecutionArgs args) { }
        public void OnException(FunctionExecutionArgs args) { }
        public void OnExit(FunctionExecutionArgs args) { }
    }

    public static class SuppressInDialogFunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        public static IFunctionExecutionHandler SuppressInDialogSelector(ExcelFunctionRegistration functionRegistration)
        {
            
            if (functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<SuppressInDialogAttribute>().Any() &&
                (functionRegistration.FunctionLambda.ReturnType == typeof(object) || 
                 functionRegistration.FunctionLambda.ReturnType == typeof(string)))
            {
                
                var suppressAtt = functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<SuppressInDialogAttribute>().First();
                functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.RemoveAll(att => att is SuppressInDialogAttribute);

                return suppressAtt;
            }
            return null;

        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Registration\TimingFunctionExecutionHandler.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.Method)]
    public class TimingAttribute : Attribute
    {
    }

    public class TimingFunctionExecutionHandler : FunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        public override void OnEntry(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            args.Tag = Stopwatch.StartNew();
        }

        public override void OnExit(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            var sw = (Stopwatch)args.Tag;
            sw.Stop();

            Debug.WriteLine("{0} executed in {1} milliseconds", args.FunctionName, sw.ElapsedMilliseconds);
        }

        
        static readonly Lazy<TimingFunctionExecutionHandler> _handler =
            new Lazy<TimingFunctionExecutionHandler>(() => new TimingFunctionExecutionHandler());

        internal static FunctionExecutionHandler TimingHandlerSelector(ExcelFunctionRegistration functionRegistration)
        {
            
            if (functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.RemoveAll(att => att is TimingAttribute) == 0)
            {
                
                return null;
            }
            return _handler.Value;
        }
    } 
}


--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Registration.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public partial class UnlockToolkit
    {
        static ParameterConversionConfiguration GetPostAsyncReturnConversionConfig()
        {
            
            
            
            
            return new ParameterConversionConfiguration()
                .AddReturnConversion((type, customAttributes) => type != typeof(object) ? null : ((Expression<Func<object, object>>)
                    ((object returnValue) => returnValue.Equals(ExcelError.ExcelErrorNA) ? ExcelError.ExcelErrorGettingData : returnValue)));


        }

        static ParameterConversionConfiguration GetParameterConversionConfig()
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            




            var paramConversionConfig = new ParameterConversionConfiguration()

                
                .AddParameterConversion(ParameterConversions.GetOptionalConversion(treatEmptyAsMissing: true))


                
                .AddParameterConversion((TestType1 value) => new TestType2(value))
                .AddParameterConversion((string value) => new TestType1(value))

                
                .AddReturnConversion((TestType1 value) => value.ToString())
                .AddReturnConversion((Complex value) => new double[2] { value.Real, value.Imaginary })

                

                
                
                
                .AddParameterConversion((object[] inputs) => inputs.Select(TypeConversion.ConvertToString).ToArray())

                
                .AddReturnConversion((Enum value) => value.ToString(), handleSubTypes: true)
                .AddParameterConversion(ParameterConversions.GetEnumStringConversion())

                .AddParameterConversion((object[] input) => new Complex(TypeConversion.ConvertToDouble(input[0]), TypeConversion.ConvertToDouble(input[1])))
                .AddNullableConversion(treatEmptyAsMissing: true, treatNAErrorAsMissing: true);

            return paramConversionConfig;
        }

        static FunctionExecutionConfiguration GetFunctionExecutionHandlerConfig()
        {
            return new FunctionExecutionConfiguration()
                
                .AddFunctionExecutionHandler(CacheFunctionExecutionHandler.CacheHandlerSelector)
                .AddFunctionExecutionHandler(TimingFunctionExecutionHandler.TimingHandlerSelector)
                .AddFunctionExecutionHandler(SuppressInDialogFunctionExecutionHandler.SuppressInDialogSelector);
        }

        
        public class TestType1
        {
            public string Value;
            public TestType1(string value)
            {
                Value = value;
            }

            public override string ToString()
            {
                return "From Type 1 with " + Value;
            }

            [ExcelFunction]
            public static string dnaTestFunction1(TestType1 tt)
            {
                return "The Test (1) value is " + tt.Value;
            }
        }

        public class TestType2
        {
            readonly TestType1 _value;
            public TestType2(TestType1 value)
            {
                _value = value;
            }

            
            [ExcelFunction]
            public static string dnaTestFunction2(TestType2 tt)
            {
                return "The Test (2) value is " + tt._value.Value;
            }

            [ExcelFunction]
            public static TestType1 dnaTestFunction2Ret1(TestType2 tt)
            {
                return new TestType1("The Test (2) value is " + tt._value.Value);
            }

            [ExcelFunction]
            public static string dnaJoinStrings(string separator, string[] values)
            {
                return string.Join(separator, values);
            }

            class InstanceMemberRegistration
            {
                public static LambdaExpression WrapInstanceMethod(MethodInfo method)
                {
                    
                    
                    
                    

                    var instanceParam = Expression.Parameter(method.DeclaringType, method.DeclaringType.Name);
                    var callParams = method.GetParameters().Select(p => Expression.Parameter(p.ParameterType, p.Name)).ToList();
                    var allParams = new List<ParameterExpression>();
                    allParams.Add(instanceParam);
                    allParams.AddRange(callParams);

                    var callExpr = Expression.Call(instanceParam, method, callParams);
                    return Expression.Lambda(callExpr, method.Name, allParams);
                }
            }
        }
    }

            SummarySetupHelper("breakdown", "raw", "desk","desk", 1, true);

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CleanFundingSummary()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            UnhideAllRowsSummary();
            SummarySetupHelper("breakdown", "raw", "grouping", "grouping", 1, false);
            SummarySetupHelper("breakdown_two", "raw", "acct_no", "acct_no", 1, true); ;

            xlh.HideAndShowColumn(true, "Summary", true);
            
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void UnhideAllRowsSummary()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            xlh.HideAndShowColumn(false, "Summary", true);
            xlh.UnHideAllRows("Summary");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GetMonthlyTradeSummary()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            DateTime asOfDate = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "asOfDate");
            DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Trades.GetMonthlyTradeSummary(UnlockToolkit.DB, asOfDate);
            XLTable xlt_tradeSummary = new XLTable(xlh, "trade_summary");
            xlt_tradeSummary.DumpData(tbl, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt_tradeSummary.TightenUpTable("trade_id");

        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void MonthlyTradeGenericExport()
        {
            Unlock_Toolkit.Utils.GenericExport();
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void AssetExitSummaryReport()
        {
            
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            XLTable filter = new XLTable(xlh, "asset_list");
            List<string> assets = filter.AllRows().Select(n => n["ASSET_ID"]).Where(n => n != null).Distinct().ToList(); 


            DataTable report_data = AssetExitSummaryReport(UnlockToolkit.DB, assets);
            
            XLTable xlt_assetExitSummary = new XLTable(xlh, "report_data_table");

            xlh.ClearRangeContents(null, "report_data_table", false);
            xlh.WriteRange("report_data_table2", report_data, true);
            xlh.WriteRange("report_data_table", report_data.Transpose(), true);

            
            

        }

        
        public static DataTable AssetExitSummaryReport(string server, List<string> assetsList)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.AssetExitSummaryReport @assetsList=@assetsList";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assetsList", assetsList);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }


        public static void SummarySetupHelper(string range_to_help, string base_data,string populate_with,string table_column_name,int blank_buffer,bool hide_rows)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XL.XLTable xlt = new XL.XLTable(xlh, base_data);
            IEnumerable<object> breakdowns = xlt.UniqueValues<object>(populate_with, true);

            XLTable sum = new XLTable(xlh, range_to_help);
            sum.ClearAllButHeader(null);
            
            foreach (XL.XLTableRow row in sum.AllRows())
            {
                row.Unhide();
            }

            if (breakdowns.Count() > 0)
            {
                int count = 0;
                int buffer_done = 0;
                foreach (XL.XLTableRow row in sum.AllRows())
                {
                    if (count < breakdowns.Count())
                        row.Update(table_column_name, breakdowns.ElementAt(count));
                    else
                    {
                        if (blank_buffer > buffer_done)
                        {
                            buffer_done++;
                            continue;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            if(hide_rows)
                                row.Hide();
                        }
                    }
                    count++;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

        public static bool AssetExists(string server,string asset_id)
        {

            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count != 0;
        }

        public static bool AssetExistsOutreach(string server, string outreach_link)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Scrape s where s.outreach_link = @outreach_link";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@outreach_link", outreach_link);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count != 0;
        }


        public static bool AssetExistsFromFilename(string server, string filename)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Scrape s where s.filename = @filename";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count != 0;
        }

        public static void InsertThings(string server, int? outreach_id, string asset_id,string name,string uam_commentary,string sales_commentary,string escrow_file_num,string legal_description,bool originated,string filename,long? pipeline_id,string outreach_link)
        {
            string sql = "insert into Scrape (outreach_id_old,asset_id,name,uam_commentary,sales_commentary,escrow_file_num,legal_description,originated,filename,pipeline_id_old,outreach_link) values (@outreach_id,@asset_id,@name,@uam_commentary,@sales_commentary,@escrow_file_num,@legal_description,@originated,@filename,@pipeline_id,@outreach_link)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@outreach_id", outreach_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.AddParameter("@uam_commentary", uam_commentary);
            q.AddParameter("@sales_commentary", sales_commentary);
            q.AddParameter("@escrow_file_num", escrow_file_num);
            q.AddParameter("@legal_description", legal_description);
            q.AddParameter("@originated", originated);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            q.AddParameter("@pipeline_id", pipeline_id);
            q.AddParameter("@outreach_link", outreach_link);
            q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }

        }

        [ExcelFunction(Name = "SQL.AddColumn")]
        public static object SQLAddColumn(string table,string column_name,string db_type,bool nullable)
        {
            string null_str = !nullable ? "NOT " : "";
            string sql = $"ALTER TABLE [dbo].[{table}] ADD [{column_name}] {db_type} {null_str}NULL";
            return sql;
        }
        [ExcelFunction(Name = "SQL.Update")]
        public static string SQLUpdate(string table, object[,] keys_obj, object[,] values_obj)
        {
            return Database.QueryBuilder.SQLUpdate(table, keys_obj, values_obj);
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Name = "SQL.InsertExecute")]
        public static string SQLInsertExecute(string server,string table, object[,] range)
        {
            string sql = SQLInsert(table, range);
            if (sql.ToUpper().Contains(@"C:\") && System.IO.File.Exists(sql))
                sql = System.IO.File.ReadAllText(sql);
            List<string> sqls = sql.Split(Environment.NewLine).ToList();
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.ExecuteBatch(sqls, 1, null);
            return sql;
        }


        [ExcelFunction(Name = "SQL.InsertValidateExecuteHeaders")]
        public static string SQLInsertValidateExecute(string server, string table, string[] columns, object[,] range)
        {

            Dictionary<string, Type> overrides = Database.DBUtils.GetTableTypes(server, table);
            DataTable raw = UtilsLib.Excel.ArrayToDataTable(range,false,overrides);
            for(int i = 0; i!= raw.Columns.Count;i++)
            {
                raw.Columns[i].ColumnName = columns[i];
            }
            var h = Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidate(raw, server, table, true);
            List<string> sqls = h.lines;
            Query q = new Query(null, server);
            q.ExecuteBatch(sqls, 1, null);
            return h.sql_or_error;
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Name = "SQL.InsertValidateExecute")]
        public static string SQLInsertValidateExecute(string server, string table, object[,] range)
        {
            return Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidateExecute(server, table, range);
        }


        [ExcelFunction(Name = "SQL.Insert")]
        public static string SQLInsert(string table, object[,] range)
        {
            
            
            return Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidate(range,UnlockToolkit.DB, table,false).sql_or_error;
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Name = "SQL.InsertValidateDB")]
        public static string SQLInsertValidateDB(string table, object[,] range)
