--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Strings.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public static class Strings
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object CountInstancesOfString(string full_str, string thing_you_want_to_count)
        {
            return full_str.Split(thing_you_want_to_count).Length - 1;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static bool HasDupes(string[] cells)
        {
            List<string> dupes = new List<string>(cells);
            dupes = dupes.Where(n => !(String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(n))).ToList();
            return !(dupes.Distinct().ToList().Count == dupes.Count());
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object SplitStr(string full_str, string delimiter, int zero_based_index)
        {
            string[] splits = full_str.Split(delimiter);
            if (splits.Length <= zero_based_index)
                return ExcelError.ExcelErrorNA;
            return splits[zero_based_index].Trim();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object SplitStrRev(string full_str, string delimiter, int zero_based_index)
        {
            int length = full_str.Split(delimiter).Length-1;
            return full_str.Split(delimiter)[length - zero_based_index].Trim();
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Name = "String.Format")]
        public static object StrFormat(string full_str, params object[] fmts)
        {
            return String.Format(full_str, fmts);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object AddAllDelimitedNumbers(string full_str, string delimter)
        {
            double d = 0;
            foreach (string s in full_str.Split(delimter))
            {
                double local_dbl;
                if (Double.TryParse(s, out local_dbl))
                {
                    d += local_dbl;
                }
            }
            return d;
        }



        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object PayStringTotalPayHack(string status_string, string pay_string)
        {
            double d = 0;
            string[] status = status_string.Split('|');
            string[] pay = pay_string.Split('|');
            int i = 0;
            foreach (string s in status)
            {
                if (s == "C")
                    d += System.Convert.ToDouble(pay[i]);
                i++;
            }
            return d;
        }

    }
}

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static int UpdatePayoffTicket(int? ticket_id, double? incentive_fee, double? premium_recapture, double? disposition_fee, double? other_fees, double? settlement_fees)
        {
            double processing_fee = 0;
            double recording_fee = 0;

            if (null != settlement_fees && settlement_fees > 0)
            {
                if (settlement_fees == 575)
                {
                    processing_fee = -500.00;
                    recording_fee = -75.00;
                }
                else
                {
                    recording_fee = -75.00;
                }
            }

            if (null == ticket_id)
                return -1;
            string sql = "update Trades set incentive_fee=-abs(@incentive_fee), premium_recapture=abs(@premium_recapture), disposition_fee=-abs(@disposition_fee), other_fees=-abs(@other_fees), processing_fee=@processing_fee, recording_fee=@recording_fee where id=@ticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.AddParameter("@incentive_fee", incentive_fee);
            q.AddParameter("@premium_recapture", premium_recapture);
            q.AddParameter("@disposition_fee", disposition_fee);
            q.AddParameter("@other_fees", other_fees);
            q.AddParameter("@processing_fee", processing_fee);
            q.AddParameter("@recording_fee", recording_fee);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_id", ticket_id);
            q.ExecuteTable();
            return ticket_id.Value;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object HistoricalOwnerName(string asset_id,DateTime asOf)
        {
            int? account_id = BadgerLib.Portfolio.HistorialInvestor(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id,asOf);
            DateTime? final_disposition_date = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<DateTime>(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id, "final_disposition_date", true);
            DateTime? effective_date = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<DateTime>(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id, "effective_date", true);
            if (effective_date > asOf)
                return "NOT YET ORIGINATED";
            if (null != final_disposition_date && final_disposition_date != DateTime.MinValue && final_disposition_date < asOf)
                return $"PAID OFF - {asOf.ToString("M/d/yyyy")}";
            if (null == account_id)
                return "<MISSING>";
            return BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountName(UnlockToolkit.DB, account_id.Value);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object NetAccruedInterestAsOf(string ticker, double oface, DateTime buy_settle, DateTime sell_settle, DateTime asOfMonth)
        {
            
            if (!UtilsLib.Validate.IsValidInput(ticker))
                return -0;

            double sell_accrued = 0;
            if(sell_settle.Year != 1899 && sell_settle.SameMonth(asOfMonth))
                sell_accrued = Assets.Trade.AccruedInterest(ticker, oface, sell_settle);

            double buy_accrued = -Assets.Trade.AccruedInterest(ticker, oface, buy_settle);

            if (!buy_settle.SameMonth(asOfMonth))
                buy_accrued = 0;

            return sell_accrued+buy_accrued;

            
            
            
            
            
            
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object AccruedInterestCPR(string ticker,double oface,DateTime buy_settle, DateTime settle_date,double cpr)

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object AccruedInterest360(string ticker,double oface,DateTime settle_date)
        {
            double accrued = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<double>(ticker, "INT_ACC", "SETTLE_DT=" + settle_date.ToString("yyyMMdd"));
            double factor = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<double>(ticker, "MTG_FACTOR_SET_DT", "SETTLE_DT=" + settle_date.ToString("yyyMMdd"));
            if (factor == 0)
                factor = 1;
            double dollars = (oface * factor )/ 100.0 * accrued;
            int days = settle_date.Day-1;
            return dollars/days*30;
        }

        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object RemitInterest(string ticker, double oface, DateTime month)
        {
            
            return RemitInterestInternal(ticker, oface, month, "interest");
        }


        public static object RemitPrincipal(string ticker, double oface, DateTime month)
        {
            return RemitInterestInternal(ticker, oface, month, "principal paid");
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object TradeOpen(DateTime? buy_settle,DateTime? sell_settle,DateTime asOf)
        {
            if(null == buy_settle && null == sell_settle)
                return false;
            if(null == sell_settle && buy_settle <= asOf)
                return true;
            if (sell_settle > asOf && buy_settle <= asOf)
                return true;
            return false;
        }
        public static object RemitInterestInternal(string ticker, double oface, DateTime month,string retVal)
        {
            double par = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetData<double>(ticker, "par_amt");
            double pct = oface / par;

            DataTable one = (DataTable) BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().GetDataBulk(ticker, "HIST_CASH_FLOW", null);
            if(one.Rows.Count == 0)
                return null;


            DataTable tbl = (DataTable) one.Rows[0]["HIST_CASH_FLOW"];
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                DateTime remit = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["PAYMENT DATE"]);
                if (remit.SameMonth(month))
                    return System.Convert.ToDouble(row[retVal])* pct;
            }
            return "";
        }



        [ExcelFunction]
        public static bool SameMonth(DateTime asOf,DateTime month)
        {
            return asOf.SameMonth(month);
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object FindNumber(string key, object[] labels, object[] numbers)
        {
            if (labels.Length != numbers.Length)
                return "#Wrong Lengths#";
            for(int i = 0;i!= labels.Length;i++)
            {
                string label = labels[i].ToString();
                if (label.ToUpper() == key)
                {
                    string num = numbers[i].ToString();
                    if (num.Length >= 2 && num.Substring(num.Length - 2) == "CR")
                    {
                        num = num.Replace("CR", "");
                        return -System.Convert.ToDouble(num);
                    }
                    return System.Convert.ToDouble(numbers[i]);
                }
            }
            return ExcelDna.Integration.ExcelEmpty.Value;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void InsertTrades()
        {
            XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;

            List<string> ranges = new List<string>();
            ranges.Add("sql_sell_trades");
            ranges.Add("sql_buy_trades");
            foreach (string r in ranges)
            {
                xlh.CalcSingleCell(null, r);
                string sql = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, r, false);
                Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
                q.Execute();
            }
        }

namespace Unlock_Toolkit

    public partial class UnlockToolkit : IExcelAddIn
    {
        public static XL.XLHelper GlobalExcel;
        public static BBGDDE _dde;

        public static string DB_SNOWFLAKE;
        public static Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.Application _app = (Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.Application) (ExcelDnaUtil.Application);


        public void AutoOpen()
        {
            
            GlobalExcel = new XLHelper((Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.Application)ExcelDnaUtil.Application);
            DB = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL;
            DB_SNOWFLAKE = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_LABEL;

            #if (DEBUG == false)
            
            {
                
                AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += CurrentDomain_UnhandledException1;
            }
#endif

            
            
            

            
            

            
            

            
            


            var conversionConfig = GetParameterConversionConfig();
            var postAsyncReturnConfig = GetPostAsyncReturnConversionConfig();

            var functionHandlerConfig = GetFunctionExecutionHandlerConfig();



            
            
            ExcelRegistration.GetExcelFunctions()
                .ProcessMapArrayFunctions(conversionConfig)
                .ProcessParameterConversions(conversionConfig)
                .ProcessAsyncRegistrations(nativeAsyncIfAvailable: false)
                .ProcessParameterConversions(postAsyncReturnConfig)
                .ProcessParamsRegistrations()
                .ProcessFunctionExecutionHandlers(functionHandlerConfig)
                .RegisterFunctions();
            ExcelRegistration.GetExcelCommands().RegisterCommands();

            


            
            InstanceMemberRegistration.TestInstanceRegistration();

            

            

        }

        private void CurrentDomain_UnhandledException1(object sender, UnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)
        {
            try
            {
                Exception n = (Exception)e.ExceptionObject;
                

                
                var caller = XlCall.Excel(XlCall.xlfCaller) as ExcelReference;
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n);
                DXHelper.ErrorBox.ShowError(n);
                
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                
            }
           
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string EmailDomain(string email)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(email))
                return "";
            return email.Substring(email.IndexOf("@") + 1, email.Length - email.IndexOf("@") - 1);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static int WriteHPI(string property_type, string region_type, int? zip, string[] date_strings, string[] values, int? region_id, int? size_rank, string state, string city, string metro, string county)
        {

            if (date_strings.Length != values.Length)
            {
                return -1;
            }
            List<Query> all = new List<Query>();
            List<string> text = new List<string>();
            int how_many = 0;
            for (int i = 0; i != date_strings.Length; i++)
            {
                string date_string = date_strings[i];
                DateTime date = DateTime.FromOADate(System.Convert.ToDouble(date_string));
                date = date.SetDay(1);
                string value_raw = values[i];
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(value_raw))
                    continue;
                Nullable<int> value = System.Convert.ToInt32(value_raw);
                
                
                string l = Assets.Collat.GetRawHPISQL(property_type, region_type, zip, date, value, region_id, size_rank, state, city, metro, county);
                text.Add(l);
                
            }

            
            string sql = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, text.ToArray());
            Query qs = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            qs.Execute();
            return text.Count;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string WriteAddressFile(object[] range)
        {
            List<string> lines = new List<string>();
            string filename = Path.GetTempFileName() + ".csv";
            lines.Add("address");
            foreach (object o in range)
            {
                string result = o as string;
                if (o.GetType() == typeof(ExcelEmpty))
                {
                    result = null;
                }
                lines.Add(result);
            }
            File.WriteAllLines(filename, lines.ToArray());
            return filename;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string WriteSimpleFile(object[,] range)
        {
            string filename = Path.GetTempFileName() + ".txt";
            int rows = range.GetLength(0);
            int cols = range.GetLength(1);
            string all_rows = "";
            List<string> lines = new List<string>();
            for (int r = 0; r != rows; r++)
            {
                string col = "";
                for (int c = 0; c != cols; c++)
                {
                    object o = range[r, c];
                    if (o.GetType() == typeof(ExcelEmpty))
                    {
                        o = null;
                    }
                    col += $"{o}\t";
                }
                lines.Add(col);
            }
            File.WriteAllLines(filename, lines.ToArray());
            return filename;
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object NiceNumber(double number, double? round = null)
        {
            double nearest = 0;
            if (null != round)
            {
                number = Math.Round(number / round.Value) * round.Value;
            }
            if (Math.Abs(number) >= 1e6)
            {
                return String.Format("{0:#,##0}MM", number / 1e6);
            }
            if (number < 1e6)
            {
                return String.Format("{0:#,##0}K", number / 1000.0);
            }
            return number;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string MakeNice(object[] headers, object[] color)
        {
            if (headers.Length != color.Length)
                return "";
            List<string> lines = new List<string>();

            int i = 0;
            foreach (string header in headers)
            {
                if (null == color[i] || (null != color[i] && color[i].GetType() == typeof(ExcelEmpty)))
                {
                    i++;
                    continue;
                }
                string color_line = color[i].ToString();
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(color_line))
                {
                    string line = String.Format("{0}: {1}", header, color_line);
                    if (header == "BLANK")
                        line = color_line;
                    lines.Add(line);
                }
                i++;
            }
            return String.Join(Environment.NewLine, lines);
        }



        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object PadRight(string input, int lenght, string pad_char)
        {
            pad_char = "";
            
            pad_char = " ";
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(32);
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(31);
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(26);
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(8195);
            
            return input.PadRight(lenght, pad_char[0]);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object PadLeft(string input, int lenght, string pad_char)
        {
            pad_char = "";
            
            pad_char = " ";
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(32);
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(31);
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(26);
            pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(8195);
            
            return input.PadLeft(lenght, pad_char[0]);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object cv(object o, object replace_with = null)
        {
            if (null == o)
                return o;
            if (o.ToString() == "#N/A N/A" || o.ToString() == "#N/A Field Not Applicable" || o.ToString() == "#N/A Invalid Security" || o.GetType() == typeof(ExcelDna.Integration.ExcelError))
            {
                if (null != replace_with)
                    return replace_with;
                return "";
            }
            return o;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object PickBucketExtrap(double val, double[] start, double[] end, double[] values)
        {
            return PickBucketInt(val, start, end, values, true);
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object CombineStrings(string delimit, string one, string two, string three)
        {
            List<string> values = new List<string>();
            foreach (string s in new string[] { one, two, three })
            {
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                    values.Add(s);
            }
            return String.Join(delimit, values.ToArray());
        }
        public static System.Data.DataTable BuildBucketDT<T>(double[] start, double[] end, T[] values)
        {
            System.Data.DataTable tbl = new System.Data.DataTable();
            tbl.Columns.Add("start", typeof(double));
            tbl.Columns.Add("end", typeof(double));
            tbl.Columns.Add("values", typeof(T));
            for (int i = 0; i != start.Length; i++)
            {
                tbl.Rows.Add(start[i], end[i], values[i]);
            }
            return tbl;
        }


        public static object PickBucketInt(double val, double[] start, double[] end, double[] values, bool extrap)
        {
            if (start.Length != end.Length || end.Length != values.Length)
                return "Lengths Wrong";

            for (int i = 0; i != start.Length; i++)
            {
                if (val > start[i] && val <= end[i])
                {
                    if (!extrap)
                        return values[i];
                    else
                    {
                        System.Data.DataTable tbl = BuildBucketDT(start, end, values);
                        double answer = MathLib.Interpolate(val, tbl, "end", "values").Value;
                        return answer;
                    }
                }
            }

            return "no match";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object PickBucket(double val, double[] start, double[] end, object[] values, object default_value)
        {
            if (start.Length != end.Length || end.Length != values.Length)
                return "Lenghts Wrong";

            for (int i = 0; i != start.Length; i++)
            {
                if (val > start[i] && val <= end[i])
                {
                    if (values[i].GetType() == typeof(ExcelEmpty))
                        return "";
                    return values[i];
                }
            }

            if (null != default_value)
                return default_value;
            return "no match";
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string concat(string[] values, string separator)
        {
            List<string> answer = new List<string>();
            foreach (string s in values)
            {
                if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s))
                    answer.Add(s);
            }

            return String.Join(separator, answer);
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Hides sheets listed in 'hideSheets' range and unhides sheets listed in 'unhideSheets' range. Sheet names are comma-separated.")]
        public static string GenericHideUnhideSheets()
        {
            XL.XLHelper xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            Workbook wb = null;
            try
            {
                wb = xlh.ActiveWorkbook();
                if (wb == null)
                    return "No active workbook";

                string hideSheetsRaw = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "hideSheets", false, "");
                string unhideSheetsRaw = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "unhideSheets", false, "");

                List<string> sheetsToHide = hideSheetsRaw?
                    .Split(new char[] { ',' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)
                    .Select(s => s.Trim())
                    .ToList() ?? new List<string>();

                List<string> sheetsToUnhide = unhideSheetsRaw?
                    .Split(new char[] { ',' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)
                    .Select(s => s.Trim())
                    .ToList() ?? new List<string>();

                int hiddenCount = 0;
                int unhiddenCount = 0;

                foreach (Worksheet ws in wb.Worksheets)
                {
                    string sheetName = ws.Name;

                    if (sheetsToUnhide.Any(s => s.Equals(sheetName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
                    {
                        ws.Visible = XlSheetVisibility.xlSheetVisible;
                        unhiddenCount++;
                    }

                    if (sheetsToHide.Any(s => s.Equals(sheetName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
                    {
                        ws.Visible = XlSheetVisibility.xlSheetHidden;
                        hiddenCount++;
                    }
                }

                return $"Hidden: {hiddenCount}, Unhidden: {unhiddenCount}";
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return $"Error: {ex.Message}";
            }
        }

        public static void ExportAndMailInternal(List<string> to, List<string> cc, List<string> bcc, string subject, Dictionary<string,string> filetypes_by_sheets, string filename_base,  string email_body_range, bool send_automatically, bool do_timestamp = true, bool exclude_attachments = false)
        {

            var common = UtilsLib.Clean.GetCommonVariables();
            
            subject = UtilsLib.Clean.CommonVariables(subject, "/");

            List<string> filenames = new List<string>();

            string filename = null;
            string export = null;
            var type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.PDF;
            foreach (string file_type in filetypes_by_sheets.Keys)
            {
                if (file_type.ContainsIns("xlsb"))
                    type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB;
                else if (file_type.ContainsIns("xl"))
                    type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX;
                else if (file_type.ContainsIns("pdf"))
                    type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.PDF;
                else
                    type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.PDF;

                List<string> sheets= filetypes_by_sheets[file_type].Split(new char[] { ',' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries).ToList<string>();


                filename = FileLib.GetQuickUniqueFile(filename_base, file_type, false, do_timestamp);
                filenames.Add(filename);
                export = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.ExportSelectedSheetStandard(false, sheets, type, true, filename);
                File.Move(export, filename);

            }
            
            if (null != email_body_range)
            {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.CopyRangeToClipboard(null, email_body_range);
            }
            Mail.CreateOutlookMail(subject, null, filenames, to, cc, bcc, false, null, !String.IsNullOrEmpty(email_body_range), send_automatically, false, null, null);
        }

        public static void ExportAndMailInternal(List<string> to, List<string> cc, List<string> bcc, string subject, List<string> sheets, string filename_base, string file_type, string email_body_range, bool send_automatically, bool do_timestamp = true, bool exclude_attachments = false)
        {

            var common = UtilsLib.Clean.GetCommonVariables();
            
            subject = UtilsLib.Clean.CommonVariables(subject, "/");

            List<string> extensions = new List<string>();
            List<string> filenames = new List<string>();

            if (!exclude_attachments)
            {
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(file_type))
                    extensions = file_type.Split(new char[] { ',' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries).ToList<string>();
                else
                    extensions = new List<string>() { "pdf" };   

                string filename = null;
                string export = null;
                var type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.PDF;
                foreach (string s in extensions)
                {
                    if (s.ContainsIns("xlsb"))
                        type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB;
                    else if (s.ContainsIns("xl"))
                        type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX;
                    else if (s.ContainsIns("pdf"))
                        type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.PDF;
                    else
                        type = XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.PDF;

                    filename = FileLib.GetQuickUniqueFile(filename_base, s, false, do_timestamp);
                    filenames.Add(filename);
                    export = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.ExportSelectedSheetStandard(false, sheets, type, true, filename);
                    File.Move(export, filename);

                }
            }

            if (null != email_body_range)
            {
                UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.CopyRangeToClipboard(null, email_body_range);
            }
            Mail.CreateOutlookMail(subject, null, filenames, to, cc, bcc, false, null, !String.IsNullOrEmpty(email_body_range), send_automatically, false, null, null);
        }

        [ExcelFunction, ExcelMapArrayFunction]
        public static object[] UniqueValuesParamsSort(object[] one, object[] two = null, object[] three = null, object[] four = null)
        {
            object[] v = UniqueValuesParams(one, two, three, four);
            List<String> o = v.Select(n => n.ToString()).ToList<string>();
            o.Sort();
            o.Reverse();
            return o.ToArray<object>();
        }

        public enum SORT_TYPE { NORMAL, ALPHANUMERIC }
        public static object[] UniqueValuesInternal(object[] ignores, SORT_TYPE st, params object[] value_param)
        {
            ExcelReference caller = XlCall.Excel(XlCall.xlfCaller) as ExcelReference;

            List<object> vals = new List<object>();

            List<object[]> arrays = new List<object[]>();
            if (value_param.GetType() == typeof(object[]))
            {
                foreach (object o in value_param)
                {
                    if (null == o)
                        continue;
                    
                    if (o.GetType() == typeof(object[]))
                        arrays.Add((object[])o);
                    else
                    {
                        arrays.Add(value_param);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            else
            {
                if (value_param.GetType() == typeof(object[]))
                {
                    arrays.Add(value_param);
                }
                else
                    arrays.Add(value_param);
            }

            foreach (object[] values in arrays)
            {
                foreach (object s in values)
                {
                    
                    
                    if (null != s && String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s.ToString()))
                        continue;
                    
                    if (!vals.Contains(s))
                    {
                        bool should_ignore = false;
                        if (null != ignores)
                        {
                            foreach (object i in ignores)
                            {
                                if (null != i && i.Equals(s))
                                {
                                    should_ignore = true;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        if (!should_ignore && (null != s))
                        {
                            if (s.GetType() != typeof(object) && s.GetType() != typeof(ExcelDna.Integration.ExcelEmpty))
                                vals.Add(s);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            int total = (caller.RowLast - caller.RowFirst) - vals.Count;
            int items = (caller.RowLast - caller.RowFirst);
            if (items == 0)
                items = vals.Count;

            if (st == SORT_TYPE.ALPHANUMERIC)
            {
                List<string> d = vals.Select(n => n.ToString()).ToList();
                vals = d.OrderByOrdinal(n => n).Cast<object>().ToList();
                
            }

            if (total < 0)
                return vals.Take(items + 1).ToArray();

            for (int i = 0; i != total + 1; i++)
                vals.Add("");

            return vals.ToArray();
        }



        [ExcelFunction]
        public static bool InStr(string cell,string checking)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cell))
                return false;
            return cell.Contains(checking);
        }
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static bool InStrIns(string cell,string checking)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cell))
                return false;
            return cell.ContainsIns(checking);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static bool ContainsSameValues(string[] one, string[] two)
        {
            List<string> one_l = new List<string>(one);
            List<string> two_l = new List<string>(two);
            return one.ContainsSameValues(two);
        }
        public static bool ContainsObject<T>(List<T> list,T o)
        {
            foreach(T obj in list)
            {
                if (obj.ToString() == o.ToString())
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }


        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string FormNote(string[] headers, string[] checks)
        {
            if (headers.Length != checks.Length)
                throw new Exception("WRONG LENGTHS");
            List<string> notes = new List<string>();
            int i = 0;
            foreach(string s in checks)
            {
                if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                {
                    notes.Add(headers[i]);
                }
                i++;
            }
            return String.Join(Environment.NewLine, notes);
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static string UpdateZillowBulk(int hpitype_id,string[] zip_str, string[] date_strings, object[,] values)
        {
            if (date_strings.Length != values.GetLength(1))
            {
                return "Date array <> values array";
            }
            List<Query> bulk = new List<Query>();
            int lines = values.GetLength(0);
            ETA eta = new ETA(lines, UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel.WriteStatusBar);
            
            bool check_exist = true;
            List<string> bulk_query = new List<string>();
            string filename_bulk = @"C:\temp\zillow.sql";
            for (int l = 0;l != lines; l++)
            {
                List<DateTime> dates = null;
                for (int i = 0; i != date_strings.Length; i++)
                {
                    double d = System.Convert.ToDouble(date_strings[i]);
                    DateTime asOf = DateTime.FromOADate(d);
                    
                    object o = values[l,i];
                    if (null == o)
                        continue;
                    string value_raw = o.ToString();

                    
                    if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(value_raw) || (null != o && o.GetType() == typeof(ExcelDna.Integration.ExcelEmpty)))
                        continue;
                    Nullable<double> value = System.Convert.ToDouble(value_raw);
                   
                    int zip = System.Convert.ToInt32(zip_str[l]);
                    if (null == value)
                        continue;
                    if (check_exist)
                    {
                        if (null == dates)
                        {
                            dates = Assets.Collat.HPIList(UnlockToolkit.DB, hpitype_id, zip);
                        }
                        
                        bool exists = dates.Contains(asOf.SetDay(1));
                        if (exists)
                            continue;
                    }


                    Query q = Assets.Collat.GetZillowSQL(UnlockToolkit.DB, hpitype_id, zip, asOf.ToString("MM/dd/yyyy"), value);
                    string sql = Assets.Collat.GetZillowSQLTxt(UnlockToolkit.DB, hpitype_id, zip, asOf.ToString("MM/dd/yyyy"), value);
                    

                    bulk_query.Add(sql);


                    if (null != q)
                        bulk.Add(q);
                    

                }
                if (bulk_query.Count > 0)
                {
                    string bulk_sqls = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bulk_query.ToArray());
                    
                    Query b = new Query(bulk_sqls, UnlockToolkit.DB);
                    b.Execute();
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                }
            }



            
            
            
            
            
            
            return filename_bulk;
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Clears all cells and objects outside the Print_Area (and Print_Titles) in every worksheet of the active workbook.")]
        public static string ClearAllButPrintArea()
        {
            var xlh = UnlockToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            Workbook wb = null;
            try
            {
                wb = xlh.ActiveWorkbook();
                if (wb == null) return "No active workbook";
                var app = wb.Application;
                
                var prevCalc = app.Calculation;
                var prevSU = app.ScreenUpdating;
                var prevEvents = app.EnableEvents;
                var prevAlerts = app.DisplayAlerts;

                app.ScreenUpdating = false;
                app.EnableEvents = false;
                app.DisplayAlerts = false;
                app.Calculation = XlCalculation.xlCalculationManual;

                foreach (Worksheet ws in wb.Worksheets)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        string printArea = ws.PageSetup.PrintArea;
                        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(printArea))
                            continue;

                        Range pr;
                        try
                        {
                            pr = ws.Range[printArea];
                        }
                        catch
                        {
                            
                            continue;
                        }

                        var ur = ws.UsedRange;
                        if (ur == null || (ur.Rows.Count == 1 && ur.Columns.Count == 1 && (ur.Value2 == null || string.IsNullOrEmpty(ur.Text as string))))
                        {
                            Marshal.ReleaseComObject(pr);
                            continue;
                        }

                        var keepRows = new List<Tuple<int, int>>();
                        var keepCols = new List<Tuple<int, int>>();

                        
                        foreach (Range area in pr.Areas)
                        {
                            int r1 = area.Row;
                            int r2 = area.Row + area.Rows.Count - 1;
                            int c1 = area.Column;
                            int c2 = area.Column + area.Columns.Count - 1;
                            keepRows.Add(Tuple.Create(r1, r2));
                            keepCols.Add(Tuple.Create(c1, c2));
                            Marshal.ReleaseComObject(area);
                        }

                        
                        try
                        {
                            string titleRows = ws.PageSetup.PrintTitleRows;
                            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(titleRows))
                            {
                                Range tr = null;
                                try
                                {
                                    tr = ws.Range[titleRows];
                                    foreach (Range area in tr.Areas)
                                    {
                                        int r1 = area.Row;
                                        int r2 = area.Row + area.Rows.Count - 1;
                                        keepRows.Add(Tuple.Create(r1, r2));
                                        Marshal.ReleaseComObject(area);
                                    }
                                }
                                catch {  }
                                finally { if (tr != null) Marshal.ReleaseComObject(tr); }
                            }

                            string titleCols = ws.PageSetup.PrintTitleColumns;
                            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(titleCols))
                            {
                                Range tc = null;
                                try
                                {
                                    tc = ws.Range[titleCols];
                                    foreach (Range area in tc.Areas)
                                    {
                                        int c1 = area.Column;
                                        int c2 = area.Column + area.Columns.Count - 1;
                                        keepCols.Add(Tuple.Create(c1, c2));
                                        Marshal.ReleaseComObject(area);
                                    }
                                }
                                catch {  }
                                finally { if (tc != null) Marshal.ReleaseComObject(tc); }
                            }
                        }
                        catch
                        {
                            
                        }

                        
                        keepRows = MergeIntervals(keepRows);
                        keepCols = MergeIntervals(keepCols);

                        int usedFirstRow = ur.Row;
                        int usedLastRow = ur.Row + ur.Rows.Count - 1;
                        int usedFirstCol = ur.Column;
                        int usedLastCol = ur.Column + ur.Columns.Count - 1;

                        
                        var clearRowIntervals = ComplementIntervals(usedFirstRow, usedLastRow, keepRows);
                        foreach (var rng in clearRowIntervals)
                        {
                            string rowAddr = $"{rng.Item1}:{rng.Item2}";
                            try { ws.Range[rowAddr].Clear(); } catch {  }
                        }

                        
                        var clearColIntervals = ComplementIntervals(usedFirstCol, usedLastCol, keepCols);
                        foreach (var rng in clearColIntervals)
                        {
                            try
                            {
                                Range colRange = ws.Range[ws.Cells[1, rng.Item1], ws.Cells[1, rng.Item2]].EntireColumn;
                                colRange.Clear();
                                Marshal.ReleaseComObject(colRange);
                            }
                            catch {  }
                        }

                        
                        for (int i = ws.Shapes.Count; i >= 1; i--)
                        {
                            Shape sh = null;
                            try
                            {
                                sh = ws.Shapes.Item(i);
                                Range tl = sh.TopLeftCell;
                                Range br = sh.BottomRightCell;

                                int tlr = tl.Row, tlc = tl.Column;
                                int brr = br.Row, brc = br.Column;

                                bool rowsIntersect = RangeIntersects(keepRows, Math.Min(tlr, brr), Math.Max(tlr, brr));
                                bool colsIntersect = RangeIntersects(keepCols, Math.Min(tlc, brc), Math.Max(tlc, brc));

                                if (!(rowsIntersect && colsIntersect))
                                {
                                    sh.Delete();
                                }

                                Marshal.ReleaseComObject(tl);
                                Marshal.ReleaseComObject(br);
                            }
                            catch
                            {
                                
                            }
                            finally
                            {
                                if (sh != null) Marshal.ReleaseComObject(sh);
                            }
                        }

                        Marshal.ReleaseComObject(ur);
                        Marshal.ReleaseComObject(pr);
                    }
                    catch
                    {
                        
                    }
                }

                
                app.Calculation = prevCalc;
                app.DisplayAlerts = prevAlerts;
                app.EnableEvents = prevEvents;
                app.ScreenUpdating = prevSU;

                return "OK";
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return $"Error: {ex.Message}";
            }
        }

        private static List<Tuple<int, int>> MergeIntervals(List<Tuple<int, int>> ranges)
        {
            if (ranges == null || ranges.Count == 0)
                return new List<Tuple<int, int>>();

            var sorted = ranges
                .OrderBy(r => r.Item1)
                .ThenBy(r => r.Item2)
                .ToList();

            var merged = new List<Tuple<int, int>>();

            int curStart = sorted[0].Item1;
            int curEnd = sorted[0].Item2;

            for (int i = 1; i < sorted.Count; i++)
            {
                var r = sorted[i];

                if (r.Item1 <= curEnd + 1)
                {
                    curEnd = Math.Max(curEnd, r.Item2);
                }
                else
                {
                    merged.Add(Tuple.Create(curStart, curEnd));
                    curStart = r.Item1;
                    curEnd = r.Item2;
                }
            }

            merged.Add(Tuple.Create(curStart, curEnd));
            return merged;
        }

        private static List<Tuple<int, int>> ComplementIntervals(int start, int end, List<Tuple<int, int>> keep)
        {
            var result = new List<Tuple<int, int>>();
            if (start > end)
                return result;

            if (keep == null || keep.Count == 0)
            {
                result.Add(Tuple.Create(start, end));
                return result;
            }

            var merged = MergeIntervals(keep)
                .Where(k => k.Item2 >= start && k.Item1 <= end)
                .Select(k => Tuple.Create(Math.Max(k.Item1, start), Math.Min(k.Item2, end)))
                .OrderBy(k => k.Item1)
                .ToList();

            int cur = start;
            foreach (var k in merged)
            {
                if (cur < k.Item1)
                    result.Add(Tuple.Create(cur, k.Item1 - 1));

                cur = k.Item2 + 1;
            }

            if (cur <= end)
                result.Add(Tuple.Create(cur, end));

            return result;
        }
        private static bool RangeIntersects(List<Tuple<int, int>> keep, int s, int e)
        {
            foreach (var k in keep)
            {
                if (e < k.Item1 || s > k.Item2)
                    continue;

                return true;
            }

            return false;
        }




    }
}

        public static bool InsertValuation(string asset_id, int valuationtype_id,DateTime asOf,double value,string identifier,string link)
        {

            if (valuation_exists)
                return false;
            BadgerLib.Valuations.InsertValidation(UnlockToolkit.DB, asset_id, asOf, valuationtype_id, value, null, null, null, "Excel Import", 0, null, null, identifier, link);

        [ExcelFunction(Description ="WARNING: Can't do settlements > 2 months out yet")]
        public static double RA(string cusip, double oface, double cface, double price, double finance_rate, double cpr, DateTime buy_settle, DateTime sell_settle,string return_value = null)
        {
            if (!Validate.IsValidInput(cusip))
                return -99999999999999;

            
            
                



            var ra = Assets.Analytics.RA(cusip, oface, cface, price, finance_rate, cpr, buy_settle, sell_settle);
            if (null == return_value)
                return_value = "drop_in_tics";
            switch (return_value)
            {
                case "net_accrued_int":
                    return ra.net_accrued_int;
                case "net_accrued_int_eom":
                    return ra.net_accrued_int_eom;
                case "remit_interest":
                    return ra.remit_interest;
                case "remit_principal":
                    return ra.remit_principal;
                case "remit_total":
                    return ra.remit_total;
                case "funding_cost":
                    return ra.funding_cost;
                case "price":
                    return ra.price;
                case "drop_in_tics":
                    return ra.drop_in_tics;
                case "total_interest":
                    return ra.total_interest;
                case "total_net_interest":
                    return ra.total_net_interest;
                case "eom_accrued":
                    return ra.eom_accrued;
                case "total_net_interest_eom":
                    return ra.total_net_interest_eom;
                case "sell_accrued_int_eom":
                    return ra.sell_accrued_int_eom;
                case "buy_accrued_int":
                    return ra.buy_accrued_int;
                case "sell_accrued_int":
                    return ra.sell_accrued_int;
                case "drop_due_to_principal":
                    return ra.drop_due_to_principal;
                case "drop_in_$":
                    return ra.drop_in_dec / 100 * cface;

            }

            return -9999999999;
        }





        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object IsHoliday(DateTime date)
        {
            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime d = new UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime(date);
            return d.IsHoliday;
        }




       
        
    }

--- FILE: Unlock Toolkit\Unlock Toolkit\Zillow.cs ---
namespace Unlock_Toolkit
{
    public class Zillow
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object GetZillowDataZip(int zip5,string return_value)
        {
            object o = GetZillowDataInternal("Zip", zip5.ToString("D5"),return_value);
            if (null == o)
                o = "<not found>";
            return o;
        }

        public static object GetZillowDataInternal(string region, string region_name,string ret_val)
        {
            string sql = "select * from ZillowHPI where region = @region and region_name = @region_name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, UnlockToolkit.DB);
            q.AddParameter("@region", region);
            q.AddParameter("@region_name", region_name);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<object>(ret_val);
        }


    }
}

namespace BatCave

        public void HandleSignalR(string server)
        {
            _bat_signal = new SignalRClient();
            
            string ip_address = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.SIGNALR_SERVER);
            if (Environment.UserName.ContainsIns("dfoster"))
            {
                bool local_server_running = UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.ProcessRunning("BatSignal.exe", 1000);
                if(local_server_running)
                    ip_address = "http:
            }

            _bat_signal = new SignalRClient();
            _bat_signal.Init(ip_address);

            _bat_signal.Connect();

            
            
            
            _bat_signal.HookUpEvent<string>("BatSignal", DoBatMessage);
            _bat_signal.HookUpEvent<AlertHelper>("GenericAlert", GenericAlert);
            _bat_signal.HookUpEvent<Classes.RestartHelper>("Restart", Restart);
            _bat_signal.HookUpEvent<AssetUpdateHelperSignal>("UpdateAsset", InsertUpdateIfNeeded);
            _bat_signal.HookUpEvent<List<BatSignalLib.Classes.Users>>("DumpConnectionHandle", DumpConnectionHandle);

            SubScribeToSignalRGroups();
        }

        public void SubScribeToSignalRGroups()
        {
            List<string> preferred_prods = BatCaveLib.Products.GetPreferredProductNames(this.server, false);
            foreach (string prod in preferred_prods)
            {
                _bat_signal.GroupSubscribe(prod);
            }

            List<string> trading_permissions = BatCaveLib.Permissions.GetTradingProductAlerts(this.server);
            foreach (string prod in trading_permissions)
            {
                
                string trading_group = BatSignalLib.Utils.CalcTraderAlertGroup(prod);
                _bat_signal.GroupSubscribe(trading_group);
            }

            _bat_signal.GroupSubscribe(Environment.UserName.ToUpper());
        }


        
        public void DoBatMessage(string message)
        {
            string hot_text = null;
            int seconds_delay = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.ALERT_DELAY);

            mainAlertControl.AutoFormDelay = seconds_delay * 1000;
            this.Invoke((Action) (() => mainAlertControl.Show(this,"Bat Signal", message, hot_text, _img_cache, null)));
        }



        public void InsertUpdateIfNeeded(AssetUpdateHelperSignal ah)
        {
            
            foreach (string asset in ah.assets)
            {
                MT.InsertUpdateIfNeeded(ah.server, asset, ah.force, ah.include_bulk, ah.db_fields, ah.do_not_update_if_in_db);
            }
        }

        public void DumpConnectionHandle(List<BatSignalLib.Classes.Users> users)
        {
            List<string> sent_to = new List<string>();

            ETA eta = new ETA(users.Count, Console.WriteLine);
            users.Shuffle();

            List<string> exempts = new List<string>(Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_BBG_EXEMPT).Split(';'));
            exempts = exempts.Select(n => n.Replace(@"US\","")).ToList();


            if (Environment.UserName.ToUpper() == "DFOSTER" && Environment.MachineName == "MHN-D-U13476" && System.Convert.ToDateTime("2/13/2020") == DateTime.Today)
            {

                List<string> assets = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetNeededUpdatedAssets(server, null);

                int max_to_send = 250;
                foreach (var user in users)
                {
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();

                    if (sent_to.Contains(user.user_id) || exempts.Contains(user.user_id))
                        continue;

                    AssetUpdateHelperSignal ah = new AssetUpdateHelperSignal();
                    var allocated = assets.Take(max_to_send);
                    assets = assets.Except(allocated).ToList();
                    ah.assets = new List<string>(allocated);
                    ah.do_not_update_if_in_db = false;
                    ah.force = false;
                    ah.server = this.server;
                    ah.include_bulk = false;
                    ah.db_fields = new List<string>() { "ticker", "cusip", "bbg_id", "collat_type", "deal_type", "negam_collat_pct", "issue_date", "master_servicer", "mtg_type_long", "coupon_type ", "security_type", "yield_maint", "mtg_type", "market_sector", "prepay_type" };
                    ah.group = user.user_id;

                    _bat_signal.UpdateAsset(ah);

                    sent_to.Add(user.user_id);
                }
            }
    }

            System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(rh.seconds*1000);
            Utils.RestartApp(this.server);
        }

            }
            else
                this.Invoke((Action) (() => mainAlertControl.Show(this, caption, message, hot_text, _img_cache, ah)));
        }

namespace BatCave
{
    public class Bond
    {
        string _server;
        public Bond(string server)
        {
            _server = server;
        }
        public void RefreshFromAssetDB()
        {
            string sql = "select * from Assets where ticker = @ticker";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker<varchar>", ticker);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (tbl.Rows.Count != 1)
                throw new Exception("No Bond");
            DataRow row = tbl.Rows[0];

            this.ticker = row["ticker"].ToString(); ;
            this.oface = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["oface"]);
        }
        public string ticker;
        public double oface;
        public double cface;


        
    }
}
