namespace BatCave
{
    public class BWIC
    {
        List<Bond> bonds = new List<Bond>();
        string _server;
        public Nullable<int> account_id;
        public Nullable<DateTime> bid_time;
        public string list_name;
        public bool indirect;
        public Nullable<int> bwic_id;
        public Nullable<int> product_id_override;

        public void AddBond(string ticker)
        {
            Bond b = new Bond(_server);
            b.ticker = ticker;
            bonds.Add(b);
        }

        public void WriteBondsToDatabase()
        {
            foreach(Bond b in bonds)
            {

            }
        }

        

        public BWIC(string server)
        {
            _server = server;
        }
        public void PopulateFromDB(int bwic_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBWICs where bwic_id = @bwic_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@bwic_id", bwic_id);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (tbl.Rows.Count != 1)
                throw new Exception("Wrong Row Count");
            DataRow row = tbl.Rows[0];


            if (DBNull.Value != row["bid_time"])
                this.bid_time = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["bid_time"]);
            else
                this.bid_time = null;

            if (DBNull.Value != row["list_name"])
                this.list_name = row["list_name"].ToString();
            else
                this.list_name = null;

            if (DBNull.Value != row["bwic_id"])
                this.bwic_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["bwic_id"]);

            this.indirect = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["indirect"]);


            if (DBNull.Value != row["account_id"])
                this.account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["account_id"]);
            else
                this.account_id = null;

            if (DBNull.Value != row["product_id_override"])
                this.product_id_override = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["product_id_override"]);
            else
                this.product_id_override = null;

            
        }

        public int RecordUpdateBWIC()
        {
            return BatCaveLib.BWICs.InsertUpdateBWIC(_server, bwic_id, bid_time.Value, account_id, indirect, list_name, product_id_override);
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\BWICDetails.cs ---
namespace BatCave
{
    public class BWICDetails
    {


        public static void SaveTalkAndResults(string server, int bwicdetail_id, string px_talk, string results, string public_color,bool write_px_talk, bool write_results,bool write_public_color,string private_color,bool private_color_write,Nullable<int> privatecolor_id,bool write_oface,Nullable<double> oface,bool write_bid,string bid,bool write_bid_acct,Nullable<int> bid_acct,Nullable<int> bid_id,Nullable<int> px_talk_kanerai_load_id, int? results_kanerai_load_id, int? privatecolorgroup_id)
        {
            Query q = new Query("exec dbo.InsertBWICColor @bwicdetail_id=@bwicdetail_id, @px_talk=@px_talk, @results=@results,@public_color=@public_color, @px_talk_write=@px_talk_write, @results_write=@results_write, @public_color_write=@public_color_write, @private_color=@private_color, @private_color_write=@private_color_write, @privatecolor_id=@privatecolor_id, @oface_write=@oface_write, @oface=@oface, @write_bid=@write_bid, @bid=@bid, @write_bid_acct=@write_bid_acct, @bid_acct=@bid_acct, @bid_id = @bid_id, @px_talk_kanerai_load_id=@px_talk_kanerai_load_id, @results_kanerai_load_id=@results_kanerai_load_id, @privatecolorgroup_id=@privatecolorgroup_id", server);
            q.AddParameter("@bwicdetail_id", bwicdetail_id);
            q.AddParameter("@px_talk", px_talk);
            q.AddParameter("@results", results);
            q.AddParameter("@public_color", public_color);
            q.AddParameter("@px_talk_write", write_px_talk);
            q.AddParameter("@results_write", write_results);
            q.AddParameter("@public_color_write", write_public_color);
            q.AddParameter("@private_color", private_color);
            q.AddParameter("@private_color_write", private_color_write);
            q.AddParameter("@privatecolor_id", privatecolor_id);
            q.AddParameter("@oface_write", write_oface);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@write_bid", write_bid);
            q.AddParameter("@bid", bid);
            q.AddParameter("@bid_acct", bid_acct);
            q.AddParameter("@write_bid_acct", write_bid_acct);
            q.AddParameter("@bid_id", bid_id);
            q.AddParameter("@px_talk_kanerai_load_id", px_talk_kanerai_load_id);
            q.AddParameter("@results_kanerai_load_id", results_kanerai_load_id);
            q.AddParameter("@privatecolorgroup_id", privatecolorgroup_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\CellSelectionHelper.cs ---
namespace BatCave
{
    public class CellSelectionHelper : Component
    {
        private bool disposed = false;
        private string[,] selection;
        private Rectangle selectedArea = Rectangle.Empty;
        private Bitmap evenPicture;
        private Bitmap oddPicture;
        private bool even = true;
        private Timer timer;

        private const int selectionBorderWidth = 3;

        public CellSelectionHelper()
        {
            if (!DesignMode)
            {
                timer = new Timer();
                timer.Tick += new EventHandler(OnTimerTick);
                timer.Start();
            }
            selectedArea.X = int.MaxValue;
        }

        private GridView fView;
        public GridView View
        {
            get { return fView; }
            set
            {
                if (fView == value) return;
                if (fView != null)
                    UnsubscribeViewEvents();
                fView = value;
                if (value != null)
                    SubscribeViewEvents();
            }
        }

        public Bitmap EvenPicture
        {
            get
            {
                if (evenPicture == null)
                    evenPicture = CreateBitmap(true);
                return evenPicture;
            }
            set
            {
                if (evenPicture != null && evenPicture.Tag.ToString() == "DXSample")
                    evenPicture.Dispose();
                evenPicture = value;
            }
        }

        public Bitmap OddPicture
        {
            get
            {
                if (oddPicture == null)
                    oddPicture = CreateBitmap(false);
                return oddPicture;
            }
            set
            {
                if (oddPicture != null && oddPicture.Tag.ToString() == "DXSample")
                    oddPicture.Dispose();
                oddPicture = value;
            }
        }

        private void OnGridViewKeyDown(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            switch (e.KeyCode)
            {
                case Keys.C:
                    if (e.Control)
                    {
                        ClearSelection();
                        GridCell[] cells = fView.GetSelectedCells();
                        if (cells.Length == 0) return;
                        int minCol, minRow, maxCol, maxRow;
                        minCol = minRow = int.MaxValue;
                        maxCol = maxRow = 0;
                        foreach (GridCell cell in cells)
                        {
                            minCol = Math.Min(cell.Column.VisibleIndex, minCol);
                            minRow = Math.Min(cell.RowHandle, minRow);
                            maxCol = Math.Max(cell.Column.VisibleIndex, maxCol);
                            maxRow = Math.Max(cell.RowHandle, maxRow);
                        }
                        if ((maxCol - minCol + 1) * (maxRow - minRow + 1) != cells.Length)
                        {
                            XtraMessageBox.Show("This action won't work on multiple selections.");
                            e.SuppressKeyPress = true;
                            break;
                        }
                        selection = new string[maxCol - minCol + 1, maxRow - minRow + 1];
                        foreach (GridCell cell in cells)
                            selection[cell.Column.VisibleIndex - minCol, cell.RowHandle - minRow] =
                                fView.GetRowCellValue(cell.RowHandle, cell.Column).ToString();
                        selectedArea = new Rectangle(minCol, minRow, maxCol - minCol, maxRow - minRow);
                    }
                    break;
                case Keys.V:
                    if (e.Control)
                    {
                        Clipboard.Clear();
                        fView.GridControl.BeginInvoke(new MethodInvoker(Paste));
                    }
                    break;
                case Keys.Escape: ClearSelection(); break;
            }
        }

        private void Paste()
        {
            if (selection == null) return;
            for (int i = 0; i <= selectedArea.Width; i++)
            for (int j = 0; j <= selectedArea.Height; j++)
            {
                if (i + fView.FocusedColumn.VisibleIndex > fView.VisibleColumns.Count - 1 ||
                    j + fView.FocusedRowHandle > fView.RowCount - 1) continue;
                fView.SetRowCellValue(j + fView.FocusedRowHandle,
                    fView.VisibleColumns[i + fView.FocusedColumn.VisibleIndex], selection[i, j]);
            }
        }

        private Bitmap CreateBitmap(bool even)
        {
            if (fView == null) return null;
            Bitmap result = new Bitmap(fView.GridControl.Bounds.Width, fView.GridControl.Bounds.Height);
            using (Graphics g = Graphics.FromImage(result))
            {
                System.Drawing.Color foreColor = even ? System.Drawing.Color.AliceBlue : System.Drawing.Color.AntiqueWhite;
                System.Drawing.Color backColor = even ? System.Drawing.Color.AntiqueWhite : System.Drawing.Color.AliceBlue;
                using (Brush brush = new HatchBrush(HatchStyle.BackwardDiagonal, foreColor, backColor))
                {
                    g.FillRectangle(brush, new Rectangle(Point.Empty, result.Size));
                }
            }
            result.Tag = "DXSample";
            return result;
        }

        private void OnGridViewCustomDrawCell(object sender, RowCellCustomDrawEventArgs e)
        {
            if (selectedArea.X == int.MaxValue) return;
            Rectangle drawingArea = Rectangle.Empty;
            if (e.RowHandle == selectedArea.Top && IsPointInRange(e.Column.VisibleIndex, false))
            {
                drawingArea = new Rectangle(e.Bounds.X, e.Bounds.Y, e.Bounds.Width, selectionBorderWidth);
                if (e.Column.VisibleIndex == selectedArea.Left)
                {
                    drawingArea.X += selectionBorderWidth;
                    drawingArea.Width -= selectionBorderWidth;
                }
            }
            if (drawingArea != Rectangle.Empty)
            {
                DrawArea(e.Graphics, drawingArea);
                drawingArea = Rectangle.Empty;
            }
            if (e.RowHandle == selectedArea.Bottom && IsPointInRange(e.Column.VisibleIndex, false))
            {
                drawingArea = new Rectangle(e.Bounds.X, e.Bounds.Bottom - selectionBorderWidth, e.Bounds.Width, selectionBorderWidth);
                if (e.Column.VisibleIndex == selectedArea.Right) drawingArea.Width -= selectionBorderWidth;
            }
            if (drawingArea != Rectangle.Empty)
            {
                DrawArea(e.Graphics, drawingArea);
                drawingArea = Rectangle.Empty;
            }
            if (e.Column.VisibleIndex == selectedArea.Left && IsPointInRange(e.RowHandle, true))
            {
                drawingArea = new Rectangle(e.Bounds.X, e.Bounds.Y, selectionBorderWidth, e.Bounds.Height);
                if (e.RowHandle == selectedArea.Bottom) drawingArea.Height -= selectionBorderWidth;
            }
            if (drawingArea != Rectangle.Empty)
            {
                DrawArea(e.Graphics, drawingArea);
                drawingArea = Rectangle.Empty;
            }
            if (e.Column.VisibleIndex == selectedArea.Right && IsPointInRange(e.RowHandle, true))
            {
                drawingArea = new Rectangle(e.Bounds.Right - selectionBorderWidth, e.Bounds.Y, selectionBorderWidth,
                    e.Bounds.Height);
                if (e.RowHandle == selectedArea.Top)
                {
                    drawingArea.Y += selectionBorderWidth;
                    drawingArea.Height -= selectionBorderWidth;
                }
            }
            if (drawingArea != Rectangle.Empty) DrawArea(e.Graphics, drawingArea);
            if (IsPointInRange(e.RowHandle, true) && IsPointInRange(e.Column.VisibleIndex, false))
            {
                GridCellInfo info = e.Cell as GridCellInfo;
                e.Appearance.DrawString(e.Cache, e.DisplayText, info.CellValueRect);
                e.Handled = true;
            }
        }

        private void DrawArea(Graphics g, Rectangle area)
        {
            area.Inflate(1, 1);
            using (Brush brush = new TextureBrush(even ? EvenPicture : OddPicture))
            {
                g.FillRectangle(brush, area);
            }
        }

        private bool IsPointInRange(int point, bool vertical)
        {
            if (vertical) return point >= selectedArea.Top && point <= selectedArea.Bottom;
            else return point >= selectedArea.Left && point <= selectedArea.Right;
        }

        private void OnTimerTick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            even = !even;
            if (selectedArea.X == int.MaxValue) return;
            for (int i = selectedArea.Left; i <= selectedArea.Right; i++)
            for (int j = selectedArea.Top; j <= selectedArea.Bottom; j++)
                fView.InvalidateRowCell(j, fView.VisibleColumns[i]);
        }

        private void ClearSelection()
        {
            selection = null;
            selectedArea.X = int.MaxValue;
            fView.Invalidate();
        }

        protected override void Dispose(bool disposing)
        {
            if (!disposed && disposing)
            {
                if (fView != null)
                {
                    UnsubscribeViewEvents();
                    fView = null;
                }
                if (evenPicture != null && object.ReferenceEquals(evenPicture.Tag, "DXSample"))
                {
                    evenPicture.Dispose();
                    evenPicture = null;
                }
                if (evenPicture != null && object.ReferenceEquals(oddPicture.Tag, "DXSample"))
                {
                    oddPicture.Dispose();
                    oddPicture = null;
                }
                if (timer != null)
                {
                    timer.Stop();
                    timer.Tick -= new EventHandler(OnTimerTick);
                    timer.Dispose();
                    timer = null;
                }
                disposed = true;
            }
            base.Dispose(disposing);
        }

        private void SubscribeViewEvents()
        {
            fView.KeyDown += new KeyEventHandler(OnGridViewKeyDown);
            fView.CustomDrawCell += new RowCellCustomDrawEventHandler(OnGridViewCustomDrawCell);
        }

        private void UnsubscribeViewEvents()
        {
            fView.KeyDown -= new KeyEventHandler(OnGridViewKeyDown);
            fView.CustomDrawCell -= new RowCellCustomDrawEventHandler(OnGridViewCustomDrawCell);
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Color.cs ---
namespace BatCave
{
    public class Color
    {

        public static DataSet SearchRaw(string server,string raw_bonds,Form parent_form,bool splash,List<int> account_ids,bool include_bids,bool include_bwics, bool include_color,bool include_trace, bool include_portfolios,bool include_matchers,bool allow_all_cusips, bool include_trades,bool run_color_filter, bool include_todays_bwics,bool deal_search_mode,bool orig_sort,bool include_scratchpad, bool include_memarks,bool include_orders, bool include_news, bool include_malls, List<int> products,bool include_color_table,bool process_row_colors,bool include_new_issue_px, bool include_offers, bool include_ooc_bids)
        {
            DataSet results = null;
            try
            {
                
                if (splash)
                    SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(parent_form, false, false, null, null);

                List<string> tickers = new List<string>();

                Assets.Assets.BondMatchHelper bonds = new Assets.Assets.BondMatchHelper();
                if (deal_search_mode || (null != raw_bonds && raw_bonds.Contains("%")))
                {
                    List<string> deals = new List<string>();
                    foreach(string s in raw_bonds.Split('\n'))
                    {
                        string raw = s.ToUpper().Trim();
                        if (!deals.Contains(raw) && !String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(raw))
                            deals.Add(raw);
                    }
                    
                    if (raw_bonds.Contains("%"))
                    {
                        tickers = BatCaveLib.Color.GetTickersFromWildCard(server,deals);

                    }
                    else
                    {
                        
                        foreach (string s in deals)
                        {
                            string ticker = BatCaveLib.Color.GetSingleTickerFromDeal(server, s);
                            if (!tickers.Contains(ticker))
                                tickers.Add(ticker);
                        }
                    }
                    foreach(string s in tickers.Distinct())
                    {
                        Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper bph = new Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper();
                        bph.ticker = s;
                        
                        {
                            bonds.AddMatched(bph);
                        }
                    }
                    
                }
                else
                {
                    bonds = Assets.Assets.CleanUpAndUpdate(server, raw_bonds, '\n', true, true);
                }
              
                if(deal_search_mode)
                {
                    int max_to_insert = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_MAX_DEAL_INSERT);
                    List<string> all_tickers_from_deal = BatCaveLib.Color.GetAllTickersFromDealAndEnsureAllLoaded(server, bonds.matched_simple, max_to_insert);
                    foreach (string s in all_tickers_from_deal)
                    {
                        var v = new Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper();
                        v.ticker = s;
                        if(!bonds.matched_simple.Contains(s))
                            bonds.AddMatched(v);
                    }
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                }

                Database.DBUtils.RecordUsage(server, 2, bonds.matched_count,null, null,null,true);

                if (bonds.notmatched.Count > 0)
                {
                    if (splash && null != SplashScreenManager.Default && SplashScreenManager.Default.IsSplashFormVisible)
                        SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
                    string matched = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.notmatched.ToArray());
                    string errors = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.errors.ToArray());
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Couldn't match: " + matched + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + errors, "Oops");
                }
                if(!allow_all_cusips && bonds.matched_count == 0)
                {
                    if (splash && null != SplashScreenManager.Default && SplashScreenManager.Default.IsSplashFormVisible)
                        SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("ERROR: No bonds selected");
                    return null;
                }
                
                results = BatCaveLib.Color.SearchBase(server, bonds.matched_simple, account_ids, include_bids, include_bwics, include_color, include_trace, include_portfolios, include_matchers, include_trades, run_color_filter, include_todays_bwics, include_scratchpad, include_memarks, include_orders, include_news, include_malls, products, include_color_table, process_row_colors, include_new_issue_px, include_offers, include_ooc_bids);

                string color_table = "Main";
                if (null != results && results.Tables.Contains(color_table) && results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Contains("oface") && results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Contains("cface"))
                {
                    foreach (var v in bonds.matched_list)
                    {
                        if (null != v.oface)
                        {
                            string sql = String.Format("ticker = '{0}'", v.ticker);
                            DataRow[] rows = results.Tables[color_table].Select(sql);
                            foreach(DataRow row in rows)
                            {
                                if (!results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Contains("custom_size"))
                                {
                                    DataColumn c = results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Add("custom_size", typeof(bool));
                                    c.DefaultValue = false;
                                }
                                if (DBNull.Value != row["oface"] && DBNull.Value != row["cface"])
                                {
                                    row["custom_size"] = true;
                                    double factor = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["cface"]) / System.Convert.ToDouble(row["oface"]);
                                    row["oface"] = v.oface/1e6;
                                    row["cface"] = (v.oface * factor) / 1e6;
                                }

                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (orig_sort)
                {
                    if (results.Tables.Count > 0)
                    {
                        results.Tables[0].Columns.Add("row_order", typeof(int));
                        int i = 0;
                        foreach (Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper s in bonds.matched_list)
                        {
                            string search = "ticker";
                            if (UtilsLib.Validate.IsCusip(s.ticker))
                            {
                                search = "cusip";
                            }
                            string sql = String.Format("[{0}] = '{1}'", search, s.ticker);
                            DataRow[] matches = results.Tables[0].Select(sql);
                            foreach (DataRow row in matches)
                            {
                                row["row_order"] = i;
                            }
                            i++;
                        }
                        
                        
                        results.Tables[0].DefaultView.Sort = "row_order asc";
                    }
                }
                
                
                
                
                
                
            }
            finally
            {
                if (splash && null != SplashScreenManager.Default && SplashScreenManager.Default.IsSplashFormVisible)
                    SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
            }
            return results;
        }

        
    }

}

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\Axe Helper\AxeSettingsDefault.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper
{
    public class AxeSettingsDefault : IAxeSettings
    {
        public virtual bool SupportsRating
        {
            get { return true;  }
        }

        public virtual bool PublishByDefault
        {
            get { return false;  }
        }

        public virtual int? PublishByDefaultGroup
        {
            get { return CommonInterfaces.Constants.BatCave.PUBLIC_COLOR_ID; }
        }

        public virtual bool ShowTag
        {
            get { return true;  }
        }


        public virtual string NotionalLabel
        {
            get { return "OFACE:"; }
        }

        public virtual string TickerLabel
        {
            get
            {
                return "FULL TICKER:";

            }
        } 
        public virtual string LevelLabel
        {
            get
            {
                return "LEVEL:";

            }
        }

        public virtual bool ShowAccount
        {
            get
            {
                return true;
            }
        }

        public virtual bool SupportsAxeFilter()
        {
            return false;
        }

        
        public virtual string OFACE_MASK
        {
            get { return "f3"; }

namespace BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper
{
    public partial class ctrlAxeCMBSHelper : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl, IAxeHelper
    {
        public ctrlAxeCMBSHelper()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private UpdateFilter _filter_update;
        private UpdateFilterEx _filter_updateEx;
        public void SetFilterDelegate(UpdateFilter uf)
        {
            _filter_update = uf;
        }
        public void SetFilterDelegateEx(UpdateFilterEx uf)
        {
            _filter_updateEx = uf;
        }

        public delegate void UpdateFilter(string column, string filter_str);
        public delegate void UpdateFilterEx(string column, CriteriaOperator filter_str);


        public void StartOver()
        {
            StartOverInternal(this.Controls);
            ApplyDefaultFilters();
        }

        public void StartOverInternal(ControlCollection coll)
        {
            foreach (Control c in coll)
            {
                if (c.GetType() == typeof(CheckEdit))
                {
                    CheckEdit chk = c as CheckEdit;
                    chk.Checked = false;
                }
                if (c.GetType() == typeof(RadioGroup))
                {
                    RadioGroup rg = c as RadioGroup;
                    rg.SelectedIndex = -1;
                }
                StartOverInternal(c.Controls);
            }
        }
        public void ApplyDefaultFilters()
        {
            LazyString("bond_label_1", "CMBS", true, "=");
        }
        private void chkNeedsMaxAnchored_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            CheckEdit c = sender as CheckEdit;
            LazyNumeric("anchored_retail_pct", .05, c.Checked, ">");
        }


        private void chkLowHoustonExposure_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            CheckEdit c = sender as CheckEdit;
            LazyNumeric("houston_pct", .05, c.Checked,">");
        }



        private void LazyNumeric(string column,double amt,bool selected,string sign)
        {
            string filter = String.Format("[{0}] {2} {1}",column,amt, sign);
            if (!selected)
                filter = null;
            _filter_update(column, filter);
        }

        private void LazyString(string column, string amt, bool selected, string sign)
        {
            string filter = String.Format("[{0}] {2} '{1}", column, amt, sign);
            
            CriteriaOperator c = new DevExpress.Data.Filtering.BinaryOperator(column, amt );
            if (!selected)
                filter = null;
            _filter_updateEx(column, c);
        }

        private void LazyBool(string column, bool bit)
        {
            
            
            CriteriaOperator c = new DevExpress.Data.Filtering.BinaryOperator(column, bit);
            
            
            _filter_updateEx(column, c);
        }

        private void ctrlAxeCMBSHelper_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void chkHighGWMarket_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            CheckEdit c = sender as CheckEdit;
            
        }
        private void chkLowGatewayExp_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            
        }

        private void grpGatewayMarket_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleComboBox(sender, WHICH_BOX.GATEWAY);
        }

        private void checkedListBoxControl1_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
      
        }

        private void radioGroup1_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleComboBox(sender, WHICH_BOX.VINTAGE);
        }

        public enum WHICH_BOX { VINTAGE, GATEWAY };
        private void HandleComboBox(object sender,WHICH_BOX wb)
        {
            RadioGroup rg = sender as RadioGroup;
            if (null != rg.EditValue)
            {
                string val = rg.EditValue.ToString();
                if (wb == WHICH_BOX.VINTAGE)
                    HandleVintage(val);
                if (wb == WHICH_BOX.GATEWAY)
                    HandleGateway(val);
            }
        }
        private void HandleGateway(string val)
        {
            if (val == "high")
                LazyNumeric("gateway_pct", .75, true, ">");
            else
                LazyNumeric("gateway_pct", .05, true, "<");
        }
        private void HandleVintage(string val)
        {
            if (val == "new issue")
                LazyNumeric("vintage", 2010, true, ">=");
            else
                LazyNumeric("vintage", 2010, true, "<");
        }

        private void checkedListBoxControl1_SelectedValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {


        }

        private void checkedListBoxControl1_ItemCheck(object sender, DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.ItemCheckEventArgs e)
        {
            
            
            List<string> selected = new List<string>();
            foreach (var v in checkedListBoxControl1.CheckedItems)
            {
                selected.Add(v.ToString());
            }

            string filter = "in ('" + String.Join("','", selected) + "')";
            
            CriteriaOperator c = new InOperator("tranche", selected);
            if (selected.Count == 0)
                c = null;
            _filter_updateEx("tranche", c);
        }

        private void chkHighGatewayExposure_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            CheckEdit c = sender as CheckEdit;
            LazyNumeric("gateway_pct", .3, c.Checked, ">");
        }

        private void chkBarclaysAgg_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            CheckEdit c = sender as CheckEdit;
            LazyBool("barclays_agg", c.Checked);
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlAccounts.cs ---
using PopupMenuShowingEventArgs = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.PopupMenuShowingEventArgs;

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlAccounts : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlAccounts()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }
        
        string _server;
        GridHelper _accounts;
        GridHelper _notes;
        GridHelper _trades;
        GridHelper _color;
        bool first_load = true;
        BatSignalLib.SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server,BatSignalLib.SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _accounts = new GridHelper(grdMyAccounts, _server,true, _bat_signal);
            _notes = new GridHelper(grdNotes, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _trades = new GridHelper(gridTrades, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _color = new GridHelper(gridColor, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _accounts.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            _notes.AppendPopup(viewNotes, _viewDeleteNotes);
            _color.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            _color.ToggleGroupBy(true);
            gridColor.Enabled = false;
            _notes.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            PopulateYears();
        }

        public void RefreshTab(bool force)
        {
            
            if(force || first_load)
            {
                first_load = true;
                PopulateCoverage();
                PopulateAllColor();
                first_load = false;
            }
        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            RefreshTab(true);
        }

        public void PopulateAllColor()
        {
            List<int> account_ids = viewCoverage.GetActiveRowList<int>("account_id", false);
            account_ids = account_ids.Where(n => n > 0).ToList();
            
            viewColor.ShowLoadingPanel();
            Query q = BatCaveLib.Color.GetColorQuery(_server, new List<string>(), true, true, false, false, account_ids, true, false, true, false, true, true,true);
            this.visible_columns = null;
            q.ExecuteAsync(ThingHelperTwo);
            _color.SetEnabled(true);
        }

        public void ThingHelperTwo(DataSet set)
        {
            viewColor.HideLoadingPanel();

            
            string formats = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "color", set.Tables[0], "product_id");

            _color.SetGrid(set, formats);
            
            
            this.EnableFormSafe(true);
            
            
        }


        
        private void PopulateYears()
        {
            int start_year = 2016;
            int last_year = DateTime.Now.Year;
            drpYear.Properties.Items.Add("ALL");
            for(int i = last_year; i != start_year-1;i--)
            {
                drpYear.Properties.Items.Add(i);
            }
            drpYear.EditValue = last_year;
        }

        public int StartYear
        {
            get
            {
                if (drpYear.Text == "ALL")
                    return 1920;
                else
                    return System.Convert.ToInt32(drpYear.Text);
            }
        }

        public int EndYear
        {
            get
            {
                if (drpYear.Text == "ALL")
                    return DateTime.Today.Year+1;
                else
                    return System.Convert.ToInt32(drpYear.Text);
            }
        }

        public void EnableFormSafe(bool enable)
        {
            if (base.InvokeRequired)
            {
                this.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { EnableFormSafe(enable); }));
            }
            else
            {
                this.Enabled = enable;
            }
        }

        private void _viewDeleteNotes(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Delete Account Note", this.DeleteAccountNote);
                item.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(item);
            }
        }

        private void DeleteAccountNote(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = viewNotes as GridView;
            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Are you POSITIVE you want to delete this from the database?\nIt will not be searchable later.", "Please opine.",MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
            if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                int note_id = v.GetActiveRowValue<int>("note_id");
                int id = BatCaveLib.Accounts.InsertUpdateNote(_server, -1, null, true, -1, note_id, null);
                v.DeleteRow(v.FocusedRowHandle);
            }
        }

        private void btnMissingAnAccount_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string html = _accounts.ExportToHTMLSimple();
            BatCaveLib.Accounts.SpawnMissingAccountEmail(_server, html);
        }

        private void PopulateCoverage()
        {
            
            DateTime start = new DateTime(this.StartYear,1,1).FirstDayOfYear();
            DateTime end= new DateTime(this.EndYear,1,1).LastDayOfYear();
            bool include_special = chkIncludeSpecialPermissionAccounts.Checked;
            DataSet summary = BatCaveLib.Coverage.GetAccountSummary(_server,start,end, include_special);
            _accounts.SetGrid(summary.Tables[0]);
            _accounts.HideColumn("account_id");

            viewCoverage.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
            viewCoverage.Columns["#_trades"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "#_trades", "Total: {0}");
            viewCoverage.Columns["total_commission"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "total_commission", "Total SC: {0:n0}");
            viewCoverage.Columns["total_traded_mv"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "total_traded_mv", "Total MV: {0:0.000}MM");

            _trades.SetGrid(summary.Tables[1]);
            viewTrades.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
            viewTrades.Columns["oface"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "oface", "CURR: {0:0.000}MM");
            viewTrades.Columns["cface"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "cface", "ORIG: {0:0.000}MM");
            viewTrades.Columns["market_value"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "market_value", "Total MV: {0:0.000}MM");
            viewTrades.Columns["total_commission"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "total_commission", "Total SC: {0:n0}");
            _trades.HideColumn("account_id");
            _trades.HideColumn("name");
            SetupCommissions(false);
        }

        bool is_commission_shown = false;
        private void btnShowCommission_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            if (!is_commission_shown)
            {
                BatCaveLib.Forms.frmVerifyPassword f = new BatCaveLib.Forms.frmVerifyPassword();
                f.ShowDialog();
                bool valid = f.valid_password;
                if (!valid)
                    return;
            }
            SetupCommissions(!is_commission_shown);
        }

        public void SetupCommissions(bool is_commission_shown)
        {
            string btn_label = "Show Commission";
            if(is_commission_shown)
            {
                btn_label = "Hide Commission";
            }
            btnShowCommission.Text = btn_label;
            DoCommissionHides(is_commission_shown);
            this.is_commission_shown = is_commission_shown;
        }

        private void DoCommissionHides(bool visible)
        {
            _trades.ToggleColumnVisible("repcode", visible);
            _trades.ToggleColumnVisible("total_commission", visible);
            _accounts.ToggleColumnVisible("total_commission", visible);
            
        }

        public void PopulateNotes(int account_id)
        {
            grdNotes.Enabled = !(account_id <= 0);
            DataTable notes = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountNotes(_server, account_id);
            _notes.SetGrid(notes, "asof,product_id,colorgroup_id,note");
            _notes.SetEditable(new string[] { "asof", "colorgroup_id", "product_id", "note" },null);
            DataTable colorgroups = BatCaveLib.Color.GetMyColorGroups(_server, true);
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            li.PopulateGridLookup(colorgroups, "name", "colorgroup_id");
            
            li.PopupFilterMode = PopupFilterMode.Contains;
            viewNotes.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewNotes.Columns["colorgroup_id"], li);


            RepositoryItemMemoEdit ti = new RepositoryItemMemoEdit();
            ti.WordWrap = true;
            ti.AcceptsTab = true;

            RepositoryItemRichTextEdit ni = new RepositoryItemRichTextEdit();
            ni.AcceptsTab = true;
            ni.MaxHeight = 80;


            viewNotes.OptionsView.RowAutoHeight = true;

            
            viewNotes.SetRepositoryRichTextEdit(viewNotes.Columns["note"], ni);

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            


            DataTable products = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductList(_server, false);
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit prods = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            prods.PopulateGridLookup(products, "name", "id");
            viewNotes.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewNotes.Columns["product_id"], prods);

            _notes.BestFitVisible();
            viewNotes.SetWidthSafe("asof", 90);
            viewNotes.SetWidthSafe("product_id", 90);
            viewNotes.SetWidthSafe("colorgroup_id", 70);
        }

        private void ctrlAccounts_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void viewCoverage_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            DoAccountChange();
        }
        private void DoAccountChange()
        {
            object account_id_obj = _accounts.GetActiveRowValue<object>("account_id");
            int account_id = -1;
            if (null != account_id_obj)
                account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(account_id_obj.ToString());
            
            
            
            FilterRecentColor(account_id);
            FilterTrades();
            if (account_id != -1)
            {
                PopulateNotes(account_id);
                

            }
        }

        public void FilterRecentColor(int account_id)
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            string filter = "[account_id] = '" + account_id + "'";
            _color.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(filter);
            if (null != _color._DataSet)
            {
                
                Nullable<int> product_id = _color.GetProductIdFromGrid("product_id", .50, true);
                string column_format = BatCaveLib.Utils.DefaultFormats(_server, "color", product_id);
                if (null == this.visible_columns || this.visible_columns != column_format)
                {
                    viewColor.CleanColumns(null, column_format, true);
                    _color.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(filter);
                    this.visible_columns = column_format;
                    _color.SetCustomSort("asof", "asof_sort");
                }
            }
            _color.HideColumnIfSameValue("bond_label_1");
            _color.BestFitVisible();
            _color.ToggleColumnVisible("ticker", true);
            
            
        }

        private string visible_columns = null;

        private void FilterTrades()
        {
            int account_id = _accounts.GetActiveRowValue<int>("account_id");
            string filter = "[account_id] = '" + account_id + "'";
            _trades.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(filter);
            
        }

        private void PopulateRecentColor(int account_id)
        {
            if (account_id == -1)
            {
                
                _color.ClearAutoFilter();
                return;
            }
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        public void ThingHelper()
        {
            string formats = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "color", _color._DataTable, "product_id");
            viewColor.CleanColumns(null,formats,true);
            _color.ShowColumn("ticker");
        }

        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        private void viewNotes_DoubleClick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView view = (GridView)sender;
            Point pt = view.GridControl.PointToClient(Control.MousePosition);
            GridHitInfo info = view.CalcHitInfo(pt);
            GridHitInfo info_new = view.CalcHitInfo(view.GridControl.PointToClient(System.Windows.Forms.Cursor.Position));
            view = info_new.View;
            if (null != info.Column && (info.InRow || info.InRowCell))
            {
                string note = view.GetActiveRowValue<string>("note");
                XtraMessageBox.Show(note);
            }
        }

        private void viewCoverage_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {

        }



        private void viewColor_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void viewNotes_ValidateRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.ValidateRowEventArgs e)
        {
            string group = viewNotes.GetRowValue<string>(e.RowHandle, "colorgroup_id");
            string note = viewNotes.GetRowValue<string>(e.RowHandle, "note");
            RichEditControl rich = new RichEditControl();
            rich.RtfText = note;
            note = rich.Text;


            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(group) || String.IsNullOrEmpty(note))
            {
                e.Valid = false;
                e.ErrorText = "Can't have blank note/color group";
                return;
            }

            
            Nullable<int> product_id = null;
            object o = viewNotes.GetRowValue<object>(e.RowHandle, "product_id");
            if (DBNull.Value != o)
                product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(o);

            int account_id = viewCoverage.GetActiveRowValue<int>("account_id");
            int colorgroup_id = viewNotes.GetRowValue<int>(e.RowHandle, "colorgroup_id");

            int id = BatCaveLib.Accounts.InsertUpdateNote(_server, account_id, note, false, colorgroup_id, null, product_id);
            viewNotes.SetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "note_id", id);
            viewNotes.SetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "asof", DateTime.Now);
            
            
        }

        private void viewNotes_InitNewRow(object sender, InitNewRowEventArgs e)
        {
            int? product_id = _notes.GetActiveRowValue<int>("product_id", false);
            int colorgroup_id = BatCaveLib.Color.GetDefaultColorGroup<int>(_server, "colorgroup_id",product_id);
            viewNotes.SetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "colorgroup_id", colorgroup_id);
            viewNotes.SetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "asof", DateTime.Now);
        }

        private void drpYear_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if(!first_load)
                PopulateCoverage();
        }

        private void gridColor_Enter(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void btnAllColor_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _color.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(null);
        }

        private void chkIncludeSpecialPermissionAccounts_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab(true);
        }

        private void btnShowAllAccountNotes_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable notes = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAllAccountNotes(_server);
            DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView f = new DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView();
            f.Init(_server, _bat_signal);
            string format = "date_entered,name,account,note,added_by,public";
            f.Populate(notes,format,null,null,false,"[public] = False",true);

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            f.ToggleAutoFilterRow(true);
            
            
            
            f.SetSize(1300, 700);
            f.SetWordwrap("note",null);
            f.SetColumnWidth("note", 120);
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            f.Show();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlAdmin.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlAdmin : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlAdmin()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        GridHelper _grid_coverage;
        GridHelper _grid_currnet;
        GridHelper _grid_mapping;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        private string _server;
        public void Init(string server,SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _grid_coverage = new GridHelper(gridCoverage, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _grid_currnet = new GridHelper(gridCurrent, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _grid_mapping = new GridHelper(gridTradeMapping, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            viewTradeMapping.ValidateRow += ViewTradeMapping_ValidateRow;
            _grid_mapping.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
        }



        private void ViewTradeMapping_ValidateRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.ValidateRowEventArgs e)
        {
            string counterparty_text = viewTradeMapping.GetRowValue<string>(e.RowHandle, "counterparty_text");
            Nullable<int> account_id = viewTradeMapping.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("account_id");
            BatCaveLib.Accounts.UpdateAccountMapping(_server, counterparty_text, account_id);
        }

        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            PopulateCoverage();
            PopulateAccountTypes();
            PopulatePendingMapping();
        }

        public void PopulatePendingMapping()
        {
            DateTime asOf = DateTime.Now.AddMonths(-12);
            DataTable map = BatCaveLib.Accounts.NeededAccountMapping(_server, asOf,false);
            _grid_mapping.SetGrid(map);
            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(_server);
            _grid_mapping.SetEditable(new string[] { "account_id" }, null);
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            li.PopulateGridLookup(accounts, "name", "account_id");
            li.PopupFilterMode = PopupFilterMode.Contains;
            viewTradeMapping.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewTradeMapping.Columns["account_id"], li);
            lblAccountMapping.Text = String.Format("Account Mapping - {0}", map.Rows.Count);
            
            
        }

        public void PopulateAccountTypes()
        {
            DataTable types = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountTypes(_server);
            drpAccountTypes.PopulateLookup(types, "type", "id", false);
        }

        string cvg_visible = "account_id,product_id,user_id,repcode,to_remove,seth_approved";
        private void PopulateCoverage()
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAllCoveragePending where sf_updated=0 AND ACTIVE=1 order by account";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            DataTable pending = q.ExecuteTable();

            sql = "select * from vAllCoverage where clone=0 order by account";
            Query c = new Query(sql, _server);
            DataTable d = c.ExecuteTable();
            _grid_currnet.SetGrid(d, null, null, null, false,null,false);
            

            _grid_coverage.SetGrid(pending, cvg_visible, null,null,false,null,false);
            
            
            _grid_coverage.SetEditable(new string[] { "account_id", "product_id" ,"user_id", "to_remove", "seth_approved" }, null);


            viewCoverage.OptionsView.ShowAutoFilterRow = true;
            _grid_currnet.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(_server);
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            li.PopulateGridLookup(accounts, "name", "account_id");
            li.PopupFilterMode = PopupFilterMode.Contains;
            viewCoverage.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewCoverage.Columns["account_id"], li);


            DataTable products = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductList(_server, true);

            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit pi = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            pi.PopulateGridLookup(products, "name", "id");
            viewCoverage.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewCoverage.Columns["product_id"], pi);

            DataTable users = BatCaveLib.Users.GetRepCodeUserList(_server);
            
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit ui = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            ui.PopupFilterMode = PopupFilterMode.Contains;
            
            
            ui.PopulateGridLookup(users, "name", "user_id", new string[] { "name", "repcode" });
            viewCoverage.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewCoverage.Columns["user_id"], ui);
            
            viewCoverage.SortInfo.AddRange(new DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumnSortInfo[] {
                new DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumnSortInfo(viewCoverage.Columns["account_id"], DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder.Ascending),
                new DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumnSortInfo(viewCoverage.Columns["user_id"], DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder.Ascending)});

            viewCoverage.FocusedRowHandle = 0;
            

        }
        private void btnProcessUpcomingCLOs_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string folder = @"S:\applications\exports\kanerai";
            string subject = "Kanerai Load Complete: @total";
            bool archive = true;
            bool do_mail = true;
            int items = 0;
            Nullable<int> process_id = null;
            try
            {
                foreach (string file in Directory.GetFiles(folder))
                {
                    KaneraiLib.KaneraiHelper r = new KaneraiHelper(_server);
                    r.SetWriter(Console.WriteLine);
                    process_id = r.StartExcel();
                    r.LoadFile(file);
                    items = r.ParseAndLoad().rows;

                    if (archive)
                    {
                        string archive_path = Path.GetDirectoryName(file) + @"\Archive";
                        UtilsLib.FileLib.WaitForFile(file, 30 * 1000);
                        UtilsLib.FileLib.ArchiveFile(archive_path, file, "M.d.yy - H.mmss", true, r.asOf,false,false);
                    }

                    if(do_mail)
                    {
                        subject = subject.Replace("@total", items.ToString());
                        Mail m = new Mail("dbloader@rwbaird.com", CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_SERVER, null, null);
                        m.SendSMTPMail("dfoster@rwbaird.com;dbarrish@rwbaird.com;GJankowski@rwbaird.com;jford@rwbaird.com", null, null, subject, null, null, false, true, "dbloader@rwbaird.com");
                    }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                if (null != process_id)
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.KillProcess(process_id.Value);
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n, "DB Loader", null, true);
            }

            XtraMessageBox.Show("Loaded: " + items, "Great Success");
        }

        private void viewCoverage_ValidateRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.ValidateRowEventArgs e)
        {
            bool any_null = viewCoverage.AnyColumnsNull(e.RowHandle, new string[] { "account_id", "user_id", "product_id" });
            if (any_null)
            {
                e.ErrorText = "All values have to be populated";
                e.Valid = false;
            }
            else
            {
                UpdateCoverage(e.RowHandle, false);
            }

        }

        private void lblCoverage_Validated(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
                
        }

        bool ignore_row_fire = false;
        private void viewCoverage_RowUpdated(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.RowObjectEventArgs e)
        {
            if (ignore_row_fire)
                return;
            int focused = viewCoverage.FocusedRowHandle;
            if(focused >= 0)
                UpdateCoverage(focused, false);
        }

        private void UpdateCoverage(int rowHandle,bool delete)
        {
            int account_id = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<int>(rowHandle, "account_id");
            int product_id = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<int>(rowHandle, "product_id");
            int user_id_single = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<int>(rowHandle, "user_id");

            string repcode = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<string>(rowHandle, "repcode");

            bool to_remove = false;
            object to_remove_obj = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<object>(rowHandle, "to_remove");
            if(DBNull.Value != to_remove_obj)
                to_remove = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<bool>(rowHandle, "to_remove");

            object seth_approved_o = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<object>(rowHandle, "seth_approved");
            bool seth_approved = false;
            if(DBNull.Value != seth_approved_o)
                seth_approved = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<bool>(rowHandle, "seth_approved");
            bool is_update = !viewCoverage.AnyColumnsNull(rowHandle, new string[] { "coverage_id" });

            Nullable<int> coverage_id = null;
            List<int> user_ids = new List<int>();
            if (user_id_single < 0)
            {
                List<int> user_ids_temp = BatCaveLib.Users.GetRepCodeUsersIds<int>(_server, -user_id_single,"user_id");
                repcode = BatCaveLib.Users.GetRepCodeUsersIds<string>(_server, -user_id_single, "repcode").Distinct().ToList().First();
                user_ids.AddRange(user_ids_temp);
            }
            else
            {
                user_ids.Add(user_id_single);
            }
            if (is_update)
                coverage_id = viewCoverage.GetRowValue<int>(rowHandle, "coverage_id");
            foreach (int user_id in user_ids)
            {
                Nullable<int> id = BatCaveLib.Coverage.InsertUpdatePendingCoverage(_server, user_id, account_id,  product_id, coverage_id, delete, to_remove, seth_approved, repcode);

                if (delete == false && null != id)
                {
                    ignore_row_fire = true;
                    viewCoverage.SetRowCellValue(rowHandle, "coverage_id", id);
                    ignore_row_fire = false;
                }
            }
        }

        private void viewCoverage_RowDeleting(object sender, DevExpress.Data.RowDeletingEventArgs e)
        {
            int focused = viewCoverage.FocusedRowHandle;
            UpdateCoverage(focused, true);
        }

        private void viewCoverage_HiddenEditor(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            viewCoverage.UpdateCurrentRow();
            
        }

        private void btnSendToSalesForce_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            _grid_coverage.ShowColumn("action");
            _grid_coverage.HideColumn("seth_approved");
            _grid_coverage.HideColumn("to_remove");
            _grid_coverage.SetActiveFilterStringSafe("[seth_approved] = True");
            string html = _grid_coverage.ExportToHTMLSimple();
            _grid_coverage.HideColumn("salesforce_name");
            _grid_coverage.HideColumn("action");
            _grid_coverage.ShowColumn("seth_approved");
            _grid_coverage.ShowColumn("to_remove");
            _grid_coverage.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(null);
            BatCaveLib.Accounts.SpawnMissingCoverageEmail(_server, html);
        }

        private void btnCreateNewAccount_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string name = txtNewAccount.Text;
            int type = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpAccountTypes.EditValue);
            int new_id = BatCaveLib.Accounts.CreateIfNoExistAccount(_server, true, name, type).Value;
            BatCaveLib.Accounts.ProcessOverrides(_server);
            XtraMessageBox.Show(new_id.ToString(), "Account Created");
            drpAccountTypes.EditValue = null;
            txtNewAccount.EditValue = null;
            Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear(); 
        }

        }

        private void btnUpdateHECMLLD_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string source = @"C:\blp\data";
            string destination = @"C:\temp\LLD";
            string raw = System.IO.File.ReadAllText(@"C:\temp\hecm.txt");
            bool ignore_if_exists = true;
            string[] tickers = raw.Split('\n');
            ETA eta = new ETA(tickers.Length, Console.WriteLine);
            foreach (string ticker in tickers)
            {
                string s = ticker.Trim();
                string full_new = Path.Combine(destination, s.Trim() + ".xlsx");
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                if (File.Exists(full_new) && ignore_if_exists)
                    continue;

                IEnumerable<string> files = System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(source);
                UtilsLib.BBGDDE.GetInstance().Send("<ESC><GO>");
                
                UtilsLib.BBGDDE.GetInstance().Send(s + " <mtge><GO>LLD<GO>");
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(5 * 1000);

                
                UtilsLib.BBGDDE.GetInstance().Send("92<GO>");

                string file = UtilsLib.FileLib.WaitForAnyNewFile(source, 30 * 1000, files);
                Nullable<int> pid = UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.WaitForNewProcess("excel", 20 * 1000);
                if (null != pid)
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.KillProcess(pid.Value);
                else
                {

                }
                UtilsLib.FileLib.WaitForFile(file, 15 * 1000);
                

                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(file))
                {


                    string old_full_path = Path.Combine(source, s.Trim());
                    System.IO.File.Move(file, full_new);
                }
            }
        }

        private void btnCombineHECMLLDFiles_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string source = @"C:\temp\LLD\";
            XLHelper xlh = new XLHelper(null);
            int pid = xlh.CreateNewApp();
            DataTable answer = null;
            string[] files = Directory.GetFiles(source);
            UtilsLib.ETA eta = new UtilsLib.ETA(files.Length, Console.WriteLine);
            bool simple_txt = true;
            foreach (string s in files)
            {

                xlh.OpenSheet(s);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                xlh.ActiveSheet("Worksheet");
                string pool = xlh.GetRange<string>("Worksheet", "A1");
                pool = pool.Replace(" PASSTHRU Mtge", "");
                xlh.DeleteRowRange(1, 1);
                string used_range = xlh.UsedRangeAddressFull("Worksheet");
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, used_range);
                DataTable d = xlt.GetDataTable(true);
                d.Columns.Add("ticker", typeof(string));
                foreach (DataRow row in d.Rows)
                    row["ticker"] = pool;
                if (null == answer)
                    answer = d.Clone();
                foreach (DataRow row in d.Rows)
                    answer.Rows.Add(row.ItemArray);
                xlh.CloseAllSheets(false);
            }
            if (!simple_txt)
            {
                string workbook = xlh.CreateNewWorkbook();
                xlh.WriteRange("A1", answer);
                string final_answer = Path.Combine(source, "Answer.xlsx");
                if (File.Exists(final_answer))
                    File.Delete(final_answer);
                xlh.SaveActiveWorkbookAs(final_answer);
                xlh.CloseAllSheets(false);
            }
            else
            {
                string final_answer = Path.Combine(source, "answer.txt");
                answer.ExportTabDelimited(final_answer);
            }
            xlh.Quit();


        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlAlerts.cs ---
using ItemCheckEventArgs = DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.ItemCheckEventArgs;

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlAlerts : XtraUserControl
    {
        private GridHelper _grid;

        private string _server;

        private Delegates.TabSwitcher _tab_switcher;
        private bool first_load = true;
        BatSignalLib.SignalRClient _bat_signal;

        public ctrlAlerts()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        public void Init(string server, SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _grid = new GridHelper(gridEvents, _server, true,_bat_signal);
        }

        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            
            PopulateSubscriptions();
            PopulateNotificationDestinationBox();
            RefreshAlerts();
            PopulateOutlookCheckbox();
            
            first_load = false;
        }

        public void PopulateOutlookCheckbox()
        {
            if(first_load)
                chkOutlookAlerts.Checked = !BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<bool>(_server, 6, false, true);
        }

        public void SetTabSwitcher(Delegates.TabSwitcher ts)
        {
            _tab_switcher = ts;
        }

        public void RefreshAlerts()
        {
            var start = DateTime.Now.AddDays(-7);
            var alerts = BatCaveLib.Alerts.GetLatest(_server, start);
            var cols = "added_to_cave,alert_type,caption,my_trades,my_matchers,my_offers,who_loaded";
            _grid.SetGrid(alerts, cols);
            
            _grid.SetFormat("added_to_cave", "ddd h:mm tt");
        }


        public void PopulateNotificationDestinationBox()
        {
            string alert_default = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(_server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.ALERT_DEFAULT);
            string default_notification = BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<string>(_server, 5, false);
            if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(default_notification))
            {
                alert_default = default_notification;
            }
            foreach (string s in alert_default.Split('|'))
            {
                chkAlertDestination.Items[s].CheckState = CheckState.Checked;
            }
            
        }
        public void PopulateSubscriptions()
        {
            if (first_load)
            {
                var prefs = BatCaveLib.Alerts.GetSummary(_server);
                var v = BatCaveLib.Alerts.GetAllAlertActiveTypes(_server);
                foreach (var kvp in v)
                {

                    chkPreferences.Items.Add(kvp.Value, kvp.Key, prefs.ContainsKey(kvp.Value) && prefs[kvp.Value] ? CheckState.Checked : CheckState.Unchecked, true);
                }
            }
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        private void checkEdit1_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        private void chkPreferences_ItemCheck(object sender, ItemCheckEventArgs e)
        {
            if (!first_load)
            {
                var colortype_id = Convert.ToInt32(chkPreferences.Items[e.Index].Value);
                var enabled = chkPreferences.Items[e.Index].CheckState == CheckState.Checked ? true : false;

    
                BatCaveLib.Alerts.ToggleAlertPref(_server, colortype_id, null,enabled);
            }
        }

        private void viewAlerts_DoubleClick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (null != _tab_switcher)
            {
                var tab_id = viewAlerts.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("tab_id");
                var respective_id = viewAlerts.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("respective_id");
                if (null != tab_id)
                    _tab_switcher(tab_id.Value, respective_id);
            }
        }

        private void btnRefreshTab_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void ctrlAlerts_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void chkAlertDestination_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void chkAlertDestination_ItemCheck(object sender, ItemCheckEventArgs e)
        {
            if (first_load)
                return;
            


            List<string> checked_items = chkAlertDestination.Items.GetCheckedValues().Select(p => p.ToString()).ToList();

            string item = String.Join("|", checked_items);
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(item))
                item = "none";
            BatCaveLib.Preferences.SetUserPreference(_server, null, 5, item);
        }

        private void chkOutlookAlerts_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (first_load)
                return;
            BatCaveLib.Preferences.SetUserPreference(_server, null, 6, !chkOutlookAlerts.Checked ? "True" : "False");
        }
    }
}
