namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlAxe : EditFormUserControl
    {
        public ctrlAxe()
        {
            
            InitializeComponent();



            first_load = true;
            this.LazyBind(txtOface, "size");
            this.LazyBind(drpAccounts, "account_id");
            this.LazyBind(drpColorGroups, "colorgroup_id");
            this.LazyBind(txtPublic, "public");
            this.LazyBind(txtPrivate, "private");
            this.LazyBind(chkLive, "live");
            
            this.LazyBind(txtTicker, "ticker");
            this.LazyBind(drpProductsNew, "product_id");
            this.LazyBind(txtLevel, "level");
            this.LazyBind(drpTag, "tag");
            this.LazyBind(drpRating, "rating_id");
            this.LazyBind(drpPublishTo, "publish_to");
            this.LazyBind(drpAxeTypes, "axetype_id");

  
            this.LazyBind(drpResults, "result_id");

            this.LazyBind(txtFilter, "filter");
            this.LazyBind(txtSQL, "sql_clause");
            this.LazyBind(chkPublish, "publish");
            txtSQL.EditValueChanged += TxtSQL_EditValueChanged;
            txtFilter.EditValueChanged += TxtFilter_EditValueChanged;
            chkPublish.CheckedChanged += ChkPublish_CheckedChanged;
            
            

            
        }

        private void ChkPublish_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
        }

        public void LazyBind(Control c, string bind_field_from_grid, string bind_val = null)
        {
            this.SetBoundFieldName(c, bind_field_from_grid);
            if (null == bind_val)
                bind_val = "EditValue";
            this.SetBoundPropertyName(c, bind_val);
        }

        bool first_load = true;

        string _server;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server, SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;


            first_load = false;
        }


        public void LockForm()
        {
            btnAddAxe.Visible = false;
        }
         public void Populate()
        {
            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountsForColor(_server);
            drpAccounts.PopulateLookup(accounts, "name", "account_id");

            DataTable color_groups = BatCaveLib.Color.GetMyColorGroups(_server, false);
            drpColorGroups.PopulateLookup(color_groups, new string[] { "name", "who" }, "colorgroup_id", false, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BatCave.COLORGROUP_DROPDOWN_WIDTH);

            List<int> my_axes = BatCaveLib.Permissions.GetInclusiveAxeccessProducts(_server);
            DataTable products = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductTableFromIds(_server, my_axes);

            drpProductsNew.PopulateLookup(products, "name", "id", false);
            drpProductsNew.Properties.Columns.HideAllExcept("name");
            drpProductsNew.Properties.AllowNullInput = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.False;


            DataTable ratings = BatCaveLib.Products.RatingSimple(_server);
            drpRating.PopulateLookup(ratings, "name", "rating_id");
            drpRating.Properties.AllowNullInput = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;

            DataTable status = BatCaveLib.Orders.GetResultStatus(_server);
            drpResults.PopulateLookup(status, "name", "result_id");
            drpResults.Properties.AllowNullInput = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;

            DataTable tags = BatCaveLib.Orders.GetMyUsedOrderTags(_server);
            drpTag.PopulateLookup(tags, "tag", "tag", false);
            drpTag.Properties.ShowDropDown = DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.ShowDropDown.SingleClick;

            DataTable color_groups_with_public = BatCaveLib.Color.GetMyColorGroups(_server,true);
            int? public_colorgroup_id = BatCaveLib.Color.GetPublicColorGroupId(_server);
            
            

            
            drpPublishTo.PopulateLookup(color_groups_with_public, new string[] {"name", "who"}, "colorgroup_id", false, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BatCave.COLORGROUP_DROPDOWN_WIDTH, false);
            if (null == drpPublishTo.EditValue)
                drpPublishTo.EditValue = public_colorgroup_id;


            DataTable axetypes = BatCaveLib.Axe.GetAxeTypes(_server);
            drpAxeTypes.PopulateLookup(axetypes, "type", "axetype_id", false);


            bool can_publish_orders = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(_server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Permission.CAN_PUBLISH_ORDERS);
            drpPublishTo.Enabled = can_publish_orders;
            chkPublish.Enabled = can_publish_orders;

            if (!drpProductsNew.ReadOnly)
            {
                List<int> prod_prefernces = BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreference<int>(_server, 1);
                if (prod_prefernces.Count() > 0)
                {
                    drpProductsNew.EditValue = prod_prefernces[0];
                }

                SetupCustomFields();

                drpAccounts.Properties.AllowNullInput = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            }

        }


        private void chkBuyAxe_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            CheckEdit c = sender as CheckEdit;
            if (c.Checked)
            {
                
            }
            txtTicker.Enabled = !c.Checked;
        }

        private void btnAddAxe_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpProductsNew.EditValue);
            bool supports_filter = BatCaveLib.Axe.SupportsFilter(product_id);
            if (!supports_filter)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Not Supported Product");
                return;
            }
            
            
            Query q = BatCaveLib.Axe.GetQuery(_server, product_id);
            Forms.frmAddAxe f = new Forms.frmAddAxe();
            f.Init(_server, _bat_signal);
            f.SetPopulateSQL(q);
            f.SetFilter(filterAxe.FilterString);
            f.Populate();
            f.SetHelper(product_id);
            f.ShowDialog();
            
            if(f.SaveAndExitPressed)
                filterAxe.FilterCriteria = f.Criteria;
        }

        private bool _can_edit;

        private string _filter;
        private string _sql_clause;


        public void ToggleAddAxeVisible(bool visible)
        {
            btnAddAxe.Visible = visible;
        }
        public void AddFilterString(string filter)
        {
            filterAxe.Visible = !String.IsNullOrEmpty(filter);
            filterAxe.FilterString = filter;
        }

        public void ToggleRatingVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            lblRating.Visible = visible;
            drpRating.Visible = visible;
        }

        private void drpProductsNew_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (first_load)
                return;
            SetupCustomFields();
        }

        private void SetupCustomFields()
        {
            Nullable<int> product_id = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != drpProductsNew.EditValue)
                product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpProductsNew.EditValue);
            if(null != product_id)
                SetupPreferances(product_id);
        }


        public static IAxeSettings GetSettingsBasedOnProduct(Nullable<int> product_id)
        {
            if (product_id == 13)
                return new BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.AxeSettingsCorp();
            if (product_id == 2)
                return new BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.AxeSettingsCDO();
            if (product_id == 5)
                return new BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.AxeSettingsAMBS();
            if (product_id == 8)
                return new BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.AxeSettingsACMBS();
            if (product_id == 3)
                return new BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.AxeSettingsCMBS();
            else
                return new BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.AxeSettingsDefault();
        }
        public void SetupPreferances(int? product_id)
        {

            IAxeSettings ias = GetSettingsBasedOnProduct(product_id);
            drpRating.Visible = ias.SupportsRating;
            lblRating.Visible = ias.SupportsRating;
            
            lblOface.Text = ias.NotionalLabel;
            bool can_publish_orders = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(_server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Permission.CAN_PUBLISH_ORDERS);
            if (can_publish_orders)
            {
                chkPublish.Checked = ias.PublishByDefault;
                if (DBNull.Value == drpPublishTo.EditValue && null != ias.PublishByDefaultGroup)
                {
                    drpPublishTo.EditValue = ias.PublishByDefaultGroup;
                }
            }

            lblTicker.Text = ias.TickerLabel;
            
            lblLevel.Text = ias.LevelLabel;
            LBLtAG.Visible = ias.ShowTag;
            drpTag.Visible = ias.ShowTag;
            txtOface.Properties.Mask.EditMask = ias.OFACE_MASK;
            txtOface.Properties.Mask.MaskType = ias.OFACE_MASK_TYPE;
            btnAddAxe.Visible = ias.SupportsAxeFilter();
            lblAccount.Visible = ias.ShowAccount;
            drpAccounts.Visible = ias.ShowAccount;
            


            

        }

        public void ToggleAxeVisible(bool visible)
        {

        }
        private void filterAxe_ItemClick(object sender, DevExpress.Utils.Frames.LabelInfoItemClickEventArgs e)
        {
            NodeEditableElement element = e.InfoText.Tag as NodeEditableElement;
            if (element == null) return;
            e.InfoText.Tag = null;

        }

        private void filterAxe_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void filterAxe_FilterStringChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            UpdateTxts(filterAxe.FilterCriteria);
        }
        private void UpdateTxts(CriteriaOperator co)
        {
            string filter = null;
            string sql = null;
            if (null != co)
            {
                filter = co.ToString();
                sql = DevExpress.Data.Filtering.CriteriaToWhereClauseHelper.GetMsSqlWhere(co);
            }
            filterAxe.Visible = !String.IsNullOrEmpty(filter);
            if(txtSQL.Text != sql)
                txtSQL.Text = sql;
            if(txtFilter.Text != filter)
                txtFilter.Text = filter;

        }

        private void TxtFilter_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            BaseEdit edit = sender as BaseEdit;
            Binding b = edit.DataBindings["EditValue"];
            if (b != null)
                b.WriteValue();
        }

        private void TxtSQL_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            BaseEdit edit = sender as BaseEdit;
            Binding b = edit.DataBindings["EditValue"];
            if (b != null)
                b.WriteValue();
        }

        private void btnCopyToClipboard_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(txtPublic.Text);
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
    }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlBWICFilter.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlBWICFilter : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlBWICFilter()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        public delegate void UpdateFilterDelegate(DevExpress.Data.Filtering.CriteriaOperator filter);

        private void BWICFilter_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        UpdateFilterDelegate _ufd;
        public void SetFilterUpdate(UpdateFilterDelegate filter)
        {
            _ufd = filter;
        }

        public void SetCheckStyle(CheckStyles cf)
        {
            chkProducts.CheckStyle = cf;
        }

        public int CheckedItemCount
        {
            get { return chkProducts.CheckedItemsCount; }
        }

        public bool AllCheckedItems
        {
            get { return chkProducts.CheckedItemsCount == chkProducts.Items.Count; }
        }

        public int AllItemsCount
        {
            get { return chkProducts.Items.Count; }
        }
        public void NoBorder()
        {
            chkProducts.BorderStyle = BorderStyles.NoBorder;
        }
        public void SetBorder(BorderStyles b)
        {
            chkProducts.BorderStyle = b;
        }

        SortedDictionary<string, string> _products;
        List<string> _preferred_products;
        public void SetPreferred(List<string> products)
        {
            _preferred_products = products;
        }

        public void CheckBox(string server, int product_id)
        {

            string product = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductName(server, product_id);
            if (chkProducts.Items.Contains(product))
            {
                chkProducts.Items[product].CheckState = CheckState.Checked;
            }
        }
        public void PopulateBoxes(SortedDictionary<string,string> products)
        {
            _products = products;
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string,string> kvp in products.ToArray())
            {
                if(!chkProducts.Items.Contains(kvp.Key))
                {
                    bool check_mark = false;
                    if (null != _preferred_products && _preferred_products.Contains(kvp.Key))
                        check_mark = true;
                    chkProducts.Items.Add(kvp.Key, check_mark);
                }
                else
                {
                    List<DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem> to_remove = new List<CheckedListBoxItem>();
                    foreach (DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem cl in chkProducts.Items)
                    {
                        if(!_products.ContainsKey(cl.Value.ToString()))
                        {
                            to_remove.Add(cl);
                        }
                    }
                    foreach (DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem cl in to_remove)
                    {
                        chkProducts.Items.Remove(cl);
                    }

                    

                }
            }

            
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        public void ToggleCheckVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            chkOnlyUpcoming.Visible = visible;
            chkOnlyToday.Visible = visible;
            chkMyBWICs.Visible = visible;
            chkTomorrowPlus.Visible = visible;
        }
        private void chkProducts_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        public void Resize(Nullable<int> width, Nullable<int> height)
        {
            int _width = chkProducts.Width;
            int _height = chkProducts.Height;
            if (null != width)
                _width = width.Value;
            if (null != height)
                _height = height.Value;

            chkProducts.Size = new Size(_width, _height);
        }

        public void ToggleHeaderVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            lblProducts.Visible = visible;
        }
        private void chkProducts_ItemCheck(object sender, DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.ItemCheckEventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }
        public void MultiColumn(bool multi)
        {
            chkProducts.MultiColumn = multi;
        }
        public void ToggleLabelVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            lblProducts.Visible = visible;
        }

        public void UnSelectAll()
        {
            chkProducts.UnSelectAll();
        }
        public void HandleFilterChanged()
        {
            string criteria = BuildFilterString();
            CriteriaOperator o = CriteriaOperator.Parse(criteria);
            if (null != _ufd)
            {
                _ufd(o);
            }

            if (null != _pfa)
                _pfa();
        }

        public delegate void PostFilterAction();
        public PostFilterAction _pfa;

        public void SetPostFilterChangeOperation(PostFilterAction pfa)
        {
            _pfa = pfa;
        }

        private string _fitler_col;
        public void SetGridFilterField(string field)
        {
            _fitler_col = field;
        }

        public List<int> GetSelectedProducts(string server)
        {
            List<int> products = new List<int>();
            foreach (DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem v in chkProducts.Items)
            {
                if (v.CheckState == CheckState.Checked)
                {
                    Nullable<int> product_id = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductsFast(server, v.Value.ToString());
                    if(null != product_id)
                        products.Add(product_id.Value);
                }
            }
            return products;
        }

        private string BuildFilterString()
        {
            List<string> sqls = new List<string>();
            List<string> final = new List<string>();
            
            foreach(DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem v in chkProducts.Items)
            {
                if (v.CheckState == CheckState.Checked)
                {
                    string src_field = _products[v.Value.ToString()];
                    if (null != _fitler_col)
                        src_field = _fitler_col;
                    
                    sqls.Add("Contains ([" + src_field + "], '" + v.Value.ToString() + "')");
                    
                }
            }
            string products_sql = String.Join("','", sqls.ToArray());
            
            if (sqls.Count > 0)
            {
                string product_filter = "(" + String.Join(" OR ", sqls.ToArray()) + ")";
                final.Add(product_filter);
            }
            

            
            if(chkOnlyToday.Checked)
            {
                string today_only = "[today] = True";
                final.Add(today_only);
            }
            if (chkOnlyUpcoming.Checked)
            {
                string  today_only = "[upcoming] = True";
                final.Add(today_only);
            }
            if (chkMyBWICs.Checked)
            {
                string my_bwics = "[my_bwic] = True";
                final.Add(my_bwics);
            }
            if(chkTomorrowPlus.Checked)
            {
                string tomorrow_later = "[future_upcoming] = True";
                final.Add(tomorrow_later);
            }
            string final_final = String.Join(" and ", final.ToArray());
            return final_final;
        }

        private void chkOnlyUpcoming_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        private void chkOnlyToday_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        private void chkMyBWICs_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        private void ctrlTomorrowPlus_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }
    }
}
